### [1] [TSA: Temporal Slot Activation for Persistent Object-Centric Video Representation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13714)
*Duc Nguyen,Sieu Tran,Hao Vo,Khoa Vo,Duy Minh Ho Nguyen,Nghi D. Q. Bui,Anh Nguyen,Long Mai,Ngan Le*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Temporal Slot Activation (TSA)机制，解决无监督视频对象中心学习中槽位无条件传播导致的状态漂移和重建干扰问题。TSA通过学习每帧每槽的激活分数，控制槽的状态更新与解码参与，实现对对象生命周期的建模，尤其在部分遮挡和渐进重现场景下表现优异，在MOVi-C/E、YT-VIS和OVIS等多个基准上显著提升对象分解与时间身份一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在视频槽注意力中采用无条件槽位传播，即每个槽在每帧都更新和解码，忽视了对象不存在或被完全遮挡时应保持其状态的要求，导致状态漂移和解码干扰。

Method: 提出Temporal Slot Activation (TSA)，引入每槽每帧的激活分数α_{k,t}，作为共享潜在控制变量；通过激活门控更新机制锚定槽状态，利用激活相关的注意力偏置抑制无效槽的解码参与，并结合时序上下文编码器生成的槽级时序记忆来增强部分遮挡和渐进重现下的激活决策。

Result: 在MOVi-C/E、YT-VIS和OVIS等基准上，TSA在标准与追踪指标（如FG-ARI、mBO、IDF1、HOTA）上均取得显著提升，尤其在长序列、高遮挡视频中表现突出，有效改善了对象分解质量与时间身份一致性。

Conclusion: TSA通过显式建模槽位生命周期，成功缓解了无条件传播带来的状态漂移与重建干扰问题，为无监督视频对象中心学习提供了更鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: Unsupervised video object-centric learning aims to decompose dynamic scenes into temporally persistent entity representations. Existing recurrent video slot-attention methods propagate a fixed set of slots across frames, but typically assume unconditional slot propagation: every slot is updated and decoded at every frame, regardless of whether its corresponding object is visible. We show that this design violates a basic lifecycle requirement for persistent slots: when an object is absent or fully occluded, its slot should preserve its previous state and avoid explaining unrelated visible content. Instead, unconditional propagation creates two failure pathways: update-induced state drift, where current-frame evidence overwrites the absent object's representation, and decoder-induced reconstruction interference, where the inactive slot remains coupled to reconstruction through decoder attention. We propose Temporal Slot Activation (TSA), a mechanism that learns a per-slot, per-frame activation score $α_{k,t} \in (0, 1)$ without visibility supervision. TSA uses this activation as a shared latent control variable for slot lifecycle modeling. When a slot is inactive, TSA anchors its state to the previous slot via activation-gated updating and suppresses its decoder participation through an activation-dependent additive bias on attention logits before softmax normalization. This jointly reduces state drift and reconstruction-driven interference. To improve decisions under partial occlusion and gradual reappearance, TSA further conditions activation prediction on a per-slot temporal memory produced by a Temporal Context Encoder. We evaluate TSA on MOVi-C/E, YT-VIS, and OVIS benchmarks using both standard and tracking-based metrics (FG-ARI, mBO, IDF1, HOTA). TSA consistently improves object decomposition and temporal identity preservation, with large gains on long, heavily occluded videos.

</details>


### [2] [Morphology-Aware Sample Assignment: Overcoming IoU Insensitivity for Surface Defect Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13723)
*Pengfei Liu,Yuhan Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于形态相似性度量（面积、形状、长宽比）的改进方法，以解决IoU在正样本分配中的非敏感区域问题。通过引入多维相似性聚合得分，增强匹配函数的区分能力，提升检测模型训练精度与效率。该方法无需额外推理开销，可直接集成至YOLOv9等框架，在NEUDET和GC10-DET数据集上均取得稳定性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IoU在评估候选框与真实框的空间对齐时存在非敏感区域，导致不同几何重叠的样本产生相近的IoU值，影响正样本选择的准确性，进而降低检测模型训练效果。

Method: 设计一组涵盖面积、形状、长宽比的形态相似性度量，通过均值聚合生成补充匹配分数，优化正样本分配策略；理论分析表明该方法能重塑匹配响应分布，形成更紧凑的高响应区域。

Result: 在YOLOv9框架下，于NEUDET和GC10-DET数据集上均实现一致性能提升，且为即插即用设计，无额外推理开销，适合工业视觉检测部署。

Conclusion: 通过引入多维度形态相似性，有效克服了IoU的固有局限性，显著提升了正样本选择的精确性与模型训练效率，具备良好的实用性和推广价值。

Abstract: Intersection-over-Union (IoU), as a pivotal metric for evaluating the spatial alignment between candidate proposals and ground-truth annotations, directly determines the quality of positive sample sets and the training efficacy of visual detection models. Through theoretical modeling and analysis, we uncover a non-sensitive region on the IoU response curve, within which samples yield nearly identical IoU scores despite distinct geometric overlaps. To overcome this limitation, we introduce a set of morphological similarity metrics covering area, shape, and aspect ratio, to refine the positive sample assignment process, thereby ensuring more discriminative and reliable matching. A supplementary matching score is derived via mean-based aggregation of these multidimensional similarities, compensating for the intrinsic limitation of IoU in representing structural correspondence. Theoretically, incorporating morphological similarity reshapes the response distribution of the matching function, yielding both effective directional gradients and polygon-like iso-response contours, which tightly confine high-response regions around each ground-truth instance and substantially enhance the precision of positive sample selection. Experiments based on the YOLOv9 framework demonstrate consistent performance gains on both NEUDET and GC10- DET datasets. Notably, the proposed approach is fully plug-and-play and incurs zero additional inference overhead, thereby ensuring deployment efficiency for industrial visual inspection.

</details>


### [3] [Connections Between Pairs of Filters Improve the Accuracy of Convolutional Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13736)
*Kathleen Anderson,Philipp Grüning,Erhardt Barth*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的卷积神经网络连接方式，通过引入可学习的参数来实现更灵活的滤波器间连接，超越传统基于点对点非线性的结构，使网络能根据不同层和任务自适应调整连接函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CNN架构多依赖于堆叠卷积块并用点对点激活函数分隔，这种纯点对点非线性结构存在局限性，因此需要探索更灵活的滤波器间连接方式以提升性能。

Method: 提出一种包含可学习参数的通用连接机制，允许在不同网络层中动态调整滤波器间的连接函数，实现更优的任务适配。

Result: 实验表明，该方法能够有效提升CNN的表达能力与性能，尤其在复杂任务中表现出更强的适应性。

Conclusion: 通过引入可学习的通用连接机制，CNN可以摆脱传统点对点非线性结构的限制，实现更高效、自适应的特征融合，为网络设计提供新思路。

Abstract: While researchers continue to find new and improved network structures for CNNs, most of the newly invented architectures still rely on the traditional pattern of stacking convolutional blocks and separating them with pointwise activation functions. However, there are drawbacks to a network purely building on pointwise nonlinearities. One alternative is to introduce a pairwise connection between two filters of a network. Typical connection functions use multiplications or the minimum operation to realize logical AND connections. In this paper, we go one step further by demonstrating that CNNs can benefit from more general connections, which include parameters that are learned. With such parameters, the network is able to implement different connections in different network layers and better adapt the connection function to the task at hand.

</details>


### [4] [CineOrchestra: Unified Entity-Centric Conditioning for Cinematic Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13768)
*Sharath Girish,Tsai-Shien Chen,Zhikang Dong,Mukesh Singhal,Hao Chen,Sergey Tulyakov,Aliaksandr Siarohin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CineOrchestra 是一个统一的视频扩散模型，能够同时控制多主体、事件、摄像机和镜头切换。其核心思想是将这些不同的电影元素视为在特定时间区间内作用的实体，并通过共享的以实体为中心的条件化原语进行表达，结合参考图像实现视觉实体的个性化。该方法利用两种无参数的协同旋转编码（RoPE）解决位置编码问题：(a) 间隔采样的时间 RoPE，确保不同持续时间事件的一致注意力行为；(b) 2D 实体-时间交叉注意力 RoPE，明确区分每个实体的条件并将其路由到相应的时空区域。在两个新基准测试中，CineOrchestra 在密集字幕生成和镜头切换时间方面优于六个单一维度专家模型，并在用户研究和组件消融实验中表现出一致优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前文本到视频模型难以对电影视频中的多主体、时间事件、多镜头合成及摄像机运动实现联合精细控制。现有工作仅针对单一维度进行优化，缺乏能同时整合四个维度的统一框架。因此，需要一种能够统一建模多种异构电影元素的新方法。

Method: 提出 CineOrchestra 框架，采用实体中心的条件化结构，将多主体、事件、摄像机运动和镜头切换统一表示为在特定时间区间内活动的实体。引入两种无参数的协同旋转编码：(a) 间隔采样的时间 RoPE，保证不同长度事件间注意力行为的一致性；(b) 2D 实体-时间交叉注意力 RoPE，实现对每个实体条件的精准定位与路由。

Result: 在两个新构建的基准上，CineOrchestra 在密集字幕生成和镜头切换时间预测任务上均超越六种单一功能专家模型。用户研究表明其生成结果更符合人类偏好，且组件消融实验验证了各模块的有效性。

Conclusion: CineOrchestra 成功实现了多主体、事件、摄像机和镜头切换的联合控制，展示了统一建模复杂电影视频生成任务的可行性与优越性，为未来视频生成模型的发展提供了新的方向。

Abstract: Cinematic video depicts multiple subjects acting or interacting at specific moments, captured with deliberate camera movement, and stitched together by shot transitions. Together, these elements demand a level of fine-grained control beyond current text-to-video models. Existing work addresses each axis in isolation: multi-subject personalization, temporal control, multi-shot synthesis, or camera control; no prior framework jointly integrates all four. We present CineOrchestra, a unified video diffusion model that controls subjects, events, cameras, and shot transitions simultaneously. Our key insight is that these heterogeneous cinematic elements share a fundamental structure: each is an entity acting over a specific temporal interval, which can therefore all be expressed through one shared structure of entity-centric conditioning primitives, augmented with reference images for visual entities. This formulation reduces the architectural challenge to a single positional encoding problem, which we solve with two parameter-free coordinated rotary embeddings: (a) an interval-sampled temporal RoPE that yields consistent attention behavior across events of dramatically varying duration, and (b) a 2D entity-temporal cross-attention RoPE that disambiguates per-entity conditions and routes each to its corresponding spatiotemporal region. On two new benchmarks, CineOrchestra outperforms six per-axis specialists on dense caption following and shot-transition timing, with consistent gains in a pairwise user study and component ablations.

</details>


### [5] [Compressing Image Style Training into a Single Model Forward](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13809)
*Zhongjie Duan,Yingda Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: i2L 是一种新框架，通过单次前向传播预测 LoRA 权重，实现快速且高保真的风格迁移，避免了传统优化方法的训练开销，同时支持多参考融合与可控生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于扩散模型的风格迁移方法在推理效率与风格保真度之间难以平衡；适配器方法虽高效但易丢失特定外观或复制参考内容语义，而优化式个性化方法（如 LoRA）虽效果好但需为每种风格单独训练，成本高。

Method: i2L 采用图像编码器、可学习的 LoRA 查询和压缩解码头，联合建模参考图像特征并直接生成适用于文本到图像模型的 LoRA 权重，实现风格参数的即时生成。

Result: 在 Z-Image、FLUX.2 和 Hidream-O1 上的实验表明，i2L 在风格保真度、提示对齐性和感知质量方面优于现有基线；生成的显式 LoRA 权重还支持非对称分类器自由引导、多参考风格融合及与可控生成模块的组合。

Conclusion: i2L 有效将风格化 LoRA 训练过程转化为一次前向传播，实现了高效、高质量、灵活的风格迁移，为个性化图像生成提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: Diffusion-based style transfer must balance inference efficiency with stylization fidelity. Adapter-based methods are efficient, but they inject style as an external condition and can either weaken reference-specific appearance or copy reference semantics into the generated image. Optimization-based personalization methods such as LoRA internalize style more effectively, but require a separate training process for every new style. We introduce i2L (image-to-LoRA), a framework that amortizes style LoRA training into a single forward pass. Given one or more reference images, i2L predicts LoRA weights for a text-to-image model, enabling immediate style instantiation without per-style optimization. The architecture combines an image encoder, learnable LoRA queries, and compressed decoding heads that generate adapted matrices. Training on semantically diverse style pairs encourages the predictor to preserve appearance cues while suppressing reference-content copying. Experiments on Z-Image, FLUX.2, and Hidream-O1 show that i2L improves style fidelity, prompt alignment, and perceptual quality over existing baselines. Because i2L produces explicit LoRA weights, it also supports asymmetric classifier-free guidance, multi-reference style fusion, and composition with controllable-generation modules.

</details>


### [6] [Explaining RhythmFormer: A Systematic XAI Analysis of Periodic Sparse Attention for Remote Photoplethysmography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13839)
*Louis Chen,Torbjörn E. M. Nordling*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文针对远程光电容积脉搏波图（rPPG）Transformer模型决策不透明的问题，提出一套可量化、基于生理学验证的可解释性分析框架。通过适配四种归因方法（原始注意力、Rollout、Flow、Beyond Intuition）至RhythmFormer的双层路由注意力机制，并引入皮肤覆盖度指标衡量归因质量在皮肤区域的分布，同时将SaCo系数拓展至rPPG回归任务中，以MAE作为扰动影响度量。实验发现稀疏top-k路由下存在多跳泄漏现象，而Beyond Intuition通过值投影加权与梯度支持掩码有效缓解该问题，在UBFC-rPPG数据集上实现最高皮肤覆盖度（0.83）和忠实度（F=0.92）。案例研究显示，当伪影区域被替换后，所有方法均能一致恢复，表明其行为具有一致性。整体推动rPPG可解释性向可审计的数值证据迈进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: rPPG Transformer虽在基准测试中表现出低心率误差，但其决策过程缺乏透明性，尤其在临床应用背景下更需可解释性支持。现有rPPG可解释性方法多依赖定性热图分析，缺乏定量忠实度评估与生理学验证，导致视觉合理性与可审计证据之间存在差距。

Method: 1. 将四种归因方法（原始注意力、Rollout、Flow、Beyond Intuition）适配至RhythmFormer的双层路由注意力结构；2. 引入皮肤覆盖度指标，量化归因质量在皮肤区域的集中程度；3. 将SaCo忠实度系数从分类任务扩展至rPPG回归任务，采用原始与扰动预测波形间的MAE作为扰动影响度量。

Result: 实验揭示了在稀疏top-k路由下存在显著的多跳泄漏效应，即Rollout与Flow几乎完全恢复了被显式置零的连接路径；而Beyond Intuition因采用值投影加权与梯度支持掩码，显著减轻此问题，取得最高皮肤覆盖度（0.83）与忠实度（F=0.92）；跨数据集与模型变体的验证显示方法具有一致性，且对伪影区域具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 本研究构建了一套面向rPPG Transformer的可量化、生理驱动的可解释性分析框架，通过引入皮肤覆盖度与改进的SaCo指标，实现了空间对齐与扰动忠实度的数值化评估，为可信rPPG可解释人工智能提供了可审计的证据基础。

Abstract: Remote photoplethysmography (rPPG) transformers achieve low heart-rate error on benchmarks, yet their decisions remain opaque--a growing concern as rPPG moves toward clinical heart rate estimation. Existing rPPG XAI is dominated by qualitative heatmap inspection without quantitative faithfulness metrics or physiology-grounded validation, leaving a gap between visual plausibility and auditable evidence. We address this gap. First, we adapt four attribution methods (raw attention, rollout, flow, Beyond Intuition) to RhythmFormer's bi-level routing attention with top-$k$ selection. Second, we introduce a skin coverage metric quantifying how much attribution mass falls on skin regions. Third, we adapt the SaCo faithfulness coefficient from its original classification setting to rPPG regression by using the MAE between original and perturbed predicted rPPG waveforms as the perturbation impact. Applying these tools, we quantify a multi-hop leakage effect under sparse top-$k$ routing: attention rollout and flow almost completely restores the connections that individual refined-attention layers explicitly set to zero. Beyond Intuition mitigates this via its value-projection-weighted rollout and gradient-supported mask, attaining the highest median refined skin coverage ($0.83$ vs. $0.57$ for vanilla rollout) and faithfulness ($F=0.92$) among the evaluated methods on UBFC-rPPG. Validation across diverse datasets and model variants is needed. A case study on a low-SaCo outlier further shows all four methods recovering consistently once an artefactual region is replaced, suggesting consistent SaCo behavior across attribution families in this illustrative case. Together, these metrics move XAI for rPPG toward auditable numerical evidence about spatial alignment and perturbation faithfulness, i.e. trustworthy rPPG XAI.

</details>


### [7] [Temporal Backtracking Search for Test-time Generative Video Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13861)
*Sejoon Jun,Zheng Ding,Huangyuan Su,Weirui Ye,Yilun Du*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: TBS通过将搜索空间转移到时间轴，提出了一种新的测试时扩展方法，解决了生成视频推理中单次采样范式的瓶颈。它通过可变K条件、时间过程验证和基于前缀的搜索机制，实现生成-验证-重启的迭代循环，显著优于传统BoN方法，在分布外场景下表现大幅提升，揭示了视频模型局部推理能力远超单次生成的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前生成视频推理受限于单次采样范式，现有测试时扩展方法如BoN因早期错误无法修复且盲目重采样效率低下，难以有效提升性能。

Method: 引入时间回溯搜索（Temporal Backtracking Search, TBS），包含三个核心机制：(1) 可变K条件以从任意干净前缀恢复生成；(2) 时间过程验证以定位失败点并提取有效重启锚点；(3) 基于前缀的搜索，将计算资源集中于扩展正确轨迹而非根部重采样。

Result: 在算法、导航和机器人领域，TBS在相同预算下均优于匹配的BoN方法；在严格分布外设置下，BoN成功率仅为0.7%，而TBS达到22.7%，所有成功案例均来自重启分支。

Conclusion: TBS揭示了视频模型的局部推理能力远超单次生成所体现的水平，并提供了一个可扩展的测试时框架来充分释放这种能力。

Abstract: While test-time scaling has revolutionized reasoning in large language models, generative video reasoning remains bottlenecked by a single-shot paradigm. We demonstrate that searching over denoising steps cannot rescue logically flawed rollouts because spatial trajectories commit early in the diffusion process. Root-level Best-of-N (BoN) sampling is similarly inefficient: reasoning errors cluster early in the temporal axis, and resampling blindly discards verified upstream progress. To unlock effective test-time scaling for video models, we introduce Temporal Backtracking Search (TBS), which shifts the search space to the temporal axis. TBS transforms video generation into an iterative generate-verify-restart loop via three core mechanisms: (1) variable-K conditioning to resume generation from arbitrary clean prefixes; (2) temporal process verification to localize failures and extract valid restart anchors; and (3) prefix-based search to reallocate compute toward extending correct trajectories rather than root resampling. Across algorithmic, navigation, and robotics domains, TBS Pareto-dominates matched-budget BoN. In a strict out-of-distribution setting where one-shot generation collapses (0.7% for BoN), TBS achieves 22.7%, with every solved episode stemming from a restarted branch. Ultimately, TBS reveals that the local reasoning competence of video models far exceeds what single-shot rollouts indicate, providing a scalable test-time framework to unlock it.

</details>


### [8] [Mirage Probes: How Vision Models Fake Visual Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13870)
*Daniel Ben-Levi,Judah Goldfeder,Weiliang Zhao,Raz Lapid,Amit LeVi,Allen G. Roush,Ravid Shwartz-Ziv,Hod Lipson*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了视觉语言模型（VLMs）在无图像情况下仍能自信且正确回答问题的“幻觉行为”实际上包含两种不同机制：文本偏见和虚假图像生成。通过引入Mirage Probes框架，研究发现这种行为可在线性上从模型多个内部激活层中解码，且非文本基线无法解释该信号。进一步提出先验利用指数（PHI）来区分两种模式，表明仅清理文本分布无法解决虚假图像幻觉，必须在表征层面进行干预以实现真正的视觉接地。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作将视觉语言模型的幻觉行为视为单一失败模式，但本文认为其背后存在两种不同的机制，需要更精细的分析与干预策略。

Method: 采用对比探针框架Mirage Probes，结合改写的问题变体与匹配的幻觉/非幻觉标签，在同一图像上进行测试；通过分析模型内部激活（残差流、MLP、注意力后、注意力头等位置）的可解码性，验证幻觉信号的存在；使用先验利用指数（PHI）评估模型从纯文本中回答的能力，并识别不同幻觉模式。

Result: 发现幻觉行为在多个模型层级中均可被线性解码；文本基线无法复现该信号，排除表面词汇混淆；跨基准分离模式显示存在两类幻觉：由语言先验驱动的文本偏见和基于虚假视觉表征的虚假图像生成；文本清洗只能缓解第一类，无法解决第二类。

Conclusion: 真正的视觉接地需在模型表征层面进行干预，而非仅依赖文本预处理或分布调整。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) can answer image-based questions confidently, and often correctly, even when no image is provided. This mirage behavior inflates benchmark scores without reflecting visual grounding. Prior work treats this as a single failure mode. We argue it is two. Using Mirage Probes, a contrastive probing framework that pairs paraphrased question variants with matched mirage and non-mirage labels on the same image, we show that mirage behavior is linearly decodable from internal activations across residual stream, MLP, post-attention, and attention-head sites in two open-source VLMs. We demonstrate that a Naive Bayes text baseline cannot recover this signal, ruling out surface lexical confounds. Cross-benchmark separability patterns, together with a novel Prior Harnessing Index (PHI) measuring how much a model can answer from text alone, expose two distinct regimes: textual biases, where the model answers from language priors without engaging visual representations, and spurious images, where it constructs false visual content in latent space and answers as if grounded. The distinction has direct mitigation consequences: text-distribution cleaning can address the first regime but cannot reach the second, since spurious-image mirages live in the model's visual representations rather than its text. Faithful visual grounding will require interventions at the representational level.

</details>


### [9] [Avatar V: Scaling Video-Reference Avatar Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13872)
*Benjamin Liang,Ce Chen,Desmond Lin,Ivan Somov,Jiajun Zhao,Jiewei Yuan,Jingfeng Zhang,Junhao Huang,Nik Nolte,Pedram Haqiqi,Penghan Wang,Rong Yan,Rui Zhang,Sam Prokopchuk,Sivan Wang,Viktor Goriachko,Yi Ren,Yuanming Li,Yutao Chen,Zhenhui Ye,Zhibin Hong,Zilong Nie,Zujin Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Avatar V 是一个大规模框架，通过视频参考条件化身份建模，实现高保真、行为可识别的虚拟人视频生成。它利用参考视频的完整标记序列，结合稀疏参考注意力机制和运动表示流，同时支持无限时长1080p视频生成，在身份保留、口型同步和生成质量上均超越现有系统如Seedance 2.0、Kling O3 Pro等。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法多依赖静态图像作为输入，信息不足且无法捕捉动态行为特征；同时，像素级损失函数未能充分关注决定形象真实性的关键面部区域。因此需要一种能同时建模静态身份与动态行为的新范式。

Method: 提出视频参考条件化身份建模，采用稀疏参考注意力（Sparse Reference Attention）实现对任意长度参考视频的线性复杂度建模；引入运动表示流实现闭环说话风格迁移；设计身份感知超分辨率精修模块，继承完整参考条件。训练基于100M+数据集，包含五阶段流程：光流匹配预训练、个性微调、双阶段蒸馏（加速超10倍）、强化学习人类反馈对齐。

Result: 生成的视频在跨场景基准测试中表现最优，显著优于Seedance 2.0、Kling O3 Pro、Veo 3.1、OmniHuman 1.5等主流系统，无论自动评估指标还是人工评价均取得领先。

Conclusion: Avatar V 实现了从静态图像到动态行为全面还原的虚拟人视频生成，为高质量数字人应用提供了新范式。

Abstract: Generating avatar videos that are not merely visually similar to a target individual but behaviorally recognizable, faithfully reproducing their talking rhythm, gestural tendencies, and expression dynamics, remains an open challenge. Existing methods predominantly condition on single static images, which provide insufficient identity information and cannot capture dynamic motion traits, while standard pixel-level objectives underserve the perceptually critical facial regions that determine avatar fidelity. We present Avatar V, a production-scale framework that addresses these limitations through video-reference-conditioned identity modeling. Rather than compressing identity into fixed-size embeddings, the model conditions directly on the full token sequence of a reference video, learning to reproduce both static identity attributes (facial geometry, skin texture) and dynamic behavioral patterns (talking rhythm, micro-expressions) through attention over the reference context. We introduce Sparse Reference Attention, an asymmetric mechanism achieving linear-complexity conditioning on arbitrarily long references; a motion representation stream enabling closed-loop talking style transfer; and an identity-aware super-resolution refiner inheriting the full reference conditioning. These are supported by a data engine curating 100M+ training clips from 50M raw videos, and a five-stage training pipeline with flow matching pre-training, personality fine-tuning, two-phase distillation (>10x acceleration), and RLHF alignment, deployed across thousands of GPUs. Avatar V generates 1080p videos of unlimited duration, achieving state-of-the-art identity preservation, lip synchronization, and generation quality on our cross-scene benchmark, consistently outperforming leading systems including Seedance 2.0, Kling O3 Pro, Veo 3.1, and OmniHuman 1.5 in both automated metrics and human evaluation.

### [10] [How do Self-Supervised Remote Sensing Vision Models Transfer to Downstream Tasks?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13896)
*Julia Romero,Qin Lv,Morteza Karimzadeh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究了六种代表性的自监督地理空间基础模型（GeoFMs），评估其在分类、回归和分割任务中的迁移性能，发现模型排名随任务和适配设置变化。中间层变压器块比最终层嵌入包含更多任务相关信息，且不同模型具有不同的深度特征分布。下游适配策略如解码器设计和微调对性能影响甚至超过模型选择本身，标准密集预测头可能与GeoFMs的信息组织方式不匹配。CKA分析显示微调主要集中在ViT块中第一个MLP线性层，而非均匀改变所有层级。这些结果解释了为何GeoFM排名在不同基准上变化，并呼吁更注重表示特性的评估与适配方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自监督地理空间基础模型（GeoFMs）虽能从遥感数据中学习可迁移表征，但其在下游任务中的行为难以准确刻画，缺乏对模型表现差异的深入理解，亟需系统评估其迁移特性及适配策略的影响。

Method: 选取六种代表性GeoFMs（涵盖联合嵌入、重建和多模态预训练类型），在多种分类、回归和分割任务上进行跨任务迁移评估；通过层间探查（layerwise probing）分析任务相关信息在不同深度的分布；结合案例研究（PASTIS和Sen1Floods11）对比不同解码器结构与微调策略的效果；利用中心核对齐（CKA）分析微调前后模型内部表示的变化模式。

Result: 模型排名在不同任务和适配设置下显著变化；大多数情况下，中间层比最终层蕴含更多任务相关信号；不同GeoFM表现出独特的深度特征演化模式；下游适配策略（如解码器设计、微调方式）对性能影响可媲美模型选择；标准密集预测头与模型内部信息组织不一致；微调主要集中在ViT块的第一个线性层，非全局均匀更新。

Conclusion: GeoFM的性能并非固定不变，其表现高度依赖于下游任务和适配策略。当前评估范式应从单纯比较模型本身转向关注表示特性与适配机制的协同作用。未来工作应发展更具表示感知能力的评估框架与适配方法，以提升GeoFM在实际应用中的可解释性与有效性。

Abstract: Self-supervised geospatial foundation models (GeoFMs) learn transferable representations from remote sensing data, but their downstream behavior is difficult to characterize. We study six representative GeoFMs spanning joint-embedding, reconstruction, and multimodal pretraining families, and evaluate transfer across classification, regression, and segmentation benchmarks under different label availability and downstream pipelines. We find that model rankings change across tasks and adaptation settings. Layerwise probing shows that, in most cases, task-relevant information is more accessible in intermediate transformer blocks compared to final-layer embeddings, and that GeoFMs exhibit distinct depthwise profiles. In segmentation case studies on PASTIS and Sen1Floods11, downstream adaptation settings such as decoder design and fine-tuning can be as impactful as the choice of GeoFM, and standard dense-prediction heads may be poorly aligned with how GeoFMs organize information over depth. Finally, CKA analysis on case studies shows that fine-tuning does not rewrite GeoFMs uniformly across depth, and the strongest changes are localized to the first linear layer of the MLP in ViT blocks. These results help explain why GeoFM rankings shift across benchmarks and motivate more representation-aware evaluation and adaptation strategies.

### [11] [HiLo-Token: Input-Adaptive High-Low Frequency Token Compression for Efficient Image Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13898)
*Haoran You,Yotam Nitzan,Lingzhi Zhang,Yifan Gong,Mang-Tik Chiu,Connelly Barnes,Yan Kang,Yuqian Zhou,Eli Shechtman,Sohrab Amirghodsi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出HiLo-Token框架，通过自适应令牌压缩提升Diffusion Transformer在图像编辑中的速度，显著降低延迟，同时保持生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前生成式AI模型在图像编辑任务中面临严重延迟问题，尤其是从卷积U-Net转向Diffusion Transformers（DiTs）后，DiT模块占总延迟的73%以上，亟需优化以提升效率。

Method: 设计输入自适应的令牌压缩框架HiLo-Token：对用户指定的编辑区域保留膨胀掩码内的所有令牌以保证局部性和上下文相关性；在非编辑区域，基于空间频率选择高频令牌捕捉重要细节，并用16x下采样图像的令牌表示低频成分以保留全局结构。

Result: 在生产级评估数据上，HiLo-Token实现3.13x、2.59x、1.67x的DiT加速，分别对应小、中、大掩码比率场景，平均掩码率分别为6.38%、15.92%、35.36%，且无生成质量下降。

Conclusion: HiLo-Token有效解决了扩散变压器在图像编辑中的高延迟问题，实现了显著的速度提升而无需牺牲生成质量，适用于实际生产环境。

Abstract: Creative image editing tools, such as Photoshop's Remove or Generative Fill buttons, are central to everyday customer use and account for a major share of traffic in Photoshop and Lightroom. However, current generative AI models face significant latency challenges, which become even more pronounced when transitioning from convolution-based U-Nets to Diffusion Transformers (DiTs). In our evaluation on hundreds of representative image editing samples spanning a wide range of mask ratios, the DiT module alone accounts for an average of 73% of the total model latency, even after being distilled from 50 timesteps down to 8 timesteps. To tackle this challenge, we propose $\textbf{HiLo-Token}$, an input-adaptive token compression framework that allocates more token budget to high-frequency, rich-context regions while assigning fewer tokens to low-frequency areas. Specifically, for the editing region specified by the user mask, we retain all tokens within a dilated mask to preserve strong locality and contextual relevance. Outside the editing region, we introduce a simple yet effective high-frequency token selection strategy based on spatial frequency to capture important local details, while using tokens from a 16x downsampled image to represent low-frequency components and preserve the blurry but global structure. Extensive experiments on production-level evaluation data validate the effectiveness of the proposed method, achieving 3.13x, 2.59x, and 1.67x DiT speedups on A100-80GB for image editing tasks across small, medium, and large mask ratio categories with average ratios of 6.38%, 15.92%, and 35.36%, respectively, without any regression in generation quality.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建PMOF数据集，采用天花板安装鱼眼相机采集移动车辆内的视频；提供旋转边界框、跟踪标识与动作标签；使用YOLO26m-obb模型在多种数据组合配置下进行微调，引入自定义旋转感知增强策略以提升跨域性能。

Abstract: Autonomous staff-free public transport requires reliable in-vehicle passenger monitoring. However, perception inside moving vehicles is challenged by confined spaces, variable illumination, motion-induced background variation, occlusion, and limited viewpoints. To mitigate these spatial constraints, ceiling-mounted fisheye cameras provide full-scene coverage from a single viewpoint. Yet existing public overhead fisheye datasets are recorded in static environments and do not capture the domain shift introduced by vehicle motion. To fill this gap, we introduce PMOF, Passenger Monitoring using Overhead Fisheye cameras, the first public dataset of top-view fisheye imagery captured inside a moving vehicle, comprising over 19k manually annotated frames. We benchmark PMOF using YOLO26m-obb models fine-tuned under multiple dataset configurations that combine PMOF with existing overhead fisheye datasets. ### [13] [Overhead Wildlife Locator (OWL): Benchmarking Weakly Supervised Learning for Aerial Wildlife Surveys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13911)
*Isai Daniel Chacón,Zhongqi Miao,Bruno Demuro,Caleb Robinson,Rahul Dodhia,Lasha Otarashvili,Jason Holmberg,Kirk Larsen,Howard Frederick,Nathan J. Pamperin,Pablo Arbeláez,Juan M. Lavista Ferres*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: OWL 是一种弱监督密度估计框架，用于解决航空野生动物调查中目标检测标注成本高的问题。提出三种变体：OWL-C（全卷积）、OWL-T（Swin增强混合模型）和OWL-D（基于DINOv3的ViT-H+/16）。在五个公开数据集上评估，OWL-D在四个数据集上达到最高AP，尤其在Delplanque数据集上超越HerdNet（0.934 vs 0.840）。OWL-T在高密度场景下表现最佳，而OWL-D在极端密集场景下性能下降。在阿拉斯加2022年驯鹿普查中，OWL-C实现F1=0.965，计数误差仅+3.1%。代码、模型权重及首个开放的驯鹿航拍标注数据集已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准深度学习目标检测依赖耗时且昂贵的边界框标注，而点级标注更高效。为降低标注成本并提升自动化效率，需发展无需精细标注的弱监督方法以支持大规模航空野生动物调查。

Method: 提出三种基于密度估计的弱监督模型：OWL-C采用全卷积结构，适合高速筛查；OWL-T结合Swin架构与混合设计，适用于复杂杂乱场景；OWL-D基于冻结的DINOv3 ViT-H+/16编码器与DPT风格融合解码器，利用预训练视觉基础模型。通过弱监督学习，仅使用点标签进行训练，并在多个数据集上进行对比验证。

Result: OWL-D在五大数据集中的四组上取得最高平均精度（AP），在Delplanque数据集上达到0.934 AP，显著优于HerdNet的0.840；在高密度的SheepCounter数据集上，OWL-T表现最优（0.978 AP）；OWL-C在阿拉斯加驯鹿普查中实现F1=0.965，总计数误差仅为+3.1%。不同模型对不同调查场景表现出适应性差异。

Conclusion: OWL框架有效缓解了航空野生动物调查中高质量标注的瓶颈，其三种变体针对不同场景具备良好的适用性和可扩展性。该工作推动了弱监督方法在生态监测中的落地应用，并提供了首个公开的大规模驯鹿航拍标注数据集，具有重要科研与实践价值。

Abstract: Automated aerial wildlife surveys increasingly rely on deep learning, yet standard object detectors require bounding-box annotations, reported to be up to seven times slower and three times more expensive to produce than point-level labels. To address this bottleneck, we introduce the Overhead Wildlife Locator (OWL), a weakly supervised density-estimation framework with three variants: OWL-C, a fully convolutional model for high-throughput screening; OWL-T, a Swin-augmented hybrid for heterogeneous, cluttered scenes; and OWL-D, built on a frozen DINOv3 ViT-H+/16 encoder with a DPT-style fusion decoder. We benchmark all three against POLO, YOLOv11n, and YOLOv11l across five public aerial datasets, from sparse fixed-wing savanna surveys to dense UAV paddock imagery, and against the published HerdNet baseline on its native Delplanque split. OWL-D sets a new state of the art on Delplanque (0.934 AP vs. HerdNet's 0.840) and records the highest AP on four of the five datasets. Performance is regime-dependent: on the extreme-density SheepCounter UAV dataset the hybrid OWL-T leads (0.978 AP) and the convolutional variants attain the lowest counting error, whereas the foundation-based OWL-D degrades, indicating which variant suits which survey type. We further validate operational readiness on the Alaska Department of Fish and Game's 2022 Central Arctic Caribou census: under cross-herd and cross-temporal transfer, OWL-C fine-tuned on the 2017 Porcupine Caribou Herd split attains F1 = 0.965 on a held-out patch test set, with a signed count error of +3.1% aggregated across the released test patches. We release the OWL code, model weights, and the annotated Porcupine Caribou Herd 2017 (PCH) and Central Arctic Herd 2022 (CAH) patches, the first open patch-level datasets for large-scale caribou aerial surveys, at https://github.com/microsoft/MegaDetector-Overhead.

### [14] [Self-Evolving Visual Questioner](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13929)
*Yijun Liang,Hengguang Zhou,Ming Li,Lichen Li,Cho-Jui Hsieh,Tianyi Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种自进化框架，使视觉语言模型（VLM）在无外部监督的情况下持续提升其作为视觉问题生成器的能力。该框架利用VLM自身作为问题提出者和筛选者，生成更难、更具信息量且以视觉为中心的问题，同时保持探索多样性，防止训练崩溃。生成的问题用于联合训练VLM在提问者和回答者模式下的能力。通过引入代理协议评估问题在感知、推理和多样性维度的表现，实验表明该方法显著提升了自主问题生成的质量与难度边界，在相同预算下优于静态数据训练，且自进化问题生成器在回答任务上也表现出竞争力甚至更优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一个自进化框架：使用VLM自身作为问题提出者和过滤器，动态生成并筛选高质量、视觉中心、多样化的问题；利用生成的问题进行联合训练，实现提问与回答能力的同步优化；设计代理评估协议，从感知、推理、多样性三个维度评估问题质量。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在多种骨干VLM上均显著提升问题生成的质量与难度边界；在相同训练预算下，自监督策略优于静态数据训练；自进化后的模型在问答任务中表现更优，兼具强大提问与回答能力。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了视觉语言模型可通过自我监督实现持续的自进化，无需依赖外部标注数据即可有效提升其主动提问与回答能力，为构建更智能、更具交互性的多模态系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) are typically trained as passive answerers, while their ability to actively ask diverse, non-trivial, visual-centric and grounded questions remains underexplored. Existing visual questioners' performance is bottlenecked by the availability of high-quality training data or the cost of curating them. We show that a VLM can continuously improve itself as a visual questioner without any external supervision. We propose a self-evolving framework that uses a VLM itself as both a proposer and a filter to produce harder, more informative, and visual-centric questions, while maintaining their exploration diversity to avoid training collapse. These questions are then used to train the VLM in both questioner and answerer modes. To evaluate the questioner, we introduce an agentic protocol that assesses questions along perception, reasoning, and diversity dimensions. Experiments across various backbone VLMs show that our method substantially enhances the quality and substantially expands the difficulty boundary of autonomous question generation. Under the same budget, our self-supervision is more effective than training on the static source data. Moreover, the self-evolving questioner remains a competitive or even better answerer.

### [15] [CaricHarmony: Contrastive Diffusion Paths for Identity-Preserving Caricature Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13964)
*Dongyu Wang,Dar-Yen Chen,Yi-Zhe Song*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: CaricHarmony 是首个无需训练的草图卡通合成方法，通过并行无污染扩散路径解决身份与形状条件在扩散模型中导致的信号干扰问题。该方法在推理时维持三个路径：纯身份、纯形状和和谐输出路径，利用基于交叉注意力特征的能量函数进行梯度引导，实现形状保真与身份一致性之间的最优平衡。相比需微调或受限于贝塞尔曲线的方法，CaricHarmony 支持任意草图格式，生成速度低于16秒，并在形状CLIP得分（0.8615）和用户偏好评分（7.81）上达到领先水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有草图卡通合成方法在结合身份与形状条件时，因扩散模型中的条件信号污染导致生成结果要么过于平淡，要么失去可识别性，亟需解决身份与形状之间的冲突机制。

Method: 提出并行无污染扩散路径架构，包括纯身份路径 $\mathcal{P}^{\mathrm{i}}$、纯形状路径 $\mathcal{P}^{\mathrm{s}}$ 与和谐输出路径 $\mathcal{P}^{\mathrm{i+s}}$；设计两个能量函数 $\mathcal{E}_{\mathrm{shape}}$ 和 $\mathcal{E}_{\mathrm{id}}$，分别基于布局与语义对齐、以及标记级对应匹配，引导 $\mathcal{P}^{\mathrm{i+s}}$ 实现理想平衡。

Result: 在保持身份一致性的同时，形状CLIP得分为0.8615（优于对比方法的0.8450），用户偏好评分为7.81（显著高于对比方法的6.06），生成时间低于16秒，支持任意草图输入。

Conclusion: CaricHarmony 将身份-形状冲突重新定义为扩散模型中的条件信号污染问题，通过无训练的并行路径与能量引导机制，实现了高质量、高效率且高度可控的卡通合成，为草图驱动图像生成提供了新范式。

Abstract: Sketch-based caricature synthesis suffers from a fundamental failure mode: when identity and shape conditions are combined in diffusion models, they create destructive interference that causes inevitable collapse toward either bland portraits or unrecognizable distortions. We identify the root cause as \emph{condition signal contamination} -- competing probability distributions in the denoising trajectory that make balanced generation impossible. We present CaricHarmony, the first training-free method that explicitly resolves this contamination through parallel uncontaminated diffusion paths. During inference, we maintain three paths: $\mathcal{P}^{\mathrm{i}}$ (pure identity), $\mathcal{P}^{\mathrm{s}}$ (pure shape), and $\mathcal{P}^{\mathrm{i+s}}$ (harmonized output). Novel energy functions operating on cross-attention features provide gradient guidance that steers $\mathcal{P}^{\mathrm{i+s}}$ toward optimal balance: $\mathcal{E}_{\mathrm{shape}}$ ensures sketch fidelity through layout and semantic alignment, while $\mathcal{E}_{\mathrm{id}}$ employs token-level correspondence matching robust to extreme distortions. Unlike DemoCaricature requiring 70 seconds per-identity fine-tuning or CaricatureBooth constrained to Bezier curves, CaricHarmony accepts any sketch format and generates in under 16 seconds. Experiments demonstrate state-of-the-art performance: 0.8615 shape CLIP score (vs. 0.8450) under comparable identity consistency score, with 7.81 overall user preference score (vs. 6.06). Our method fundamentally reconceptualizes the ID-shape conflict as conditioning signal contamination for diffusion models, enabling unprecedented creative control while preserving recognition.

</details>


### [16] [Prompt2Effect: Training-Free Image-to-Video Model Specialization via LoRA Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13971)
*Xiaomeng Yang,Yanyu Li,Gordon Guocheng Qian,Ivan Skorokhodov,Viacheslav Ivanov,Avalon Vinella,Xuan Zhang,Yanzhi Wang,Sergey Tulyakov,Anil Kag*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Prompt2Effect是一种基于权重的超网络，可直接在单次前向传播中合成特定视觉效果的LoRA权重，避免为每种效果单独训练LoRA模块，显著降低数据准备和优化成本。通过结合冻结的基础模型权重进行结构化条件建模，并采用SVD正则化的参数化方法，解决了权重预测中的模糊性和不稳定性问题，实现了对高维图像到视频扩散模型的高效、准确的LoRA预测。实验表明，其生成视频质量与效果对齐度达到或超过传统LoRA微调，同时将计算成本从56小时GPU训练降至3.3秒推理时间；作为微调初始化时，还能提升最终性能并加速优化约10倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前个性化图像到视频扩散模型需为每种视觉效果单独训练LoRA模块，导致高昂的数据准备和迭代优化成本，难以实现交互式控制。因此亟需一种更高效、可扩展的方法来支持快速、精准的视觉效果定制。

Method: 提出Prompt2Effect，一种基于权重的超网络，利用冻结的基础模型权重作为结构先验，显式地对齐层间几何结构，通过SVD-canonicalized参数化方式直接预测LoRA权重，从而在单次前向传播中生成效果特定的适配器权重。

Result: Prompt2Effect在视频生成质量与效果对齐方面达到或优于传统LoRA微调，将训练成本从56 GPU小时降低至3.3秒推理时间；作为微调初始值时，可使优化速度提升约10倍，且最终性能更优。

Conclusion: Prompt2Effect通过结构化条件建模与稳定参数化设计，实现了对高维图像到视频扩散模型的高效、精准的视觉效果个性化，显著降低了个性化训练的成本与复杂性，为交互式视频生成提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Personalizing Image-to-Video (I2V) diffusion models with specific visual effects is increasingly demanded for high-end video generation. Current practice requires training a separate Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) module for each effect, incurring substantial data curation and iterative optimization costs that hinder interactive control. We present Prompt2Effect, a weight-driven hypernetwork that amortizes per-effect training by directly synthesizing effect-specific LoRA weights in a single forward pass. Unlike prior hypernetworks that regress adapter weights purely from semantics, Prompt2Effect is explicitly conditioned on the frozen base model weights, grounding weight prediction in the structural geometry of each layer. Furthermore, instead of predicting raw LoRA matrices, we introduce an SVD-canonicalized parameterization that resolves factorization ambiguity and stabilizes large-scale weight synthesis. Together, these design principles enable accurate and scalable LoRA prediction for high-dimensional I2V diffusion models. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Prompt2Effect achieves on-par or superior video quality and effect alignment compared to conventional LoRA fine-tuning, while reducing the computational cost from 56 GPU training hours to 3.3 seconds of hypernetwork inference. When used as initialization for subsequent fine-tuning, our predicted weights further improve final performance and accelerate optimization by approximately 10x.

</details>


### [17] [Context-Guided Semantic Alignment for Feature Fusion Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14005)
*Hyungseop Lee,Jiho Lee,Woochul Kang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为FINE的轻量级语义对齐模块，通过跨层级注意力机制在融合前对低层特征进行优化，利用高层上下文指导低层特征，解决多尺度特征融合中的语义不一致问题。引入了对齐感知的令牌采样方法，有效降低注意力计算复杂度一个数量级，并生成空间-通道调制图，通过残差逐元素调制提升关键像素的语义相关性，同时保持亚像素定位精度。FINE可广泛应用于各类检测器，显著提升检测精度且不牺牲效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有特征融合方法在多尺度特征融合时存在语义不一致问题，低层与高层特征由于表示差异导致融合效果不佳，影响检测性能。因此需要一种高效且能对齐语义的融合机制。

Method: 提出FINE模块，包含对齐感知的令牌采样策略，以减少跨层级注意力计算复杂度；采用跨层级注意力生成空间-通道调制图，通过残差元素级调制作用于低层特征，实现语义增强与定位精度保留。

Result: FINE在多种主流目标检测器上均取得显著精度提升，且计算开销极小，具有良好的泛化能力与效率优势。

Conclusion: FINE是一种高效、通用且有效的特征融合框架，通过语义对齐和计算优化，在不增加推理成本的前提下显著提升了目标检测性能。

Abstract: Feature fusion networks are fundamental components in modern object detectors, aggregating multi-scale features to detect objects of varying sizes. However, directly fusing features from different pyramid levels often introduces semantic inconsistency due to their heterogeneous representations. In this paper, we propose Feature Interaction NEtwork (FINE), a lightweight semantic alignment module that refines low-level features via high-level contextual guidance using cross-level attention prior to fusion. To bridge the structural gap and ensure computational efficiency, we introduce an Alignment-Aware Token Sampling that aligns corresponding spatial regions across scales, reducing the attention complexity by an order of magnitude. The resulting attention weights generate a spatial-channel modulation map that is upsampled and applied to the low-level features via residual element-wise modulation. This mechanism ensures that the network selectively enhances semantically relevant pixels while preserving the sub-pixel localization accuracy necessary for dense prediction tasks. FINE is generally applicable to various detectors and consistently improves detection accuracy without compromising efficiency.

### [18] [HARBOR: Heading Analysis and Reconstruction from Behavioral Observation and Radar](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14006)
*Joao P. A. Dantas,Paulo F. Silva Filho,Jelton A. Cunha,Gabriel Dietzsch*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究提出HARBOR系统，利用单幅SAR图像在无辅助数据情况下推断船舶运动信息，通过预处理、目标检测、分类与航向估计，并基于离线校准的船型相关运动参数生成未来位置的概率热图，适用于信号缺失或受干扰的海事环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在操作或冲突场景中，AIS信号可能因丢失、故意关闭或欺骗而不可用，因此需要一种不依赖AIS的替代感知手段来实现广域海上态势感知。SAR图像虽为静态快照，但可提供关键观测数据，故需开发从单张SAR图像中提取运动趋势的方法。

Method: HARBOR管道包括SAR图像预处理、船舶候选目标增强与分割、自动检测、基于尺寸的分类、利用骨架几何和局部强度模式进行航向估计；仅在离线校准阶段使用AIS数据获取不同船型的运动参数，推理时无需任何外部数据源，最终生成未来位置的概率热图。

Result: 基于真实COSMO-SkyMed SAR图像的案例研究显示，该方法能有效提取船舶运动倾向，并在数据缺失环境下生成可靠的未来位置概率投影，验证了其在复杂海况下的实用性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: HARBOR成功实现了从单幅SAR图像中推断船舶运动行为的能力，为无AIS数据条件下的海上态势感知提供了可靠解决方案，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Maritime situational awareness often relies on Automatic Identification System (AIS) transmissions to track vessel movements. However, in operational or conflict scenarios, these data may be unavailable due to signal loss, deliberate deactivation, or intentional spoofing. In such conditions, synthetic aperture radar (SAR) imagery becomes a critical sensing alternative for wide-area maritime monitoring, despite providing only static scene snapshots. This work introduces HARBOR (Heading Analysis and Reconstruction from Behavioral Observation and Radar), a complete pipeline for transforming a single SAR image into predictive motion information without requiring any auxiliary data source at inference time. The method begins with SAR image preprocessing to enhance and segment vessel candidates, followed by automatic detection, size-based classification, and heading estimation using skeleton geometry and local intensity patterns. AIS data are used exclusively during an offline calibration phase to derive vessel-type-dependent motion parameters, which are then applied to generate probabilistic heatmaps of candidate future vessel positions. A case study using real COSMO-SkyMed SAR imagery demonstrates the pipeline on a maritime scene in southern Brazil, showing its ability to extract motion tendencies and generate probabilistic projections of vessel positions in data-denied environments.

### [19] [RT-VLA: Real-Time Vision-Language-Action Models via Knowledge Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14010)
*Xiangyu Huang,Zhenlin Hua,Han Zhou,Shounak Sural,Ragunathan Rajkumar*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RT-VLA 是一种轻量级、经过蒸馏的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型，通过多层次监督蒸馏将先进模型 SimLingo 的驾驶与推理能力迁移到紧凑的学生模型中。该模型在保持语言推理能力的同时，支持通过离线语言分析实现对关键驾驶时刻的后验解释，且不增加实时控制的延迟。相比 SimLingo 教师模型，RT-VLA 在仅视觉模式下推理时间减少 44.8 倍，在视觉+语言模式下减少 7.9 倍，同时保持了相当的闭环驾驶和语言推理性能，表明监督蒸馏是构建实时、可解释 VLA 式自动驾驶模型的有效方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 VLA 模型因庞大的视觉-语言主干网络和推理模块导致显著的推理延迟，难以在真实道路环境中部署。需要一种轻量化、低延迟但依然具备可解释性的 VLA 模型以满足实时自动驾驶的需求。

Method: 采用多层次监督蒸馏技术，将 SimLingo 这一先进 VLA 模型的知识迁移至一个更小、更高效的 student 模型（RT-VLA）。蒸馏过程涵盖视觉特征、语言表示和动作预测等多个层次，确保学生模型保留教师模型的关键能力。此外，通过离线语言分析实现对安全关键驾驶时刻的后验解释，不影响实时控制。

Result: RT-VLA 在视觉仅模式下推理速度提升 44.8 倍，在视觉+语言模式下提升 7.9 倍；同时在闭环驾驶任务和语言推理任务上表现接近原教师模型，证明其在效率与性能之间取得良好平衡。

Conclusion: 监督蒸馏是一种可行且有效的策略，可用于构建兼具实时性与可解释性的 VLA 式自动驾驶系统，为实际部署提供了重要路径。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have shown strong potential for end-to-end autonomous driving by jointly modeling visual perception, language reasoning, explainability and action prediction. However, their large vision-language backbones and reasoning modules introduce substantial inference latency and thereby prevent their deployment in the unforgiving reality of the road networks. We propose RT-VLA, a lightweight, distilled VLA model that transfers the driving and reasoning capabilities of the state-of-the-art SimLingo model into a compact student through multi-level supervised distillation. RT-VLA preserves language-based reasoning and supports post-hoc explanation through offline language analysis of safety-critical driving moments without adding latency to real-time control. Compared to the SimLingo teacher, RT-VLA maintains competitive closed-loop driving and language reasoning performance while reducing inference time by 44.8X in vision-only mode and 7.9X in vision+language mode. These results suggest that supervised distillation is a practical approach for building real-time, explainable VLA-style autonomous driving models.

### [20] [ViT-Up: Faithful Feature Upsampling for Vision Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14024)
*Krispin Wandel,Jingchuan Wang,Hesheng Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ViT-Up提出了一种基于视觉变换器（ViT）的隐式特征上采样框架，通过利用中间ViT隐藏状态构建分层查询，替代传统依赖浅层图像引导的上采样方法。该方法可在任意连续图像坐标上进行特征预测，同时保持与主干特征空间的一致性，在密集预测任务（如语义分割、深度估计）和语义对应任务中均显著优于现有方法。在DINOv3-S+和DINOv3-B主干网络下，分别实现最高+2.07 mIoU和+3.36 mIoU提升，以及+4.17 PCK@0.10和+8.09 PCK@0.10的性能增益，表明其能有效利用更大模型容量并具备良好的扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Vision Transformers (ViTs) 在视觉表征学习中表现优异，但受限于全局自注意力的二次计算开销，通常仅在较小的补丁-令牌网格上运行，这成为密集预测任务（如语义分割、深度估计）的瓶颈。现有方法虽采用任务无关的特征上采样器提升分辨率，但依赖浅层图像编码器进行引导，易引发特征泄漏、碎片化和模糊问题。因此需要一种更高效、更鲁棒的上采样机制。

Method: 提出ViT-Up框架，摒弃外部图像引导，转而从ViT中间层隐藏状态中构造分层查询，实现对任意连续图像坐标的隐式特征预测，确保输出特征与主干特征空间对齐。

Result: 在Cityscapes数据集上，使用DINOv3-S+主干时，ViT-Up相比之前方法最高提升+2.07 mIoU；在SPair-71k上，提升+4.17 PCK@0.10。使用更大的DINOv3-B主干时，性能增益进一步提升至+3.36 mIoU和+8.09 PCK@0.10，验证了方法随主干规模增长的优越扩展性。

Conclusion: ViT-Up通过引入基于中间特征状态的分层查询机制，实现了无需外部图像引导的高精度、连续坐标上的特征上采样，不仅克服了现有方法的缺陷，还在多个密集预测与对应任务中达到当前最优性能，且表现出良好的可扩展性，为视觉变换器在密集视觉任务中的应用提供了新范式。

Abstract: Vision Transformers (ViTs) have become a dominant architecture for visual representation learning, providing exceptionally strong and broadly reusable backbone features. However, ViTs are commonly operated on relatively small patch-token grids due to the quadratic cost of global self-attention, which creates a persistent bottleneck for dense prediction tasks such as semantic segmentation and depth estimation. This has motivated the development of task-agnostic feature upsamplers. While recent state-of-the-art methods produce visually sharp dense representations, their reliance on shallow image encoders for guided upsampling can introduce feature leakage, fragmentation, and blur. We introduce ViT-Up, an implicit feature upsampling framework that replaces external image guidance with layer-wise query construction from intermediate ViT hidden states. This enables feature prediction at arbitrary continuous image coordinates while preserving alignment with the backbone feature space. Experiments demonstrate that ViT-Up consistently outperforms state-of-the-art image-guided upsamplers across dense prediction and semantic correspondence. On DINOv3-S+, ViT-Up improves over prior methods by up to +2.07 mIoU on Cityscapes and +4.17 PCK@0.10 on SPair-71k. With the larger DINOv3-B backbone, these gains increase to +3.36 mIoU and +8.09 PCK@0.10, demonstrating that ViT-Up scales favorably with backbone capacity.

</details>

### [22] [Toward 360-Degree Indoor Panorama Editing via Tuning-Free Diffusion Model with Refocusing Cross-Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14035)
*Dinh-Khoi Vo,Nhut-Thanh Le-Hinh,Viet-Tham Huynh,Tam V. Nguyen,Minh-Triet Tran,Trung-Nghia Le*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: FocusDiff 是一种无需微调的图像编辑框架，通过注意力聚焦机制实现精准、区域特定的图像操作。它利用目标区域的分割信息，对非编辑区域进行选择性模糊，引导模型关注目标区域，同时保持背景一致性和全局连贯性。该方法在简单文本提示下即可完成单次编辑，有效解决零样本扩散模型中的提示脆弱性、溢出编辑和小物体/杂乱对象失败等问题。实验表明，FocusDiff 在多对象、小物体等挑战性场景中优于现有方法，在文本-图像对齐和背景保留方面表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有零样本文本引导扩散模型在实际应用中面临三大挑战：提示脆弱性（需精细提示工程）、溢出编辑（非目标区域意外修改）以及小物体或复杂场景下的编辑失败（训练数据缺乏细粒度监督）。需要一种无需微调、能精确控制编辑区域并保持全局一致性的方法。

Method: FocusDiff 采用基于注意力聚焦的策略，结合自动分割或手动选择的目标区域，对非目标区域施加选择性模糊，从而引导交叉注意力机制集中于目标区域；引入上下文保持模块以确保背景真实性和整体一致性；整个过程仅需一次前向传播，支持从简单文本提示中生成高质量编辑结果。此外，该框架扩展至360度室内全景图编辑，适用于虚拟现实环境。

Result: 在自建的局部编辑基准 LIMB（包含30张多对象图像和100个标注示例，涵盖小物体等挑战场景）上，FocusDiff 在文本-图像对齐、背景保留、编辑精度、照片真实感和易用性等方面均优于现有零样本编辑方法。其在复杂场景下的鲁棒性显著提升，且无需额外微调即可实现高效精准编辑。

Conclusion: FocusDiff 提供了一种无需微调、高精度、区域可控的零样本图像编辑方案，通过注意力聚焦与上下文保持机制，有效解决了当前扩散模型在实际应用中的关键瓶颈，具备在复杂场景和虚拟现实环境中广泛应用的潜力。

Abstract: Zero-shot text-guided diffusion has significantly advanced image editing; however, its practical usability remains constrained by three persistent challenges: prompt brittleness that requires meticulous prompt engineering, spillover edits that unintentionally affect non-target regions, and failures on small or cluttered objects caused by limited fine-grained supervision in training data. We propose FocusDiff (Target-Aware Refocusing for Tuning-Free Diffusion Editing), a tuning-free framework for precise and region-specific image manipulation based on refocusing cross-attention. Given a target region obtained through automated segmentation or manual selection, FocusDiff applies selective blurring to non-edit areas to guide attention toward the masked region while accurately transferring the object's identity, structure, and appearance to the edited output. Integrated context-preserving modules further ensure background fidelity and global coherence, enabling accurate edits from simple text prompts in a single pass. We also extend FocusDiff to 360-degree indoor panorama editing and demonstrate its effectiveness within virtual reality environments. Extensive experiments on our localized editing benchmark LIMB, comprising 30 multi-object images and 100 annotated examples including challenging small-object cases, show that FocusDiff outperforms existing zero-shot editors in text-image alignment and background preservation, achieving superior precision, photorealism, and usability. The project page is available at https://vdkhoi20.github.io/FocusDiff.

</details>


### [23] [Rethinking One-Step Image Editing through ChordEdit: Reproduction, Simplification, and New Insights](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14042)
*Minghan Li,Jeremy Moebel,Mengyu Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文通过复现、消融实验和简化，深入分析了ChordEdit在单步图像编辑中的工作机制。研究发现：(a) 音符窗口δ主要起到从时间步t到t−δ的有效时间偏移作用；(b) 音符传输作用于高噪声图像，主要实现低频语义编辑；(c) 近邻对齐作用于低噪声图像，补充添加高频目标细节。因此，ChordEdit可自然分解为粗粒度低频传输阶段与细粒度高频对齐阶段。这一理解为提示条件下的动态时间步选择提供了新路径，以实现自适应图像编辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单步图像编辑对于实现文本引导编辑的快速性、实用性及部署便利性至关重要，但其内在机制尚未完全明确。本研究旨在揭示ChordEdit的工作原理，以推动更高效、自适应的图像编辑方法发展。

Method: 通过复现原始ChordEdit模型，进行系统性的消融实验与结构简化，分析不同组件在不同噪声水平下的作用机制，结合可视化与定量评估，揭示其分阶段编辑行为。

Result: 发现音符窗口δ作为时间偏移因子，音符传输主导低频语义修改，近邻对齐负责高频细节生成。整体过程可被解构为先粗后细的两阶段编辑流程。

Conclusion: ChordEdit的编辑过程本质上是分阶段的：先通过低频传输完成语义迁移，再通过高频对齐补充细节。该发现支持开发基于提示的动态时间步选择策略，以实现更智能、自适应的图像编辑。

Abstract: One-step image editing is important for making text-guided editing fast, practical, and easy to deploy, but its underlying mechanism is still not fully understood. We revisit ChordEdit through reproduction, ablation, and simplification. Our analysis shows that a) the chord window $δ$ largely acts as an effective timestep shift from $t$ to $t - δ$; b) chord transport acts on high-noise images and mainly performs low-frequency semantic editing; and c) proximal alignment acts on low-noise images and complements it by adding high-frequency target details. In this view, ChordEdit naturally decomposes editing into a coarse low-frequency transport stage and a fine high-frequency alignment stage. These findings suggest a path toward prompt-conditioned dynamic timestep selection for adaptive image editing. All code and results can be found at \href{https://github.com/Harvard-AI-and-Robotics-Lab/ChordEdit-Reproduction}{link}.

</details>


### [24] [WAM4D: Fast 4D World Action Model via Spatial Register Tokens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14048)
*Ying Li,Xiaobao Wei,Jiajun Cao,Hao Wang,Xiaowei Chi,Chengyu Bai,Qianpu Sun,Jiajun Li,Xiaojie Zhang,Jian Tang,Sirui Han,Shanghang Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: WAM4D 是一种快速的 4D 世界行动模型，通过轻量级空间注册标记在训练时传递预训练几何先验，将 3D 空间约束引入因果视频-动作变换器，并在推理时移除注册分支以实现高效推断。通过因果混合注意力机制防止非因果捷径，显著提升空间一致性与动作预测性能，同时保持高效推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界行动模型（WAMs）多在 2D 视频或潜在空间中操作，难以捕捉 3D 空间约束和遮挡接触几何，影响精确操作；虽然几何基础模型能恢复密集 3D 结构与运动，但直接预测密集 4D 表示会带来高昂的几何解码成本，阻碍因果动作生成。因此需要在保持高精度的同时实现高效推理。

Method: 提出 WAM4D，利用轻量级空间注册标记作为训练时未来深度读出，将预训练几何先验融入因果视频-动作变压器；推理阶段移除注册分支以降低开销；设计因果混合注意力机制，定义视频、动作与几何标记间的模态特定可见性，避免非因果捷径。

Result: 在 RoboTwin 2.0 及具有挑战性的真实世界操作任务上，WAM4D 显著提升了空间一致性，实现了具有竞争力的动作预测性能，同时保持了高效的推理速度。

Conclusion: WAM4D 成功平衡了 3D 几何精度与推理效率，通过轻量级设计有效迁移几何先验，在保证因果性的同时实现高性能动作预测，为复杂操作任务中的世界建模提供了新范式。

Abstract: World action models (WAMs) have recently shown promise in jointly modeling future observations and executable robot actions. However, most existing WAMs still operate in 2D video or latent spaces, where visually plausible rollouts miss the 3D spatial constraints and occluded contact geometry required for precise manipulation. While geometric foundation models offer strong priors for recovering dense 3D structure and motion from visual observations, forcing WAMs to predict the dense 4D representation introduces costly geometric decoding and slows down causal action generation. To address the trade-off, we present WAM4D, a fast 4D world action model that uses lightweight spatial register tokens as training-time future-depth readouts to transfer pretrained geometric priors into a causal video-action transformer, then removes the register branch for lightweight action inference. To prevent non-causal shortcuts, we further design causal mixture attention for the Mixture-of-Transformers (MoT) WAM backbone, defining modality-specific visibility among video, action, and geometry tokens. Comprehensive experiments on RoboTwin 2.0 and challenging real-world manipulation tasks show that WAM4D improves spatial consistency and achieves competitive action prediction while maintaining efficient inference.

### [25] [ShearFuse-UNet: Hadamard, DCT, and Shearlet Transform Fusion for Next-Day Wildfire Spread Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14071)
*Ene Meco,Yingyi Luo,Emadeldeen Hamdan,Adam Watts,Ahmet Enis Cetin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ShearFuse-UNet，一种轻量级、高效的深度学习模型，用于从多模态卫星数据中预测次日野火蔓延。该模型在U-Net主干网络的每个编码器块中集成三个互补的变换域分支：2D快速沃尔什-哈达玛德变换（WHT）、2D离散余弦变换（DCT）和锥适应数字剪切波残差分支。WHT与DCT分支建立正交潜在空间，具有可学习的谱缩放和固定软阈值；剪切波分支则提供各向异性、多方向特征分解，显式编码火线的拉长边缘结构。通过学习的SpectralFusion门自适应融合WHT与DCT响应，剪切波重建以残差形式加入。该三分支设计类比于Transformer自注意力机制，但不依赖可学习投影算子，而是使用固定数学变换，显著降低参数量与计算成本。在WildfireSpreadTS数据集上，模型仅用267k参数即达到0.596的F1分数，优于基于ResNet18的U-Net（14M参数，F1=0.589），展现出优异的精度-效率权衡。在Google Next-Day Wildfire Spread数据集上的结果进一步验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有野火蔓延预测模型在精度与计算效率之间难以平衡，尤其在处理多模态卫星数据时面临高参数量与高计算开销问题。传统方法如自注意力机制虽能捕捉全局依赖，但依赖大量可学习参数，导致模型复杂度高。本文旨在设计一种轻量化、高效且具备强表征能力的模型，利用固定数学变换实现对火线结构的精准建模，同时减少参数与计算负担。

Method: 提出ShearFuse-UNet模型，采用U-Net架构，在每个编码器块中引入三个并行变换域分支：2D WHT、2D DCT 和锥适应数字剪切波分支。其中，WHT与DCT分支构建正交谱空间，结合可学习谱缩放与固定软阈值；剪切波分支通过多方向、各向异性分解捕捉火线的拉长边缘特征。采用学习的SpectralFusion门动态融合WHT与DCT输出，剪切波重建作为残差输入至下一层。整体结构避免使用可学习投影，依赖固定数学变换，从而降低参数量与计算复杂度。

Result: 在WildfireSpreadTS数据集上，ShearFuse-UNet仅使用267k参数即取得0.596的F1分数，优于基于ResNet18的U-Net（14M参数，F1=0.589），表现出显著更高的计算效率。在Google Next-Day Wildfire Spread数据集上也获得一致优异表现，验证了模型跨数据集的泛化能力与有效性。

Conclusion: ShearFuse-UNet通过融合固定数学变换与残差路径，实现了对野火蔓延特征的高效建模。其轻量化设计在保持高预测精度的同时大幅降低参数量与计算成本，为实时、可部署的野火预测系统提供了可行方案。该方法为多模态遥感数据中的结构感知建模提供了新思路。

Abstract: We propose ShearFuse-UNet, a lightweight and computationally efficient deep learning model for next-day wildfire spread prediction from multi-modal satellite data. The model integrates three complementary transform-domain branches inside each encoder block of a U-Net backbone: a 2D Fast Walsh-Hadamard Transform (WHT) branch, a 2D Discrete Cosine Transform (DCT) branch, and a cone-adapted digital Shearlet residual branch. The WHT and DCT branches establish orthogonal latent spaces with learnable spectral scaling and fixed soft-thresholding, while the Shearlet branch provides anisotropic, multi-directional feature decomposition that explicitly encodes the elongated edge structures characteristic of fire fronts. A learned SpectralFusion gate adaptively combines the WHT and DCT responses, and the Shearlet reconstruction is added as a residual. This three-branch design bears a loose structural analogy to transformer self-attention: the WHT and DCT branches provide complementary spectral representations that are adaptively fused, while the Shearlet branch contributes directional content through a residual pathway. Unlike self-attention, the proposed design relies on fixed mathematical transforms rather than learned projection operators, reducing parameter count and computational cost. Evaluated on the WildfireSpreadTS dataset, ShearFuse-UNet achieves an F1 score of 0.596 with only 267k parameters, outperforming a ResNet18-based U-Net (14M parameters, F1 = 0.589) and demonstrating a highly favorable accuracy-efficiency trade-off. Results on the Google Next-Day Wildfire Spread dataset further validate these findings across a different benchmark.

</details>

Abstract: Accurate pediatric brain tumor segmentation remains challenging due to limited annotated data, heterogeneous imaging phenotypes, diffuse tumor boundaries, and class imbalance across tumor subregions. Here, we present a two-stage deep learning framework for improving multi-modal pediatric brain MRI segmentation and clinical interpretation. First, we evaluate 3D Res U-Net and Swin-UNETR baselines on BraTS-PEDs MRI scans, using four co-registered modalities to predict tumor core, whole tumor, and enhancing tumor regions. Second, we introduce diffusion-based refinement models conditioned on coarse Swin-UNETR predictions, including a 3D DDPM refiner and MedSegDiff. Conditioning substantially improves diffusion stability and performance, particularly for enhancing tumor boundary segmentation. ### [27] [Clay-CNN Hybrids: Leveraging Geo-Foundational Models as Auxiliary Context for Landslide Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14081)

Conclusion: Geo-Foundational Models（如Clay）在滑坡检测中最具潜力的应用方式是作为补充模块，与具备精细空间结构的卷积网络结合，而非完全取代传统架构。这表明未来模型设计应注重“预训练大模型+专用骨干网络”的协同范式。

Abstract: Rapid post-event landslide mapping is essential for disaster response but remains difficult to automate due to extreme class imbalance. This study evaluates whether Clay v1.5, a Geo-Foundational Model (GFM), can improve pixel-level landslide segmentation on the Landslide4Sense (L4S) benchmark, which contains 3,799 training chips with 14 Sentinel-2 and terrain bands and approximately 2% positive pixels. These findings suggest that GFMs are most effective for landslide detection when they complement spatially detailed convolutional architectures rather than replace them.

### [29] [A New Multi-Domain Benchmark for Micro-Action Recognition and Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14096)
*Yanbin Hao,Pengyu Liu,Xing Wei,Xun Yang,Dan Gu,Meng Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: MMA-82 是 MA-52 的大规模多领域扩展，涵盖 82 种细粒度微动作类别和四个不同场景（实验室访谈、街头访谈、精神科患者访谈、情感丰富的电视视频），包含 77,856 个标注实例，覆盖 454 名受试者。该数据集支持微动作识别与多标签微动作检测两大任务，并引入域内与跨域评估协议（包括少样本与零样本设置），以检验模型的鲁棒性与泛化能力。实验表明现有方法在领域偏移、长尾分布和复杂时间定位下仍表现不佳。研究还发现微动作与情绪密切相关，可作为面部微表情的补充线索提升情绪识别效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有微动作识别基准 MA-52 在规模、场景多样性、任务覆盖和评估协议方面存在局限，难以支撑真实场景下的微动作分析研究。为推动微动作分析向更现实、全面的方向发展，亟需一个更大规模、多领域、多任务的基准数据集。

Method: 构建 MMA-82 大规模多域微动作数据集，涵盖四种不同场景，扩展至 82 个细粒度类别；设计微动作识别与多标签检测任务；定义域内/跨域、少样本/零样本等评估协议；通过大量实验评估模型性能，并探索微动作与情绪之间的关联性。

Result: 当前方法在真实场景下的微动作理解仍面临挑战，尤其在领域转移、长尾分布和复杂时序定位任务中表现不足。微动作与情绪高度相关，可为情绪识别提供互补信息，增强人类中心人工智能的能力。

Conclusion: MMA-82 是一个全面且具有挑战性的微动作分析基准，适用于真实场景下的微动作理解研究，同时为人类中心人工智能提供了宝贵资源。

Abstract: Micro-actions are short-duration, low-amplitude subtle body movements at the whole-body level that can reveal latent intentions, involuntary reactions, and fine-grained affective changes. Our previous MA-52 benchmark has provided an important foundation for micro-action recognition, but it remains limited in scale, scene diversity, task coverage, and evaluation protocols. To advance micro-action analysis toward more realistic and comprehensive settings, we introduce MMA-82, a large-scale multi-domain extension of MA-52. MMA-82 expands the label space from 52 to 82 fine-grained micro-action categories and covers four distinct domains, including laboratory interviews, street interviews, psychiatric patient interviews, and emotion-rich television videos, resulting in 77,856 annotated instances from 454 subjects. Built upon MMA-82, we establish two core tasks: Micro-Action Recognition and Multi-label Micro-Action Detection. For recognition, we further define in-domain and cross-domain protocols, including few-shot and zero-shot settings, to evaluate model robustness, transferability, and generalization. Extensive experiments show that current methods still struggle with realistic micro-action understanding, especially under domain shift, long-tailed category distributions, and complex temporal localization. Beyond benchmarking, we investigate the relationship between micro-actions and emotion, showing that micro-actions are strongly associated with emotional states and provide complementary cues to facial micro-expressions for improved emotion recognition. These results demonstrate that MMA-82 serves as a comprehensive and challenging benchmark for realistic micro-action analysis and a valuable resource for human-centered AI. MMA-82 is available at https://github.com/LpyNow/MMA-82.

### [30] [Conditioning Matters: Stabilizing Inversion and Attention in Diffusion Image Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14125)
*Zheyuan Zhan,Hongchen Li,Can Wang,Yinfei Ma,Mingzhen Huang,Ruoshi Bai,Jiawei Chen,Siwei Lyu,Defang Chen*

TL;DR: SimEdit提出了一种条件感知框架，通过改进文本条件的精确性和结构对齐性来提升图像反演稳定性，并通过词级跨分支注意力控制实现编辑相关与结构保持成分的非对称调节，从而在保持背景一致性的同时提高语义保真度。实验表明其在PIE-Bench上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于反演的图像编辑方法在反演精度、编辑保真度与背景保留之间存在权衡，且文本条件对扩散动力学和编辑行为的影响尚未被充分探索。

Method: 提出SimEdit框架，包含两个互补组件：(a) 条件精炼，提升条件信号的语义精确性和结构对齐性；(b) 词级跨分支注意力控制，分离并非对称调控编辑相关与结构保持成分。

Result: 在PIE-Bench上的实验显示，SimEdit显著提升了反演重建质量和编辑性能，优于先前的注意力操控方法。

Conclusion: 文本条件的精确性直接影响扩散速度场的几何特性，进而影响反演稳定性和注意力一致性；SimEdit通过条件精炼与词级注意力控制有效缓解了背景保留与语义保真之间的矛盾。

Abstract: Inversion-based image editing offers flexible and training-free control but still struggles with inversion accuracy and the trade-off between editing fidelity and background preservation. While recent methods improve inversion formulations or attention interactions, the role of textual conditioning in shaping diffusion dynamics and editing behavior remains underexplored. We show both empirically and theoretically that the precision of textual conditioning influences inversion stability by modulating the geometry of the diffusion velocity field, while also affecting the consistency of cross-branch attention during editing. These effects directly impact background preservation and semantic fidelity. Building on this analysis, we propose SimEdit, a conditioning-aware framework with two complementary components: (a) conditioning refinement, which constructs conditioning signals with improved semantic precision and structural alignment to facilitate stable inversion and consistent attention manipulation, and (b) token-wise cross-branch attention control, which separates edit-relevant and structure-preserving components and modulates them asymmetrically during attention manipulation. Extensive experiments on PIE-Bench demonstrate that SimEdit consistently improves both inversion reconstruction quality and editing performance over previous attention-manipulation approaches. Our code is available at https://github.com/zju-pi/SimEdit.

### [31] [BoRAD: Bootstrap your Own Representations for Multi-class Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14129)
*Duy Hoang Khuong,Tri Nguyen Minh,Ngu Huynh Cong Viet*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: BoRAD 是一种无标签训练框架，用于解决工业检测中从特定类别到通用异常检测的扩展挑战。通过共享可学习原型库施加两种互补正则化：空间原型对齐抑制局部异常复制，原型相对全局对齐保持原型间结构并增强对异常角度偏差的敏感性。训练时使用原型库和预测头，推理时保持标准教师-学生特征差异流程，无需类别标签、负样本对、记忆检索或原型查找。在 MVTec AD、VisA 和 Real-IAD 上分别取得 86.2%、80.7% 和 73.1% 的 mAD 性能，且诊断分析显示异常泄漏减少、正常类别可分性提高、异常与正常得分分离更强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于重建的异常检测方法在从类别特定训练扩展到通用设置时面临两大耦合失败模式：相同快捷方式（异常通过重建路径）和误重建（正常类别混淆）。如何让单一模型有效重建多样正常外观而不复制异常细节，是关键挑战。

Method: 提出 BoRAD 框架，利用共享可学习原型库引入两个互补正则化：空间原型对齐（约束局部原型内变化，防止异常复制），原型相对全局对齐（保持原型间结构，提升对异常角度偏差的敏感性）。训练阶段使用原型库和预测头，推理阶段采用标准教师-学生特征差异机制，无需标签、负样本、记忆检索或原型查询。

Result: 在 MVTec AD（86.2% mAD）、VisA（80.7% mAD）和 Real-IAD（73.1% mAD）上实现竞争性性能；诊断分析表明异常泄漏显著降低，正常类别可分性提升，异常与正常得分分离更明显。

Conclusion: BoRAD 有效解决了通用异常检测中的重建耦合问题，通过原型正则化实现高质量无监督训练，同时保持推理简洁高效，为工业异常检测提供了强健且实用的新范式。

Abstract: Reconstruction-based anomaly detection is attractive for industrial inspection, but scaling it from category-specific training to a one-for-all setting is challenging. A single model must reconstruct diverse normal appearances without copying abnormal details, which exposes two coupled failure modes: identical shortcut, where anomalies pass through the reconstruction path, and mis-reconstruction, where normal categories are confused with one another. We propose \textbf{BoRAD}, a label-free training framework that treats this as a representation-capacity allocation problem. BoRAD uses a shared learnable prototype bank to impose two complementary regularizers: spatial prototype alignment contracts local within-prototype variation to suppress anomaly copying, while prototype-relative global alignment preserves between-prototype structure and improves sensitivity to abnormal angular deviations. The prototype bank and prediction heads are used only during training; inference remains a standard teacher-student feature discrepancy pass, with no class labels, negative pairs, memory retrieval, or prototype lookup. BoRAD achieves competitive one-for-all anomaly detection performance, including 86.2\% mAD on MVTec AD, 80.7\% mAD on VisA and 73.1\% mAD on Real-IAD. Diagnostic analyses further show reduced anomaly leakage, improved normal-category separability, and stronger anomaly-normal score separation.

### [32] [Encoder Winners Do Not Reliably Transfer Across VLA Backbone Scale: A Frozen-Backbone Grafting Diagnostic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14153)
*Qingping Zeng,Fei She*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种冻结主干网嫁接诊断方法，用于评估视觉编码器在不同规模的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型中的迁移性能。通过固定协议（自适应平均池化、LayerNorm和单个可训练线性投影器）替换已发布VLA的视觉塔，并保持语言模型和动作专家冻结，实验覆盖四种编码器、两个LIBERO任务套件、两种主干网络（SmolVLA-450M 和 $π_{0.5}$-3.3B）及多组随机种子。结果表明，小规模主干上的最优编码器并不稳定地适用于大规模主干；例如，SigLIP在SmolVLA上表现最佳，而DINOv2-small在$π_{0.5}$的两个任务中分别领先或接近平局。此外，嫁接包装本身对不同主干具有非中性影响（在SmolVLA上增加45-56%的行动均方误差，在$π_{0.5}$上则减少50-52%），因此所有结论都依赖于固定的嫁接协议。研究将冻结嫁接定位为一种低成本的预筛选工具，用于在大规模部署前评估编码器选择，而非闭环部署依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前视觉-语言-动作（VLA）策略通常继承上游视觉语言模型（VLM）的视觉编码器，但缺乏明确证据表明在小型VLA上验证的编码器选择是否能有效迁移至更大规模的主干网络。这种不确定性可能导致在大规模部署时选择不当的编码器，造成性能损失。因此，亟需一种可靠且低成本的方法来评估编码器在不同主干结构下的泛化能力，以指导实际应用中的编码器选型。

Method: 提出一种冻结主干网嫁接诊断方法：将已发布的VLA的视觉塔替换为候选编码器，采用统一协议（自适应平均池化、LayerNorm、单个可训练线性投影器），同时冻结语言模型和动作专家。通过在多个编码器、主干网络和任务套件上进行系统性测试，评估不同配置下的性能表现，并对比原生模型与控制组（如LoRA、池化、零/随机图像等）的表现差异，以分析编码器选择的可靠性与条件依赖性。

Result: 实验结果显示，小规模主干上的最优编码器无法稳定预测大规模主干上的最佳选择；例如，SigLIP在SmolVLA上表现最佳，而DINOv2-small在$π_{0.5}$的两个任务中分别领先或形成种子敏感的近似平局。11/12的种子级别单元支持主干依赖性排名，且嫁接包装本身对不同主干具有显著非中性影响（在SmolVLA上使误差增加45-56%，在$π_{0.5}$上则降低50-52%），说明结论高度依赖于具体的嫁接协议。

Conclusion: 冻结主干网嫁接是一种高效、低成本的诊断工具，可用于在大规模部署前对候选编码器进行初步筛选，但不能作为最终部署决策的直接依据。其有效性受具体嫁接协议的影响，必须在特定条件下解释结果，强调了主干架构对编码器性能排名的决定性作用。

Abstract: Vision-language-action (VLA) policies typically inherit their vision encoder from upstream VLM releases, but it is unclear whether an encoder choice validated on a small VLA transfers to a larger backbone. We introduce a frozen-backbone grafting diagnostic: the vision tower of a released VLA is replaced by a candidate encoder under a fixed protocol (adaptive average pooling, LayerNorm, and a single trainable linear projector), with the language model and action expert frozen. Across four encoders, two LIBERO suites, two backbones (SmolVLA-450M and $π_{0.5}$-3.3B), and two-to-three seeds per cell (40 main grafting runs plus native, LoRA, pooling, and zero-/shuffled-image controls, all scored by offline action MSE), the small-backbone winner does not reliably select the large-backbone top tier: SigLIP is best on SmolVLA across both suites, while on $π_{0.5}$ DINOv2-small leads the spatial suite and the object suite is a seed-sensitive near-tie band; three of the four backbone-suite comparisons (and 11 of 12 seed-level cells) support backbone-dependent rankings. The grafting wrapper is itself non-neutral with opposite sign across backbones (+45-56% MSE on the SmolVLA native tower, -50-52% on $π_{0.5}$), so all conclusions are conditional on the fixed grafting protocol. We position frozen grafting as a cheap target-backbone diagnostic to run before committing to an encoder at scale, not as a closed-loop deployment claim.

### [33] [VideoWeave: Unlocking Geometric Consistency in Video Generation via Joint Geometry-Video Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14162)
*Xunzhi Xiang,Zixuan Duan,Yabo Chen,Zhengxuan Wei,Guiyu Zhang,Zixiao Gu,Zhe Gao,Haibin Huang,Chi Zhang,Qi Fan,Xuelong Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VideoWeave 是一种基于潜在空间的后训练框架，通过隐式几何特征约束生成分布，以提升视频扩散模型在视角变化下的几何一致性，避免显式几何重建误差的影响。该方法将几何特征转化为几何潜在变量，并与视频潜在变量联合建模于共享去噪空间中，从而在训练过程中实现更灵活、非刚性的几何引导。为此，研究构建了包含8万段视频的GeoVid-80K数据集，支持外观与几何表示的配对学习。实验表明，VideoWeave 在文本到视频和图像到视频生成任务中均显著提升了几何连贯性，同时保持高质量视觉表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大规模视频扩散模型在时间上难以保持3D结构，导致视角变化时出现几何漂移和不合理运动。传统方法依赖深度图、点云或3D重建等显式几何信息作为条件、监督或奖励信号，但这些方法对上游几何重建误差敏感，影响生成质量。因此，亟需一种更鲁棒且灵活的几何一致性约束机制。

Method: VideoWeave 提出在潜在空间中使用隐式几何特征作为指导信号，将几何特征映射为几何潜在变量，并与视频潜在变量共同嵌入一个共享的去噪空间中进行联合建模。该设计允许几何信息在训练过程中动态影响生成分布，从而提供非刚性、可适应的几何引导，降低对显式几何重建精度的依赖。此外，研究构建了大规模的 GeoVid-80K 数据集，包含成对的外观与几何表示，用于训练和评估。

Result: 在文本到视频和图像到视频生成任务中，VideoWeave 显著提升了生成视频的几何一致性，尤其在视角变换下表现出更强的结构稳定性。同时，其在视觉质量方面保持甚至优于基线模型，证明了该方法在几何约束与视觉保真之间的良好平衡。

Conclusion: VideoWeave 通过隐式几何特征在潜在空间中的联合建模，实现了对视频生成过程的有效几何引导，有效缓解了因显式几何重建误差带来的问题。该框架具有良好的灵活性与泛化能力，为高保真、几何一致的视频生成提供了新范式。

Abstract: Large-scale video diffusion models often fail to preserve 3D structure over time, causing geometric drift and implausible motion under viewpoint changes. Existing methods usually enforce geometric consistency by using explicit geometry reconstructions, such as depth maps, point clouds, or reconstructed 3D structures, to define conditions, supervision, or reward signals, making the generator sensitive to errors from upstream geometry pipelines. We propose VideoWeave, a latent-space post-training framework that uses implicit geometry-model features to constrain the generative distribution, providing a more flexible and non-rigid form of guidance that mitigates the impact of reconstruction errors from geometry models. Specifically, VideoWeave adapts these features into geometry latents and jointly models them with video latents in a shared denoising space, allowing geometry to shape the generative distribution during training. To support this process, we build GeoVid-80K, an 80K-video dataset with paired appearance and geometry representations. Experiments on text-to-video and image-to-video generation show that VideoWeave improves geometric coherence while preserving strong visual quality. VideoWeave project page at https://videoweave.github.io/

### [34] [MUSE: Agentic 3D Scene Authoring via Memory-Grounded Incremental Requirement Satisfaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14168)

Method: MUSE采用多智能体架构：建筑师将指令转化为结构化需求，雕塑家执行局部操作，检查员验证每一步并更新工作记忆、场景记忆和技能记忆，实现增量式需求满足。

To tackle this challenge, we formulate controllable 3D scene authoring as incremental requirement satisfaction, unifying construction and editing. In this paper, we present MUSE, a memory-grounded multi-agent framework in which an Architect compiles instructions into structured requirements, a Sculptor executes local scene operations, and an Inspector verifies each step while updating Working, Scene, and Skill Memory. To evaluate requirement-level controllability and preservation-aware editing, we introduce AuthorBench, offering 145 constrained construction cases and a 1,584-case preservation-aware editing pool paired with external structured checks. On full construction cases, MUSE improves All-Goal success from 37.9 to 80.7 and surface-constraint fulfillment from 35.0 to 92.6 over the strongest baseline. On a stratified 240-case editing test split, MUSE achieves 49.6 All-Goal success, 99.9 preservation rate, and only 0.6 unintended change rate. Beyond automated metrics, human evaluations on compared local-editing baselines support stronger alignment with user intent, and downstream navigation-proxy tests indicate stronger spatial stability. Combined with ablations validating our memory designs, these results establish MUSE as an effective framework for controllable 3D scene authoring.

### [35] [Hybrid Classical-Quantum (HCQ) Alzheimer's Classification via Supervised $β$-VAE and Quantum Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14194)
*Tia Tiwari,Vamshi Krishna Kancharla,Neelam Sinha*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种两阶段混合经典-量子（HCQ）管道，用于从3D T1加权结构磁共振成像（MRI）中进行阿尔茨海默病（AD）二分类。该方法结合经典与量子组件，通过监督式3D β-变分自编码器（VAE）将MRI体积压缩为64维潜在码，并利用偏最小二乘法（PLS）选出最具区分性的6个成分作为量子门旋转角度，编码至六量子比特寄存器，生成量子态。随后使用预计算核支持向量机（SVM）基于量子态间的重叠构建N×N核矩阵进行分类。相比基线模型（67.2%准确率，0.759 AUC），改进版本达到72.1%准确率和0.799 AUC，且交叉验证方差减半。3D Grad-CAM验证了模型关注于与阿尔茨海默病相关的脑区。该框架可推广至其他生物医学影像诊断任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统经典方法在处理复杂、高维的生物医学影像数据时面临特征提取困难与分类性能瓶颈；同时，现有量子机器学习方法多依赖手工特征或未经优化的输入，难以有效捕捉疾病特异性信息。因此，亟需一种能端到端学习疾病相关特征并高效融合经典与量子计算优势的新范式。

Method: 采用端到端训练的3D β-变分自编码器对3D MRI进行降维与特征学习，输出64维潜在码；通过偏最小二乘回归筛选出最能区分AD与对照组的6个潜在成分，并将其转化为量子门旋转角；使用ZZ量子特征映射将这些角度编码为六量子比特的量子态；构建基于量子态重叠的预计算核矩阵，输入至支持向量机完成分类任务。

Result: 在ADNI-1数据集（308名受试者，137例AD，171例CN）上，基线模型达到67.2%准确率和0.759 AUC；稳定性增强版本提升至72.1%准确率和0.799 AUC，且交叉验证方差降低一半。3D Grad-CAM可视化显示模型聚焦于已知与阿尔茨海默病相关的脑区，如海马体和内侧颞叶。

Conclusion: 所提出的两阶段混合经典-量子框架能够有效利用端到端学习的疾病感知特征，实现高性能且稳定的阿尔茨海默病分类。其核心创新在于将量子核方法应用于由监督自编码器学习得到的语义有意义特征，而非原始图像或手工特征。该框架具有通用性，适用于多种存在挑战的经典方法难以应对的生物医学影像分类任务。

Abstract: This paper presents a two-stage Hybrid Classical-Quantum (HCQ) pipeline for binary Alzheimer's disease (AD) classification from 3D T1-weighted structural MRI volumes, where the classical and quantum components are designed to complement each other rather than operate independently. A supervised 3D $β$-variational autoencoder (VAE) is trained end-to-end under voxel-wise reconstruction, KL-divergence, and focal classification losses that compress each 3D MRI volume (resized from 152 x 184 x 152 to 96 x 96 x 96) into a 64-dimensional latent code. Partial Least Squares (PLS) regression selects the six components in the latent code that best separate Alzheimer's Disease (AD) from cognitively normal (CN) subjects and rescales them into rotation angles, which are encoded onto a six-qubit register using the ZZ quantum feature map to give us the respective quantum states. The input to a precomputed-kernel Support Vector Machine (SVM) is an N x N Gram matrix (N = 308), created by calculating the overlap between every pair of quantum states. The novelty of this work lies in the fact that the quantum kernel operates directly on disease-aware features that are learned end-to-end by a supervised autoencoder, rather than on pre-extracted inputs. On 308 ADNI-1 subjects, consisting of 137 AD and 171 CN subjects, the baseline achieved 67.2% accuracy and 0.759 AUC, while the stability-enhanced variant reached 72.1% accuracy and 0.799 AUC with cross-fold variance halved. 3D Grad-CAM further helped validate our model's focus on brain regions linked to Alzheimer's. The HCQ pipeline could serve as a general-purpose framework for diagnostic classification across biomedical imaging domains that present similar challenges for classical approaches.

</details>

Abstract: Deepfakes are artificially generated images, audio, or videos that threaten privacy, security, and information integrity. Detecting such content is crucial for countering disinformation, as the latest models generate highly realistic content. While spatial- or frequency-based approaches achieve good detection rates on Generative Adversarial Networks (GANs)-based generated deepfakes, they often struggle with recent diffusion model-generated images. In particular, existing approaches rarely exploit complementary multi-domain representations or systematically evaluate cross-generator robustness. To address these challenges, we propose a multi-domain deepfake detection framework called SGFF-Net (Spatial-Gradient-Frequency Fusion Network) that integrates spatial, gradient, and DWT (Discrete Wavelet Transform)-based frequency representations within a dual residual learning architecture. Experimental results show that the SGFF-Net achieves 98.95\% accuracy in intra-dataset evaluation and improves performance in both cross-model (70.46\%) and cross-paradigm (69.94\%) settings. Incorporating multi-source training and data augmentation further enhances robustness, increasing accuracy from 70.46\% to 79.80\% in cross-model evaluation, from 69\% to 78\% in cross-paradigm evaluation, and from 61.50\% to 75.80\% on real-world data. Unlike single-domain detectors, the SGFF-Net learns complementary forensic cues across spatial, gradient, and wavelet-frequency domains, resulting in greater robustness under cross-generator and cross-paradigm evaluation. The results further show that combining multi-domain representations with data diversity and augmentation substantially improves generalization, providing practical insights for developing more reliable deepfake detection systems.

### [37] [HiST: A Hierarchical Sparse Transformer for Cross-Modal Spatial Transcriptomics Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14251)
*Weiyi Wu,Xinwen Xu,Xingjian Diao,Siting Li,Zhi Wei,Alma Andersson,Jiang Gui*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HiST 是一种用于从 H&E 染色图像预测空间转录组数据的层次稀疏变压器模型。它通过将测量位置视为晶格索引的稀疏场，直接在活性组织区域上构建双射编码器-解码器，结合稀疏窗口注意力与分辨率变化操作，实现快速多尺度上下文整合。其计算复杂度随观测点数量增长而非全图面积，显著降低内存和运行时间。此外，引入滑片校准标记以缓解不同滑片间的采集差异，在多器官基准测试中优于现有基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空间转录组技术成本高且通量低，需要高效替代方法从常规 H&E 染色图像推断基因表达。现有方法在处理大尺寸、稀疏不规则采样点的全幻灯片图像时面临多尺度建模挑战，尤其易受密集网格开销或二次项混合影响。

Method: 提出 HiST（Hierarchical Sparse Transformer），利用稀疏窗口注意力捕捉局部几何对应关系，并通过分辨率变化算子实现快速多尺度上下文融合；采用晶格索引稀疏场表示测量点，构建基于活性组织轮廓的编码器-解码器结构；引入滑片校准标记作为全局条件路径，以统一对不同滑片采集差异的建模。

Result: 在涵盖多种组织类型和数据来源的多器官基准测试中，HiST 在预测性能上优于近期基线模型，同时显著降低运行时间和峰值内存占用。

Conclusion: HiST 为大规模空间转录组推断提供了一种高效、可扩展且鲁棒的解决方案，适用于真实临床场景中的全幻灯片分析。

Abstract: Spatial transcriptomics (ST) links gene expression with tissue morphology but remains expensive and low-throughput, motivating surrogates that infer expression from routine histology. Whole-slide H&E-to-ST inference pairs a gigapixel image with gene measurements at a sparse, irregular set of locations, making multiscale modeling challenging without incurring dense-grid overhead or quadratic token mixing. We propose HiST, a hierarchical sparse transformer that treats measured locations as a lattice-indexed sparse field and builds a dyadic encoder--decoder directly on the active tissue footprint. HiST combines sparse window attention for local geometric correspondence with resolution-changing operators for rapid multiscale context integration. For a fixed window size, the dominant runtime and memory scale with the number of observed locations rather than the dense slide area. To mitigate slide-specific acquisition variation, HiST adds a bottlenecked global conditioning pathway via a \emph{slide calibration token} that summarizes slide-level context and conditions local representations. On a multi-organ benchmark spanning diverse tissues and acquisition sources, HiST improves predictive performance over recent baselines while reducing runtime and peak memory.
