<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉标记剪枝方法在特定层剪枝后无法恢复，导致信息过早丢失，影响模型性能；不同层对视觉区域的关注度不同，存在各层最优标记子集。

Method: 设计轻量级标记选择器，动态识别重要标记并路由处理，不重要标记则跳过当前层，两路标记在后续层前重新融合，结合低秩近似约束保证重要性一致性，模拟完整注意力机制。

Result: 在LLaVA-1.5、LLaVA-NeXT和Qwen2.5-VL上验证，89%标记压缩下保留96.7%原始精度，显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: ALVTS突破传统静态剪枝局限，实现分层自适应压缩，在效率与精度间取得更优平衡，为大型视觉语言模型高效部署提供有效解决方案。

Abstract: Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) have achieved remarkable success across diverse multimodal tasks, yet their practical deployment remains constrained by the computational burden arising from lengthy visual tokens. While visual token pruning has emerged as a promising solution, existing methods suffer from a fundamental limitation: once tokens are pruned at a specific layer, they become inaccessible to all subsequent layers, leading to premature information loss that can compromise model performance. Through empirical studies, we observe that different layers exhibit distinct visual region focus, indicating a varying optimal token subset across layers. Motivated by this insight, we propose Adaptive Layer-wise Visual Token Selection (ALVTS), a novel framework that breaks away from the conventional static token pruning paradigm. ALVTS incorporates a lightweight token selector to identify and route important tokens for further processing, while allowing less important tokens to skip the layer, thus minimizing computational redundancy. These two streams of tokens are seamlessly reintegrated before being fed into subsequent layers, facilitating adaptive compression across the entire model. Grounded in our importance consistency constrained low-rank approximation, the proposed token selection module closely emulates the full attention mechanism, effectively capturing its essential patterns without requiring model retraining. Extensive experiments on LLaVA-1.5, LLaVA-NeXT, and Qwen2.5-VL validate the effectiveness of our method. With an 89% token compression ratio, ALVTS retains 96.7% of the original model's accuracy, achieving a superior efficiency-accuracy trade-off for LVLM inference.

By combining discrete and continuous encoding, our design replaces traditional Multilayer Perceptrons (MLPs) with more efficient and robust BINNs. Building upon this framework, we further propose an extended model, DC-CCNN++, to improve robustness under complex corruption conditions. Specifically, we introduce a Neuro-Inspired Robust Modulation-and-Readout Module (NRMR) to enhance feature stability and decision robustness through global-context gain modulation and dual-code evidence integration. We also design a Cortically Inspired Progressive Variability Training (CPVT) strategy, which progressively exposes the model to structured environmental variability while preserving stable clean-sample anchors during training. Experimental results show that DC-CCNN++ improves the performance of brain-inspired networks on point cloud analysis while maintaining performance comparable to state-of-the-art methods. Compared with the original DC-CCNN, it achieves stronger results on both classification and part segmentation, and exhibits enhanced robustness against sparsity, occlusion, Gaussian noise, salt-and-pepper noise, and spatial transformations. With its efficiency, robustness, and biologically grounded design, DC-CCNN++ provides a promising alternative to traditional deep learning methods for point cloud analysis. Code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/DC-CCNNpp-44E3.

*Jiazhen Huang,Xiao Chen,Zhiming Liu,Yaru Sun,Jingyan Jiang,Zhi Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将现有方法归纳为三类统一范式；构建开放源码的TTABC基准，标准化评估协议并集成20余种代表性方法；通过受控实验分析参数更新、证据利用方式及不同分布偏移下的适应表现。

Result: 发现参数基方法的增益主要来自测试时证据与可靠代理而非复杂优化；轻量级原型更新与跨样本/当前样本证据利用即可实现高效且有竞争力的性能；不存在适用于所有分布偏移的万能适应范式，最优策略依赖于具体偏移类型。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) such as CLIP have become a standard backbone for open-vocabulary recognition, yet their zero-shot predictions remain vulnerable to distribution shifts encountered at deployment. Test-Time Adaptation (TTA) has recently been extended to CLIP as a lightweight solution, leading to a rapidly growing body of TTA4CLIP methods. However, empirical progress in this area has largely outpaced our understanding of what truly drives adaptation, where their gains originate, and under which shifts they remain reliable. In this paper, we take a step back from the pursuit of state-of-the-art accuracy and conduct a systematic controlled study of TTA4CLIP. We first organize existing methods into three unified paradigms according to what is updated at test time. We then introduce TTABC, an open-source TTA Benchmark for CLIP, which standardizes evaluation protocols and integrates more than 20 representative methods. Our controlled empirical analysis focuses on three key areas. First, we determine the driving factors in parameter-based methods, revealing that adaptation gains are primarily driven by test-time evidence and reliable proxies rather than heavy optimization. Second, we explore evidence utilization beyond heavy parameter tuning, showing that competitive and efficient performance can be achieved through cross- or current-sample evidence and lightweight prototype updates. Finally, we demonstrate that there is no silver bullet for TTA: no single adaptation paradigm is universally optimal, and the preferred paradigm depends on the nature of shift. We hope our benchmark and study provide a clearer understanding of the current TTA4CLIP landscape and establish a foundation for further research.

We build on existing 3D reconstruction models and augment them with a set-based mask decoder. The approach is jointly trained with a geometric and semantic loss, which are shown to be mutually beneficial. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: PUtPFS采用优化策略，通过选取稀疏区域的点集，利用空间频率叠加技术估计表面，并在该表面上生成新点，逐步提升点云密度以实现均匀上采样。

Abstract: In recent years, neural networks have become the dominant models in most point cloud upsampling methods. Although these approaches are achieving good results, they do have drawbacks, such as a lack of interpretability and data dependency. Moreover, they have to be trained on a dataset that is similar to the test data in order to perform well. To avoid these disadvantages, we propose Point Cloud Upsampling through Patch-based Frequency Superposition (PUtPFS), an optimization-based approach that selects subsets of points and estimates the surface of this set through superpositioning spatial frequencies. Then, new points are placed on this surface. By successively selecting points in the least dense regions of the point cloud, a uniform upsampling can be reached. With this method, we surpass the current best upsampling results in the commonly considered point-to-surface distance. Furthermore, we achieve the best Chamfer and Hausdorff distance among the optimization-based approaches. As an additional advantage, our method does not need any training data and is mathematically interpretable.

### [46] [FLaRA: Predicting Future Latent Representations for Accident Anticipation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14380)

Abstract: Anticipating traffic accidents from dashcam videos is a critical challenge in intelligent transportation systems. Existing methods typically map visual context directly to a collision probability without explicitly modeling the future evolution of the driving scene. In this paper we propose FLaRA (Predicting Future Latent Representations for Accident Anticipation), a novel predictive architecture that shifts this paradigm by forecasting future latent representations for accident anticipation. Building upon the Video Joint-Embedding Predictive Architecture (V-JEPA2), our model conditions a predictor network on observed context frames to predict the forthcoming latent features of the scene. A classifier then operates on these predicted future representations rather than only on past observations. To ensure these forecasts remain grounded in realistic future dynamics, we introduce a joint training objective that simultaneously optimizes an auxiliary feature-level reconstruction loss and a cross-entropy classification loss. Extensive evaluations on the Nexar dataset, alongside cross-domain validations on the DAD, DADA-2000, and DoTA benchmarks, demonstrate that our approach achieves state-of-the-art performance while maintaining realistic early warning capabilities.

Conclusion: 多图像工业产品理解的关键挑战不在于单图识别准确率，而在于跨图像证据整合与完整性恢复能力。现有MLLMs在处理复杂、分散的工业规格信息时存在明显局限，亟需发展更强的跨模态推理与上下文整合机制。该基准已公开，可推动后续研究。

To fill this gap, we introduce IndustryBench-MIPU, the first large-scale benchmark for multi-image industrial product understanding, built around structured attribute extraction -- recovering property-value pairs from product images. Concretely, the benchmark comprises 4,559 products across 27,652 images with 103,703 annotations spanning 18 industrial categories, constructed through multi-model consensus and three-tier quality assurance.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Industrial anomaly detection suffers from limited data, making cross-domain generalization particularly challenging. Generalist Anomaly Detection (GAD) aims to train a unified model on a source domain that can effectively detect anomalies in unseen target domains. In the initial semantic feature space, strong entanglement between anomalies and object categories or defect types hinders effective generalization across domains. Recent works address this issue by projecting features into a residual space; however, such methods primarily increase cross-domain overlap for normal features, while anomalous features remain specific to object categories, defect types and data domains, leading to poor alignment and generalization. To address this limitation, we propose Value-order Decomposition (VOD), a simple yet effective technique that bridges \textbf{three types of generalization gaps} across object categories, defect types (including real and synthetic defects), and data domains. VOD disentangles and suppresses object-category-, defect-type-, and domain-specific information, promoting alignment within normal and abnormal samples while preserving their separability, thereby enabling robust generalization across the three gaps. Leveraging the strong alignment between real and synthetic defects within the same object, we perform anomaly detection using only normal and synthetic-abnormal reference, and effectively generalize to unseen real defect types. Experiments on diverse industrial and medical benchmarks demonstrate that our method, using a simple cut-and-paste anomaly simulation strategy, achieves strong generalization across the three gaps.

### [50] [Scratched Lenses, Shifted Depth: Passive Camera-Side Optical Attacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14504)
*Qinlin He,Zeming Zhuang,Yongji Wu,Lan Zhang,Xiaoyong,Yuan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为SLASH的新型物理对抗攻击，通过相机镜头或保护罩上的微小划痕，在特定光照条件下产生结构化光条纹伪影，干扰几何推断。该攻击在光学空间中建模，具有持久性与场景触发特性，可在单目深度估计和3D目标检测任务中引发高达32%的相对误差，并在真实世界中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有物理对抗攻击多关注图像空间扰动或可控制的场景操纵，忽略了硬件缺陷与环境光、光学系统之间的复杂交互；本文揭示了被动式镜头侧损伤（如划痕）作为潜在攻击面的可能性，其在特定视觉条件下才会触发，但一旦触发则持续影响感知系统。

Method: 将划痕建模为触发条件依赖的光学通道，基于光学空间进行攻击设计，优化单一固定配置以适应多种观测条件；采用物理-数字联合评估框架验证攻击效果。

Result: 在单目深度估计中，方向性深度偏差最高达32%相对误差；在单目3D目标检测中也表现出一致的负面影响；真实相机实验验证了攻击在现实场景中的可迁移性与有效性。

Conclusion: 微小的硬件缺陷（如划痕）在特定光照下可能成为隐蔽且可触发的对抗性机制，挑战了视觉系统对物理鲁棒性的假设，提示需加强针对此类攻击的防御设计。

Abstract: Physical adversarial attacks on vision systems are typically studied through scene manipulation, such as adversarial patches or projections, where the adversary controls what the camera observes. Camera-side attacks using stickers or auxiliary optics have also been explored, but they treat attacks as image-space perturbations from designed patterns. This misses how physical imperfections interact with scene-dependent lighting and optics. We identify a threat: passive lens-side damage that is persistent yet trigger-conditioned, producing optical artifacts that bias geometric inference under particular visual conditions.
  We instantiate this threat through Scratch-induced Lens Adversarial Streak Hijacking SLASH, a physical-world attack caused by small scratches on a camera lens or protective cover. Scratches interact with bright light sources and specular reflections to create structured streak artifacts that distort depth cues. Since the perturbation is fixed in the optical path but triggered by the scene, it is both persistent and selective. We formulate the attack in optical space, model the scratch pattern as a trigger-conditioned optical channel, and optimize one fixed configuration across diverse viewing conditions. We evaluate SLASH on monocular depth estimation and monocular 3D object detection in digital and real-world settings. Under the fixed-scratch constraint, directional depth shifts reach up to 32% relative error for monocular depth estimation, with consistent effects on monocular 3D object detection. Physical experiments confirm transfer to real camera recordings, inducing depth shifts above the model's natural prediction baseline. These findings reveal an attack surface where benign-looking hardware imperfections act as latent, scene-triggered adversarial mechanisms, challenging assumptions about physical robustness and motivating defenses for secure vision systems.

</details>


### [51] [A Lightweight Fiducial-Based Pipeline for 3D Hyperspectral Mapping of ex-vivo Lumpectomy Specimens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14534)
*Anna Bicchi,Alberto Rota,Leonardo Passoni,Nicola Ancellotti,Andrea Peroni,Lorenzo Vinco,Dario Polli,Elena De Momi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种全自动、无需校准的管道，可从消费级相机的RGB图像和单次顶视高光谱成像（HSI）获取中生成体外乳房切除标本的3D高光谱点云。通过深度学习的运动结构（SfM）重建几何形状，并利用自定义的捆绑调整保持度量参考框架的一致性。通过四个ArUco标记的角点对应关系，将HSI立方体注册到重建结果中，无需恢复HSI相机姿态。3D坐标通过正交渲染的深度图查找获得。在两个体外乳房切除样本上评估，该方法实现了低于1毫米的中位3D配准误差和低于0.02毫米的2D重投影误差，单个样本处理时间少于4分钟（加速硬件）。结果支持将HSI引导的空间定位整合到保乳手术的术中边缘评估流程中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了实现高光谱成像（HSI）在保乳手术术中边缘评估中的临床应用，需要将固有的二维光谱信息与切除组织的三维形状对齐，以精确定位可疑区域并进行针对性后续处理。然而，传统方法依赖复杂的校准过程，限制了其临床转化。因此，亟需一种自动化、无需校准的解决方案来实现高效的3D HSI点云生成与空间配准。

Method: 采用基于深度学习的运动结构（SfM）重建3D几何；通过放置在标本周围的四个ArUco标记的角点，使用自定义捆绑调整稳定在度量参考系中；利用标记在两种模态中可见的特点，建立16个角点对应关系，驱动平面单应性变换，将HSI立方体注册到3D重建中；3D坐标通过正交渲染的深度图查表获得。

Result: 在两个体外乳房切除标本上的实验表明，该方法的中位3D配准误差低于1毫米，2D重投影误差低于0.02毫米，单个标本处理时间在加速硬件下小于4分钟，证明了该方法在临床应用中的可行性。

Conclusion: 所提出的全自动、无校准的3D高光谱点云生成管道，能够高效、精确地实现体外乳房切除标本的多模态空间对齐，为将高光谱成像技术集成到保乳手术的术中边缘评估流程中提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: Hyperspectral Imaging (HSI) is a promising modality for intraoperative assessment of resection margins in Breast-Conserving Surgery (BCS), but its clinical translation requires aligning the inherently 2D spectral information onto the 3D shape of the excised tissue so that suspicious regions can be precisely localized for targeted follow-up. We present a fully automated, calibration-free pipeline that produces a 3D hyperspectral point cloud of an ex-vivo lumpectomy specimen from a set of consumer-camera RGB images and a single top-down HSI acquisition. The 3D geometry is reconstructed with a deep-learning Structure-from-Motion backbone, stabilized in a metric reference frame by a custom bundle adjustment that enforces consistency on the corners of four ArUco markers placed around the specimen. The HSI cube is then registered to the reconstruction without recovering the HSI camera pose: the markers, visible in both modalities, define 16 corner correspondences that drive a planar homography, and 3D coordinates are recovered by lookup on an orthographically rendered depth map. Evaluated on two ex-vivo lumpectomy specimens, the pipeline achieves a median 3D registration error below 1~mm and a 2D reprojection error below 0.02 mm, with a total per-specimen processing time under 4 minutes on accelerated hardware. These results support the feasibility of integrating HSI-guided spatial localization into intraoperative margin assessment workflows for breast-conserving surgery.

### [52] [Rethinking Global Average Pooling: Your Classifier Is Secretly a Multi-Instance Learner](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14555)
*Aray Karjauv*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文探讨了现代图像分类器中全局平均池化（GAP）与线性分类头的组合结构，指出其在多对象场景下仍能有效学习分类任务，并提出一种基于多实例学习（MIL）的解释框架。通过将图像级逻辑值分解为预测网格，实现了对空间类别证据的后处理诊断，验证表明模型能一致地在前景区域恢复真实类别。此外，分类器失败的原因被归因于均值聚合的固有局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示标准分类器在使用GAP和线性分类头时，尽管图像级预测错误，仍保留可恢复的空间类别证据；探索如何利用这一特性进行故障诊断与分析。

Method: 采用多实例学习（MIL）视角重新解释标准分类器结构，通过将图像视为空间实例的集合，推导出图像级逻辑值与局部逻辑值之间的关系；设计并实现一种后处理方法，将图像级输出转化为预测网格以提取空间类别的分布信息。

Result: 实验表明，即使图像级预测错误，预训练模型仍能在前景区域准确恢复真实类别；常见分类失败现象与均值聚合的局限性高度相关。

Conclusion: 标准分类器的线性结构天然支持空间类别证据的保留，可通过后处理方法挖掘；该发现为理解模型行为、提升可解释性提供了新思路，并揭示了当前主流架构在复杂场景下的潜在缺陷。

Abstract: Modern image classifiers widely adopt global average pooling (GAP) followed by a linear classification head. This linearity ensures that the image-level logits equal the average of logits obtained by applying the classification head pointwise to the feature grid prior to GAP. Consequently, standard classifiers may inherently retain spatial class evidence that remains recoverable even when the image-level prediction is incorrect. This structure naturally suggests a multiple-instance learning (MIL) interpretation, where an image is viewed as a bag of spatial instances. Within this formulation, we demonstrate that standard classifiers trained with a single label per image can still learn the intended classification task in multi-object scenes. We further exploit this property to decompose image-level logits into a prediction grid, providing a post-hoc diagnostic to extract spatial class evidence that GAP otherwise obscures. Our systematic evaluation reveals that off-the-shelf models consistently recover the ground-truth class within foreground regions. The MIL interpretation further suggests that common classifier failures reflect known limitations of mean aggregation.

### [56] [S$^2$COPE: Self-Supervised Concept Discovery via Preference Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14586)
*Shilong Xiang,Zirui Zhang,Chengzhi Mao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为Self-Supervised Concept discOvery via Preference lEarning (\model)的无标签框架，通过让视觉-语言大模型（VLLM）在自监督偏好优化循环中主动参与，从原始图像中自主发现结构化概念，无需任何人工标注。该方法在自然、医学和物理等多个领域成功提取了标准VLLM难以生成的特定领域概念，并在下游分类任务中实现高达24个百分点的准确率提升，证明了可解释性可通过模型与视觉结构的自主交互自发产生。

Method: \\model框架利用VLLM作为主动参与者，在自监督偏好优化循环中自主假设、验证并强化候选视觉属性，直接从原始图像中发现新型结构化概念。通过将概念发现过程内嵌于VLLM主干网络，避免依赖静态生成与分离过滤，实现端到端的自监督学习。

Abstract: Current representation learning paradigms force a fundamental compromise: self-supervised methods scale to massive datasets but yield opaque features, whereas interpretable models remain bottlenecked by the need for dense human annotation. We introduce Self-Supervised Concept discOvery via Preference lEarning (\model), a label-free framework that resolves this dilemma. Instead of treating Vision-Large-Language Models (VLLMs) as static feature extractors, \model leverages them as active participants in a self-supervised preference optimization loop. By autonomously hypothesizing, validating, and reinforcing candidate visual attributes directly from raw imagery, our framework discovers novel, structured concepts without a single label. Extensive experiments across natural, medical, and physics domains demonstrate that \model successfully extracts domain-specific concepts where standard VLLMs often fail to generate. By amortizing concept discovery directly into the VLLM backbone through our self-supervised preference objective -- rather than relying on static generation and disjoint filtering -- we achieve up to a 24-point absolute improvement in downstream top-1 classification accuracy on unseen data. Our work suggest that interpretability can emerge through a model's autonomous interaction with incidental visual structures, without any human supervision.

### [58] [SED:Lightweight Saliency prediction for Event-based data via Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14631)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有事件感知显著性预测方法要么是类神经形态的且性能不佳，要么因依赖Transformer或3D卷积而过于庞大，难以在资源受限的边缘设备上部署。因此需要一种高效、轻量且能有效利用事件数据时间信息的方法。

Method: 提出基于深度时空卷积块（DSTconv）的轻量级网络SED，通过知识蒸馏从一个大型教师模型中学习，实现模型压缩与性能保留。DSTconv是对3D深度可分离卷积的分解，有效提取时空特征。

Result: 模型大小从180MB降至0.32MB（562倍压缩），参数量从45M降至81k（554倍压缩），在N-DHF1K和N-UCF Sports数据集上达到或超过教师模型性能，并能在合成到真实事件数据间良好迁移，而训练从头的模型无法做到这一点。

Abstract: Event-based saliency prediction has gained attention recently, as combining event cameras with saliency estimation can act as an upstream stage that naturally improves the efficiency of downstream eventbased perception at the edge. However, current approaches are either neuromorphic, underperforming on event-based saliency benchmarks, or too heavy for resource-constrained edge applications due to their reliance on transformers or 3D convolutions. Drawing inspiration from efficient convolutional modules, SED and aiming to exploit the temporal information in event data, we propose a lightweight network, trained through knowledge distillation, built on a Depthwise Spatio-Temporal Block (DSTconv) -- a factorization of the 3D depthwise separable convolution. Relative to its teacher, our model reduces the model size from 180 MB to 0.32 MB (562x) and the parameter count from 45M to 81k (554x), while matching or outperforming it on the N-DHF1K and N-UCF Sports datasets. Moreover, it generalizes strongly beyond its training distribution, transferring from synthetic to real event data where a model trained from scratch fails.

</details>


### [59] [Improving Lunar Topography with Deep Learning Schrödinger Bridges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14638)

Abstract: Increasing the resolution of planetary topography models can enable a better understanding of surface processes and geomorphology; however, existing analytical super-resolution methods are expensive and difficult to apply at large scales. We present a diffusion-based Schrödinger Bridge (SB) generative modeling approach for lunar topography super-resolution, connecting the distribution of low-resolution topography to that of high-resolution topography, incorporating physically-constraining optical imagery. ### [60] [HPSv3++: Scaling Reward Models Across the Full Spectrum of Diffusion Model Capabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14657)
*Yijun Liu,Jie Huang,Zeyue Xue,Yuming Li,Ruizhe He,Haoran Li,Shijia Ge,Siming Fu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HPSv3++ 是一种改进的奖励模型框架，旨在解决传统奖励模型（如 HPSv3）在应对文本到图像生成模型能力演进和强化学习迭代时的适应性不足问题。该框架引入了一个包含 21.2 万条双维度偏好数据（HPDv3++）的标注数据集，涵盖文本忠实度与美学质量，并基于最新高能力模型（Qwen-Image）进行人类监督标注。通过两阶段训练：第一阶段采用数据感知正交梯度投影，保留 HPSv3 的有效人类偏好知识并融合多样化的审美感知；第二阶段利用跨能力水平和强化学习迭代阶段的未标注数据，引入联合能力-迭代条件信号与标准差驱动的无监督引导机制，增强模型在全能力-迭代谱上的表现。实验表明，HPSv3++ 在 HPDv3、GenAI-Bench 等基准上分别超越 HPSv3 9.8% 和 5.5%，在自建的 HPDv3++ 上达到 79.1%/88.1% 的性能，且在多种 T2I 模型的 RL 训练中持续提升 GenEval 得分，展现出广泛的适用性。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有奖励模型（如 HPSv3）依赖于早期 T2I 模型的预标注数据，未能考虑模型能力演进和强化学习迭代带来的质量感知变化，导致其在新模型或不同训练阶段的应用中效果下降。因此，亟需一个能适应不同模型能力水平和训练迭代状态的通用奖励模型框架。

Method: 提出 HPSv3++ 框架，包含：1）构建 HPDv3++ 数据集（212K 条双维度偏好数据，由高能力模型辅助并经人类标注）；2）两阶段训练策略：第一阶段使用数据感知正交梯度投影，在保留原始偏好知识的同时融合多样化审美；第二阶段引入联合能力-迭代条件信号与标准差驱动的无监督引导机制，利用多阶段未标注数据增强模型泛化能力。

Result: HPSv3++ 在 HPDv3 基准上比 HPSv3 提升 9.8%，在 GenAI-Bench 上提升 5.5%，在自建的 HPDv3++ 上取得 79.1% 和 88.1% 的得分；用于 T2I 强化学习训练时，显著提升多种模型的 GenEval 评分，验证了其在不同能力水平与迭代阶段下的广泛适用性。

Conclusion: HPSv3++ 通过构建新型标注数据集与设计适应性强的两阶段训练框架，有效解决了奖励模型在模型能力演化和迭代过程中的适应性问题，实现了更稳定、更广泛适用的偏好预测能力，为下一代 T2I 系统的对齐训练提供了有力支持。

Abstract: Reward models guide text-to-image (T2I) systems toward outputs aligned with human preferences. However, typical reward models such as HPSv3 are trained on pre-annotated data from earlier T2I models, without accounting for quality discriminative shifts arising from evolving model capabilities and reinforcement learning (RL) iterations, limiting their broader applicability. In this work, we propose HPSv3++, a reward model framework that elevates the HPSv3 model for varying T2I model capabilities and their RL iteration changes across the full capability-iteration spectrum. Specifically, we first introduce HPDv3++, a 212K dual-dimension preference dataset annotated for text fidelity and aesthetic quality using a recent high-capability (Qwen-Image) model with human supervision. We then propose a two-stage training framework. Stage 1 employs data-aware orthogonal gradient projection to incorporate diverse aesthetic perception from HPDv3++ while preserving the original effective human preference knowledge in HPSv3. Stage 2 further leverages unlabeled data from T2I models spanning different capability levels and RL iterations, and introduces a joint capability-iterations conditioned signal for the reward model together with a standard deviation-driven unsupervised guidance mechanism, strengthening reward model across the capability-iteration spectrum. HPSv3++ achieves state-of-the-art preference prediction, outperforming HPSv3 9.8% on HPDv3, 5.5% on GenAI-Bench, while achieving 79.1%/88.1% on our proposed HPDv3++. When used for T2I RL training, it consistently improves GenEval scores across diverse T2I models, demonstrating its wide-range capabilities. The code is available at https://github.com/PlantPotatoOnMoon/HPSv3-PlusPlus.

Method: 通过物理实验，使用不同频率的可听声波共振商用摄像头，观察其内部稳定机制受扰后的成像变化，并在该条件下测试YOLO11模型的表现，评估攻击对目标检测性能的影响。

Result: 实验证明，可听范围内的低频声波可有效引发摄像头物理振动，破坏图像稳定性，导致AI模型出现显著误判、漏检及幻觉现象；特定图像和物体特征对攻击更为敏感。

Conclusion: 低频声波攻击是威胁真实世界中AI驱动视觉系统的一种可行且有效的新型物理攻击手段。理解其影响因素有助于设计更具鲁棒性的抗干扰机制。

Abstract: Artificial Intelligence (AI) is increasingly used to automate a variety of real-world computer vision (CV) applications, such as autonomous vehicle control, facial recognition, and security cameras. Recent research has shown that acoustic vibration can induce real physical motion in cameras, interfering with their internal stabilization mechanisms. Because the motion falls outside the conditions the stabilization system was designed to handle, the system introduces artifacts into the frame, causing AI-based CV models to misclassify, miss targets, or hallucinate objects.
  Previous work used ultrasonic frequencies (>20 kHz) to perform short-range attacks, which limits them to short distances due to the attenuation exhibited by high frequencies. In this work, we investigate acoustic attacks using lower frequencies in the audible range (<20 kHz), and we further expand our analysis to include how various image and object features are affected by the attacks.

Based on our results, we provide insights into several factors that make an AI CV system more vulnerable to these attacks, which could help inform the development of future mitigation strategies.

Abstract: Building trustworthy medical multimodal large language models (MLLMs) is critical for reliable clinical decision support. To enable source-level hallucination diagnosis, we introduce ClinHallu, a benchmark for stage-wise hallucination diagnosis in medical MLLM reasoning. We also use stage-replacement interventions to measure how correcting specific stages affects the final answer. Beyond evaluation, we show that trace-supervised fine-tuning reduces stage-wise hallucinations. ### [63] [Memento: Reconstruct to Remember for Consistent Long Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14667)
*Xuan Wei,Longbin Ji,Guan Wang,Xiangrui Liu,Zhenyu Zhang,Shuohuan Wang,Yu Sun,Qingqi Hong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Memento提出一种基于主体重建引导的框架，通过显式地将主体保持作为身份基础问题，解决长视频生成中重复主体的一致性问题。该方法联合训练自回归下一镜头生成与基于记忆的主体重建，利用历史记忆和全局故事描述恢复目标外观。引入双查询记忆机制以分离长程主体证据与短程线索，并采用主体感知的电影数据流水线提供精确的重建监督。实验表明，Memento在长期主体一致性、跨镜头连贯性和视觉质量方面达到当前最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有时间分解方法虽提升了生成可扩展性，但主要关注下一镜头的合理性，忽视了历史记忆是否保留关键主体信息，导致重复主体在生成过程中逐渐被稀释或遗忘。因此需要一种能够显式保障主体身份一致性的机制。

Method: Memento联合训练自回归下一镜头生成与基于记忆的主体重建任务，采用双查询记忆机制分别检索身份相关记忆和短上下文关键帧，结合全局故事描述和主体感知的数据管道实现精准监督。

Result: Memento在长期主体一致性、跨镜头连贯性及视觉质量上均优于现有方法，达到当前最佳水平。

Conclusion: Memento通过将主体保持建模为可重构的身份问题，有效缓解了长视频生成中的主体遗忘现象，显著提升了生成内容的长期一致性与连贯性。

Abstract: Long-form video generation requires recurring subjects to remain consistent across various shots, viewpoints, motions, and scene transitions. Existing temporal decomposition methods improve scalability by generating videos shot by shot. However, they mainly focus on optimizing plausible next-shot continuations without verifying whether the historical memory preserves identity-critical subject evidence. Consequently, as generation proceeds, recurring subjects may be diluted, overwritten, or forgotten. In this paper, we propose Memento, a subject-reconstruction-guided framework that treats subject preservation as an explicit identity grounding problem, based on the premise that a memory bank faithfully preserving a subject should support reconstructing that subject from memory alone. Specifically, Memento jointly trains autoregressive next-shot generation with memory-based subject reconstruction, recovering target appearances using historical memory and global story captions. To disentangle long-range subject evidence from short-range cues, Memento introduces a dual-query memory mechanism, where one query retrieves identity-relevant memory and the other selects short-context keyframes for coherent continuation. Additionally, a subject-aware cinematic data pipeline provides precise reconstruction supervision via consistent, pronoun-free subject descriptions. Experiments demonstrate that Memento achieves state-of-the-art performance in long-term subject consistency, cross-shot coherence, and visual quality.

### [64] [Gaze Heads: How VLMs Look at What They Describe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14703)
*Rohit Gandikota,David Bau*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究发现视觉语言模型（VLM）在描述图像时，会通过其语言模型骨干中的少数特定注意力头（称为“凝视头”）来跟踪当前描述的图像区域。这些凝视头可通过少量前向传播计算相关性得分识别，并在漫画条等结构化场景中实现对模型输出的精准控制。仅对前100个凝视头进行注意力掩码干预，即可在83.1%准确率下将模型引导至任意指定漫画面板，而随机头或全头干预则无效或破坏生成。该机制支持连续控制，可在生成过程中切换目标区域，且在不同模型规模（2B至32B参数）和架构中均有效，但部分冻结编码器架构无此现象。研究揭示了基于机械分析的目标干预可作为无需重训练的推理时行为调控工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解视觉语言模型如何内部完成图像描述任务，尤其是其注意力机制是否具有可解释、可操控的行为模式，是提升模型透明度与可控性的关键。现有方法难以定位具体注意力头的作用，因此亟需一种简单有效的机制识别方式，以实现对模型行为的精确干预。

Method: 利用漫画条作为受控测试环境，其中叙事顺序在空间上呈现；通过少量前向传播计算注意力头与图像区域之间的相关性，识别出一组特定的“凝视头”；采用注意力掩码干预手段，测试这些头在引导模型描述特定区域时的效果；进一步验证其在自然图像（如COCO数据集）上的泛化能力及跨模型规模与架构的稳定性。

Result: 识别出的凝视头仅占全部注意力头的不足9%，却能在单次干预下使模型准确描述目标漫画面板（83.1%准确率）；改变注意力目标可实现生成过程中的动态转移；该机制在多个模型尺寸和架构中复现，但在某些冻结编码器结构中未观察到；干预不依赖再训练，具备实用性和可扩展性。

Conclusion: 视觉语言模型通过一组特定注意力头实现对图像描述的精细控制，这些“凝视头”构成一个可解释、可操控的推理时调控杠杆。这一发现为模型可解释性与可控性提供了新范式，展示了基于机械分析的轻量级干预在多模态生成任务中的强大潜力。

Abstract: How a vision-language model internally solves the task of describing an image is far from obvious. We find that the model develops a specific mechanism for this: a small set of attention heads in its language-model backbone, which we call gaze heads, whose attention tracks the image region the model is currently describing. We find them with a simple correlation score from a few forward passes, using comic strips as a controlled testbed where narrative order is laid out spatially. These gaze heads do not just track the image tokens being described: redirecting their attention to a chosen region forces the VLM to describe that region instead. A single attention-mask intervention on the top-100 gaze heads, fewer than 9% of all heads, steers the model's answer to any chosen comic panel at 83.1% accuracy, while the same intervention on random heads fails to redirect the answer, and intervening on all heads destroys generation. The same lever also extends to continuous control: switching the gaze target mid-generation makes the model wrap up its current panel description and move to the new one within a few tokens. Beyond comics, the same intervention redirects answers to chosen regions in natural COCO images. The mechanism further recurs across model sizes from 2B to 32B parameters and across other VLM architectures, although some frozen-encoder families show no comparable head set. More broadly, this shows that targeted edits identified through mechanistic analysis can serve as practical inference-time levers for steering multimodal model behavior, without any retraining. Our code, interactive demo, and datasets are available at https://gaze.baulab.info/

</details>


### [65] [HumP-KD: A Hybrid Uncertainty-Aware Multi-Stage Progressive Knowledge Distillation Framework for Efficient Fire Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14684)
*Mohammed Arif Mainuddin,Najifa Tabassum,Omar Ibne Shahid,Riasat Khan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HumP-KD提出了一种混合不确定性感知的多阶段渐进式知识蒸馏框架，用于高效火灾分类。该方法在FlameVision和Dataset-II两个数据集上验证，通过融合Swin-Tiny、ViT-Base及其Meta-MLP集成作为教师模型，将知识蒸馏到轻量级MobileViT-S学生模型中。采用分层特征构建与渐进式蒸馏策略，提升模型在判别区域上的注意力精度，并在多种退化条件下表现出强鲁棒性。实验表明，该模型在Dataset-II上达到0.9876±0.0063的平均F1分数，显著优于未蒸馏的MobileViT-S基线（0.9537±0.0351），且参数量仅4.94M，模型大小19.01MB，推理速度达37.72 FPS，适合实时部署。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有实时火灾分类系统需兼顾高精度、低计算开销与资源受限硬件的可部署性。传统模型在性能与效率间难以平衡，尤其在复杂或退化视觉条件下表现不佳。因此，亟需一种高效、鲁棒且可部署的轻量化模型框架。

Method: 提出HumP-KD框架，包含三个核心组件：1）分层渐进式知识蒸馏（Hierarchical Progressive Knowledge Distillation），利用分层特征构建生成空间注意力掩码，引导蒸馏聚焦于判别区域；2）多阶段知识蒸馏，逐步激活三个蒸馏阶段以优化学习过程；3）基于两个异构教师模型（Swin-Tiny、ViT-Base）及其Meta-MLP集成的联合蒸馏机制，提升学生模型泛化能力。

Result: 在Dataset-II上，HumP-KD实现0.9876±0.0063的平均F1分数，显著优于基线（p=0.0195, Wilcoxon p=0.0039）。模型参数量仅4.94M，比Swin-Tiny减少5.7倍，比ViT-Base减少17.5倍，模型大小19.01MB，推理速度达37.72 CPU FPS，具备良好的实时性与部署潜力。

Conclusion: HumP-KD框架有效实现了高精度、低参数、高效率的火灾分类，在多种退化条件下保持强鲁棒性，为资源受限设备上的实时火灾检测提供了可行解决方案。

Abstract: Real-time fire classification systems require models that are simultaneously accurate, computationally efficient, and deployable on resource-constrained hardware. This work proposes \textbf{HumP-KD}, a Hybrid Uncertainty-aware Multi-stage Progressive Knowledge Distillation framework for efficient fire classification. Two datasets, FlameVision and Dataset-II, containing 8,600 and 31,309 images, are used. Various CNN and transformer baselines are applied under standard preprocessing, online augmentation, Gaussian noise and motion blur robustness conditions. The proposed HumP-KD model distills knowledge from two frozen heterogeneous transformer teachers, Swin-Tiny and ViT-Base, along with their Meta-MLP ensemble, into a lightweight MobileViT-S student via three tightly integrated components. Hierarchical Progressive Knowledge Distillation employs a Hierarchical Feature Builder. It generates a fused spatial attention mask to guide distillation toward discriminative regions selectively. Multi-Stage Knowledge Distillation progressively activates three distillation stages across training. On Dataset-II, HumP-KD achieves a mean F1 score of $0.9876 \pm 0.0063$ across 10 independent trials, significantly outperforming the MobileViT-S baseline trained without distillation ($0.9537 \pm 0.0351$), with statistical significance confirmed by both independent t-test ($p = 0.0195$) and Wilcoxon signed-rank test ($W = 1$, $p = 0.0039$). The proposed method also demonstrates strong generalization across datasets and robustness under degraded visual conditions. The student model retains only 4.94M parameters and 19.01Mb model size, representing a $5.7\times$ parameter reduction over Swin-Tiny and a $17.5\times$ reduction over ViT-Base, while achieving 37.72 CPU FPS, making it suitable for real-time deployment.

</details>

Abstract: Globally, cotton is a highly economically beneficial crop, as the textile industry heavily depends on it. This image dataset includes seven classes, six disease classes, and one healthy class, collected under various field conditions reflecting real-world challenges. Among these pretrained models, with DenseNet201, we have achieved the highest classification accuracy of 98%. To enhance the model reliability and interpretability, we have implemented different techniques and methods such as Gradient-weighted Class Activation Mapping (Grad-CAM), occlusion sensitivity analysis and adversarial training to increase the noise resistance of the model. Finally, we have developed a prototype in order to utilize the model's capabilities on real life agriculture. This paper shows the deep learning model's capabilities to classify the disease in real-life cotton disease management situations.

### [67] [Instruct-Particulate: Scaling Feed-Forward 3D Object Articulation with Kinematic Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14699)
*Ruining Li,Yuxin Yao,Matt Zhou,Chuanxia Zheng,Christian Rupprecht,Joan Lasenby,Shangzhe Wu,Andrea Vedaldi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Instruct-Particulate 是一种新模型，通过结合3D网格与目标运动学规格（如部件描述、连接关系、关节类型和可选点提示），预测对应的动作部件分割和关节运动参数。该模型利用视觉-语言模型生成的异构训练数据，实现对多样化3D对象的泛化能力，尤其在类别间和AI生成网格上表现优异，支持从真实图像中重建带动作结构的3D资产。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经网络在估计3D对象的关节结构时受限于标注数据稀缺，导致泛化能力差。为解决此问题，需一种能利用更丰富、异构数据并灵活适应不同标注粒度的方法。

Method: 引入基于运动学规格的输入方式，将部件描述、连接性、关节类型和点提示作为条件输入；利用视觉-语言模型自动标注大量非标准3D模型，构建超过15万条的异构训练数据集；采用端到端神经网络架构进行部件分割与关节参数预测。

Result: 模型在跨类别和面对AI生成网格时表现出更强的泛化能力；可在无需人工标注的情况下，通过图像到3D模型流程实现真实世界图像中的带动作结构3D资产重建。

Conclusion: Instruct-Particulate 有效缓解了标注数据稀缺带来的限制，通过融合视觉-语言模型与异构数据训练，显著提升了3D关节结构重建的通用性与实用性，为动画、游戏和机器人仿真提供了高效解决方案。

Abstract: Reconstructing articulated 3D objects is important for animation, gaming, and robotic simulations. Recent neural networks can estimate the articulated structure of 3D objects, but their generalization remains limited by the scarcity of annotated data for this task. To address this gap, we introduce Instruct-Particulate, a model that takes a 3D mesh together with a target kinematic specification, including part descriptions, connectivity, joint types, and optional point prompts, and predicts the corresponding kinematic part segmentation and joint motion parameters. The kinematic specification disambiguates the task and allows the model to target annotations of different granularity, thereby making it possible to use more abundant heterogeneous training data. At test time, the kinematic specification can be obtained automatically from large-scale vision-language models, so the model can be applied to any input mesh. To train our model at scale, we construct a heterogeneous dataset of more than 150,000 articulated 3D objects, extending existing publicly available collections with data obtained by partially labelling other 3D models (monolithic or already decomposed into parts) with kinematic labels by means of vision-language models. Experiments show that our model generalizes better across categories and to AI-generated meshes, enabling articulated asset reconstruction from real-world images via image-to-3D models.

### [68] [RepFusion: Leveraging Multimodal Priors for Denoising in Representation Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14700)
*Xichen Pan,Aashu Singh,Satya Narayan Shukla,Xiangjun Fan,Shlok Kumar Mishra,Saining Xie*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RepFusion leverages multimodal LLMs (MLLMs) as noisy representation encoders to condition a diffusion transformer in text-to-image generation, outperforming baselines with dedicated denoisers at similar compute budgets by utilizing MLLMs' strong priors for denoising visual representations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing text-to-image systems rely on pretrained language models for text encoding but use newly trained generative backbones for denoising, limiting integration. Representation autoencoders enable semantically structured latent spaces compatible with LLM priors, motivating the use of MLLMs to extend this alignment from clean to noisy inputs.

Method: RepFusion repurposes an MLLM as a noisy representation encoder, using its outputs as conditioning signals for a diffusion transformer. This enables iterative, test-time conditioning on evolving noisy representations, leveraging MLLM priors for improved denoising.

Result: In controlled experiments with comparable inference budgets, RepFusion surpasses state-of-the-art baselines that employ newly initialized denoisers, demonstrating that MLLMs provide powerful priors and that repeated MLLM conditioning effectively utilizes test-time compute.

Conclusion: MLLMs serve as effective denoising priors when conditioned on evolving noisy representations, enabling more efficient and high-quality text-to-image generation in modern systems through strategic use of test-time computation.

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are widely used in text-to-image (T2I) systems, but they are typically limited to text encoding, while denoising is handled by newly trained generative backbones. The emergence of representation autoencoders (RAEs) shifts the generation target toward semantically structured visual representations, creating a latent space that is more compatible with pretrained LLM priors. Inspired by multimodal LLMs (MLLMs), where an MLP projector is sufficient to align clean visual representations with a pretrained LLM, we repurpose the MLLM itself as a noisy representation encoder, extending this mechanism from clean to noisy inputs. We present RepFusion, which uses the resulting MLLM outputs as the conditioning signal for a diffusion transformer. In controlled comparisons at similar inference budgets, RepFusion outperforms baselines that devote comparable capacity to newly initialized denoisers. These results demonstrate that MLLMs provide strong priors for denoising visual representations and that, by conditioning on evolving noisy representations, test-time compute can be productively spent on repeated MLLM conditioning in modern T2I systems.

### [69] [RATS! Patches Talk Through Registers: Emergent Parts in Register Attention Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14701)
*Timing Yang,Predrag Neskovic,Jansen Seheult,Wenchao Han,Anand Bhattad,Alan Yuille,Feng Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: RATS (Register Attention Transformers) is a self-supervised visual model that discovers compositional structure in images by decomposing the classification token into learnable register tokens. These registers specialize into proto-semantic regions resembling object parts without part annotations or auxiliary losses, achieving superior performance on segmentation benchmarks and demonstrating part-level consistency across categories.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To determine whether self-supervised models can autonomously discover compositional structures similar to how humans recognize objects through reusable parts like heads, wings, and talons.

Method: RATS uses a three-step compress-communicate-broadcast attention mechanism via N learnable register tokens partitioned across H attention heads, enabling non-interacting specialization into proto-semantic regions.

Result: RATS outperforms all baselines by +12 mIoU on average across five segmentation benchmarks, with notable gains on ADE20K (+1.11 mIoU) and COCO (+0.2 AP^m), and shows part-level consistency and semantic proximity across categories.

Conclusion: RATS demonstrates the potential of architectural design in enabling structured, interpretable visual representation learning by allowing models to spontaneously discover object parts through self-supervision.

Abstract: When humans see a bird, they recognize far more than just "bird" -- they see a head, wings, and talons, a structured assembly of reusable parts that can be identified across every bird they have ever seen. We ask whether a self-supervised visual model can discover the same compositional structure on its own. To this end, we propose RATS (Register Attention Transformers), which decomposes the classification token into N learnable register tokens that route patch information through an L->N->N->L bottleneck via a three-step compress-communicate-broadcast attention. The N registers are partitioned across the H attention heads, so that registers assigned to different heads do not interact with each other. Without auxiliary losses or part annotations, each register spontaneously specializes into a proto-semantic region whose emerging structure resembles object parts. RATS surpasses all baselines by +12 mIoU on average across five segmentation benchmarks, with consistent gains on ADE20K (+1.11 mIoU) and COCO (+0.2 AP^m). Its register dictionary further exhibits part-level consistency and semantic proximity across related categories. Our results suggest that RATS may provide a useful architectural prior for structured and interpretable visual representation learning.

</details>


### [70] [OmniVideo-100K: A Dataset for Audio-Visual Reasoning through Structured Scripts and Evidence Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14702)
*Xinyue Cai,Chaoyou Fu,Yi-Fan Zhang,Ran He,Caifeng Shan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新型自动化数据引擎，解决现有音频-视觉问答（QA）管道中视频片段化处理导致的音视频关联断裂与跨片段实体不一致问题。通过两项机制：(1) 实体锚定视频脚本（Entity-Anchored Video Scripting），将视频转化为包含摘要、核心实体列表和分段音视频描述的结构化脚本，以全局实体先验保障一致性并重建音视频关联；(2) 线索引导的QA生成（Clue-Guided QA Generation），引导模型从脚本中挖掘跨片段多模态线索，再基于高价值线索生成问答对。基于此构建了指令微调数据集OmniVideo-100K与人工验证测试集OmniVideo-Test，对VITA-1.5、Qwen2.5-Omni-7B和Qwen3-Omni-30B进行微调后，在OmniVideo-Test上性能提升最高达20.59%，在Daily-Omni和JointAVBench等基准上也表现出显著泛化能力（最高提升12.64%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有音频-视觉问答方法采用'视频-字幕-QA'范式，将视频分割为短片段并分别生成音视频描述，导致音视频间固有关联被切断，同一实体在不同片段中描述不一致；同时，将长文本理解与问答合成一步完成，限制模型仅关注局部事件，难以生成具有长期时序联系和深层跨模态推理的复杂问题。

Method: 提出两个核心机制：(1) 实体锚定视频脚本，将视频转化为结构化脚本，包含摘要、主要实体列表及分段音视频描述，利用实体列表作为全局先验确保跨片段一致性并重建音视频关联；(2) 线索引导的QA生成，先从脚本中挖掘跨片段多模态线索，再基于这些线索生成高质量问答对。

Result: 构建了指令微调数据集OmniVideo-100K和人工验证测试集OmniVideo-Test；在多个主流基准（如Daily-Omni、JointAVBench）上，使用该数据集微调的模型（VITA-1.5、Qwen2.5-Omni-7B、Qwen3-Omni-30B）性能提升显著，最高达20.59%（在OmniVideo-Test上），且在跨任务泛化能力上提升最高达12.64%。

Conclusion: 所提出的自动化数据引擎有效缓解了音视频关联断裂与跨片段不一致问题，通过结构化脚本与线索引导机制增强了模型对长期时序关系和深层跨模态推理的理解能力，显著提升了音频-视觉问答系统的性能与泛化性。

Abstract: Current automated pipelines for audio-visual Question Answering (QA) generally adopt a ``video-caption-QA'' paradigm. However, these methods typically segment videos into short clips and generate separate descriptions for audio and visual modalities. This decoupled processing severs inherent associations between sounds and their visual sources, while independent clip processing often causes inconsistent descriptions of the same entity across segments. Furthermore, coupling long-text comprehension and QA synthesis into a single step often restricts models to localized events, yielding questions lacking long-term temporal connections and deep cross-modal reasoning. To address these issues, we propose an automated data engine featuring two mechanisms: (1) \textbf{Entity-Anchored Video Scripting} transforms videos into structured scripts, comprising summaries, main entity lists, and segment-wise audio-visual descriptions. The entity list serves as a global prior to ensure cross-segment referential consistency and reconstruct audio-visual associations. (2) \textbf{Clue-Guided QA Generation} prompts models to first mine cross-segment, multimodal clues from the script, and subsequently generate QA pairs based on these high-value clues. Leveraging this pipeline, we construct the instruction-tuning dataset \textbf{OmniVideo-100K} and a human-verified test set, \textbf{OmniVideo-Test}. Fine-tuning VITA-1.5, Qwen2.5-Omni-7B and Qwen3-Omni-30B on OmniVideo-100K yields performance gains of up to 20.59% on OmniVideo-Test, demonstrating strong generalization (up to 12.64% improvements) across established benchmarks like Daily-Omni and JointAVBench.

### [71] [The Coin Flip Judge? Reliability and Bias in LLM-as-a-Judge Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13685)
*Abel Yagubyan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了LLM作为裁判在重复评估中的可靠性问题，发现即使在相同任务下，不同运行间的结果存在显著波动。使用GPT-4o-mini和GPT-4.1-mini进行29个任务的50次成对与点对点评估，结果显示成对偏好平均有13.6%的翻转率，部分问题甚至高达56%；点对点得分差距小且不显著，表明判断结果常基于微弱差异。跨模型一致性仅76%（κ=0.51），提示需多轮投票、随机化位置并报告不确定性。单次评估噪声过大，不适合高风险场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM-as-a-Judge被广泛用于模型输出排序、奖励模型训练及排行榜构建，但其评估结果的稳定性尚未充分研究，尤其在重复运行中是否存在不一致尚不清楚。

Method: 在29个涵盖10类任务的数据集上，使用两个OpenAI提供的裁判模型（GPT-4o-mini和GPT-4.1-mini）进行50次成对与50次点对点评估，并辅以温度和提示敏感性分析。通过多次重复实验、多数投票、可靠性曲线分析等方法评估一致性与稳定性。

Result: 成对偏好平均13.6%翻转，28%的问题翻转率超过20%，最高达56%；点对点得分差异小且不显著，存在明显的第一名偏差（72%偏向A项，p=0.024）；跨模型一致性仅为76%（κ=0.51），语义等价提示模板改变结果的比例达25%；即使采用确定性解码，仍存在不一致；平均需11次重复才能以95%概率恢复参考结论，高方差问题则需15次。

Conclusion: 单次LLM评估结果过于嘈杂，不适合高风险评价；应推广多轮聚合、位置随机化和显式不确定性报告。由于两模型均来自同一提供商，跨供应商复制验证是未来关键方向。

Abstract: LLM-as-a-Judge is now widely used to rank model outputs, train reward models, and populate public leaderboards, but its run-to-run reliability remains under-characterized. We study repeated identical evaluations on 29 tasks spanning 10 categories using two OpenAI judge models (GPT-4o-mini and GPT-4.1-mini), with 50 pairwise trials and 50 pointwise trials per question, supplemented by temperature and prompt-sensitivity ablations. Across judges, pairwise preferences flip on average 13.6% of the time, with 28% of questions exceeding a 20% flip rate and one question reaching 56%. GPT-4o-mini also exhibits a significant first-position bias (72% A-majority, p = 0.024). At the same time, mean pointwise score gaps are small (0.19--0.36 on a 10-point scale) and not statistically significant in aggregate, producing a pairwise--pointwise gap: judges frequently choose a winner even when their own scalar scores provide little evidence of a meaningful quality difference. Beyond within-judge instability, cross-judge agreement is only 76% ($κ= 0.51$), semantically equivalent prompt templates change majority outcomes in 25% of tested cases, and deterministic decoding reduces but does not eliminate inconsistency. A reliability curve analysis shows that, in our dataset, 11 repeated trials are needed for a majority vote to recover the 50-trial reference verdict with 95% probability on average, rising to 15 for high-variance questions. These findings suggest that single-trial LLM judging is often too noisy for high-stakes evaluation, and that multi-trial aggregation, position randomization, and explicit uncertainty reporting should be standard practice. Because both judges are from a single provider, cross-provider replication remains an important next step.

</details>


### [72] [Benchmarking Web Agent Safety under E-commerce Deceptive Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13686)
*Zijing Shi,Meng Fang,Ling Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在电商领域中，自主网络代理在面对现实世界欺骗性界面时的安全性问题。提出了一种名为WebDecept的轻量级、可配置的插件框架，用于在现有网页环境中可控地注入欺骗性界面模式。通过在任务执行过程中注入七种常见的欺骗模式（如定向广告、域名重定向和购物操纵），对多个多模态网络代理进行了受控评估。结果显示，当前网络代理对多种欺骗性界面极为敏感，且基于提示的约束往往无法有效缓解这些问题。研究还分析了欺骗性设计选择如何影响操纵的成功率。这些发现揭示了在将网络代理扩展到真实世界部署时需解决的安全挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着自主网络代理在现实世界任务中的广泛应用，其安全性成为一个关键问题。特别是，在电商领域中，欺骗性界面的存在可能严重威胁代理的正确行为，因此需要系统性研究其影响并提出有效的防御机制。

Method: 提出并实现WebDecept框架，用于在网页前端动态注入七类常见欺骗性界面模式（如定向广告、域名重定向、购物操纵等），并在真实任务场景下对多个多模态网络代理进行受控测试与评估。

Result: 实验表明，当前主流网络代理对多种欺骗性界面高度脆弱，即使使用基于提示的约束也难以有效防范。不同欺骗性设计特征显著影响攻击成功率，揭示出潜在的系统性安全漏洞。

Conclusion: 本研究强调了在真实世界部署网络代理前必须重视其对欺骗性界面的鲁棒性。未来工作应聚焦于增强代理的感知、推理与防御能力，以应对日益复杂的在线欺骗行为。

Abstract: As autonomous web agents are increasingly deployed to perform real-world tasks, ensuring their safety has become a critical concern. In this work, we study web agent behavior under realistic deceptive interfaces in the e-commerce domain. We introduce WebDecept, a lightweight and configurable plugin framework that enables controlled injection of deceptive interface patterns into existing web environments. Using WebDecept, we instantiate seven deceptive patterns commonly observed on the open web, including targeted advertisements, domain redirection, and shopping manipulation. By injecting these patterns into the frontend during task execution, we perform controlled evaluation of multiple multimodal web agents. Our results show that current web agents are highly susceptible to multiple classes of deceptive interfaces, and that prompt-based constraints are often insufficient to mitigate these failures. We further analyze how the design choices of deceptive patterns influence the success of such manipulations. These findings highlight safety challenges that should be addressed as web agents are scaled toward real-world deployment.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建多维度文化标签框架，对预训练、微调、对齐和推理阶段的数据进行标注，量化文化信号的分布与衰减情况，并评估文化标记对下游任务的影响。

Abstract: Current cultural alignment approaches focus on inference-time interventions, assuming models already contain sufficient cultural knowledge. We argue modern LLM pipelines suffer from a cultural data funnel. Using a multidimensional tagging framework across pretraining, fine-tuning, alignment, and reasoning datasets, we show explicit cultural signals decline sharply during post-training, while geographically concentrated, task-specialized data dominates. Multilinguality enhances geographic diversity of cultural knowledge but does not ensure balanced representation. Our tags improve downstream cultural benchmark performance, demonstrating that advances require shifting focus in training data pipelines. To facilitate future research, we release our culturally tagged dataset with 5.6M samples at https://huggingface.co/datasets/CohereLabs/CultureMarkers.

### [76] [When Plausible Is Not Realistic: Evaluating Human Mobility in LLM-Based Urban Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13835)
*Gustavo H. Santos,Aline Carneiro Viana,Thiago H. Silva*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种评估基于大语言模型（LLM）的城市模拟器中生成代理移动行为真实性的框架，通过对比真实世界数据中的移动规律、时间节奏、网络模式、语义活动转换和行为移动特征，发现现有模拟器在叙事合理性与实际移动模式之间存在显著差距。尽管能捕捉部分高层次的活动分布，但在行程长度、起讫点流量、停留时间及转换动态等核心时空约束方面表现不佳。研究还指出，真实的移动多样性在默认提示设置下不稳定，可能需要显式的个性化初始化。此外，作者提供了可扩展、开源的基础设施支持区域级地图生成、可观测性增强的模拟、移动指标计算和交通模拟，以促进可复现的评估。

Method: 构建了一个多维度验证框架，涵盖移动定律、时间节奏、网络拓扑结构、语义活动转换以及个体行为移动特征；利用巴黎大区与上海的真实移动数据集，对AgentSociety和CitySim两个典型城市模拟器进行多角度评估；同时开发了支持区域规模地图生成、可观测性增强模拟、移动指标计算与交通模拟的开放工具链。

Result: 实证分析表明，尽管生成代理在高层语义活动中表现出一定相似性，但在关键空间-时间特性上如行程长度分布、OD流动、停留时间和转换动态等方面明显偏离真实数据。此外，移动多样性在不同提示配置下波动较大，缺乏稳定性，暗示需要引入个体行为特征初始化机制。

Conclusion: 基于大语言模型的城市模拟器虽具备生成合理叙事的能力，但其移动行为尚未达到经验真实性水平。必须加强基于真实数据的严格验证，并建议采用个性化的初始化策略与开放可复现的评估工具，以推动更真实、可靠的都市模拟系统发展。

Abstract: LLM-based generative agents are increasingly used in urban simulators, yet it remains unclear whether they reproduce empirically realistic human mobility patterns or merely generate plausible mobility narratives. Our analysis reveals a substantial gap between narrative plausibility and empirical mobility realism. Although the simulators capture some high-level semantic activity distributions, they struggle to reproduce core spatial and temporal constraints, including realistic trip-length distributions, origin-destination flows, dwell times, and transition dynamics. We further observe that realistic mobility diversity is unstable across default prompting configurations and may require explicit profile-aware initialization. To support reproducible evaluation, we also contribute scalable and open LLM-driven infrastructure for regional-scale map generation, observability-enhanced simulation, mobility-metric computation, and traffic simulation. Our findings highlight the need for rigorous empirical validation of LLM-based urban simulators and provide practical tools for building more realistic and reproducible urban simulation systems.

### [77] [Hybrid Classical-Quantum Variational Autoencoder for Neural Topic Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13852)
*Ivan Kankeu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种混合经典-量子变分自编码器（VAE）用于主题建模，将参数化量子电路嵌入到VAE的推断网络中，同时保留经典的主题-词解码器。为应对量子硬件资源限制，提出了改进的高斯Softmax后验分布，解耦了潜在空间维度与主题数量，使模型能在10量子比特的低资源设备上运行。在AgNews数据集上，该混合模型优于现有神经主题模型（NTMs），达到C_v一致性得分0.71和NPMI得分0.20，同时保持高主题多样性。此外，构建的全经典版本也表现优异，且在潜在空间中表现出清晰的类别分离。结果表明，即使在当前的NISQ时代设备上，混合VAE也具有计算可行性，是量子增强主题建模的有前景方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索神经主题模型与量子硬件的结合，解决现有模型在量子计算资源受限条件下的应用难题，推动量子增强主题建模的发展。

Method: 提出一种混合经典-量子变分自编码器（VAE），在推断网络中嵌入参数化量子电路，使用改进的高斯Softmax后验分布以降低对量子资源的需求，并保留经典主题-词解码器。

Result: 在AgNews数据集上，混合量子-经典VAE模型在C_v一致性得分（0.71）和NPMI得分（0.20）方面优于现有神经主题模型，且保持高主题多样性；全经典版本同样表现优异，具备良好的类别分离能力。

Conclusion: 混合经典-量子变分自编码器在当前NISQ设备上具有计算可行性，展示了量子增强主题建模的巨大潜力，是未来研究的重要方向。

Abstract: Neural topic models enable scalable semantic discovery, but their integration with quantum hardware remains largely unexplored. We present a proof-of-concept hybrid classical-quantum variational autoencoder (VAE) for topic modeling, embedding parameterized quantum circuits within the VAE inference network while retaining a classical topic-word decoder. To address the resource constraints of quantum hardware, we propose a modified Gaussian Softmax posterior that decouples latent space dimensionality from the number of topics to be extracted, enabling the model to operate with a low-resource 10-qubit quantum device. On the AgNews dataset, the hybrid VAE outperforms state-of-the-art neural topic models (NTMs), reaching a $C_v$ coherence score of 0.71 and an NPMI score of 0.20 while preserving high topic diversity. For comparison, we also construct a fully classical variant, which also outperforms state-of-the-art models on AgNews and exhibits clear class separation in the latent space. These results demonstrate that hybrid VAEs are computationally viable even on NISQ-era devices and represent a promising direction for quantum-enhanced topic modeling.

### [78] [SANA: What Matters for QA Agents over Massive Data Lakes?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13904)
*Austin Senna Wijaya,Jiaxiang Liu,Haonan Wang,Eugene Wu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SANA是一个诊断性消融框架，用于分析探索式问答（EQA）中数据湖代理在搜索、规划、数据分析和行动策略等环节的失败原因。通过将EQA任务转化为包含理想化组件的运行时轨迹，SANA能够隔离各模块的表现，揭示政策决策缺陷。在LakeQA和KramaBench两个基准上的实验表明，数据分析是普遍瓶颈，搜索在大规模数据湖中尤为关键，而规划相对稳定。该框架实现了对代理性能的系统性诊断与比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有端到端准确率无法区分探索式问答中搜索、规划、数据分析或行动策略等环节的失败，缺乏对具体故障环节的诊断能力。需要一种可复用的评估框架来识别数据湖代理在复杂任务中的薄弱环节。

Method: 提出SANA框架，将EQA任务转化为包含黄金源序列、净化子问题和执行记录的运行时轨迹；构建理想化的搜索、规划和数据分析工具，通过逐项消融各组件，以残差差距作为诊断依据，定位策略失败点。

Result: 在LakeQA和KramaBench上验证，数据分析是持续瓶颈，搜索在大规模数据湖中构成主要限制，规划影响较小；SANA成功分解端到端准确率，实现对各组件性能的精准诊断与系统比较。

Conclusion: SANA提供了一种可复用的诊断评估框架，能够有效识别数据湖探索式问答中代理的性能瓶颈，推动对搜索、规划、数据分析及代理设计的针对性改进。

Abstract: Exploratory question answering (EQA) over data lakes requires an LLM agent to discover relevant sources, analyze retrieved data, and adapt its actions based on intermediate results. End-to-end accuracy alone cannot distinguish failures in search, planning, data analysis, or the agent's Action Policy: its decisions about what to do next and when to submit an answer. We present SANA (Search Agent Navigation Ablation framework), a diagnostic ablation framework that transforms EQA tasks into runtime profiles containing gold source sequence, sanitized subquestions, and execution records. SANA uses these profiles to construct idealized search, planning, and data-analysis tools, allowing each component to be ablated; the residual gap is diagnostic evidence for policy failures.
  To illustrate SANA as a reusable evaluation framework, we adapted two recent EQA benchmarks, LakeQA and KramaBench, and evaluated lightweight and mid-sized agents under fixed prompts, budgets, data lakes, and runtimes. Across both benchmarks, data analysis is a consistent bottleneck while planning is less so. Search is a major limitation in LakeQA's large data-lake setting, but less so for the smaller-scale KramaBench. SANA thus deconstructs end-to-end task accuracies into a diagnosis of where data-lake agents fail, and allows for systematic comparisons of progress in search, planning, data analysis, and agent design.

### [79] [DLawBench: Evaluating LLMs Through Multi-Turn Legal Consultation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13931)
*Li Zhang,Yuzhen Shi,Yiran Hu,Jingwen Zhang,Wenbo Lv,Yubo Ma,Wei Wang,Rongyao Shi,Yuanyang Qiu,Xinran Xu,Yuemeng Qi,Linlin Miao,Jaromir Savelka,Yun Liu,Kevin Ashley,Bing Zhao,Hu Wei,Lin Qu*

TL;DR: 提出DLawBench，一个用于评估大语言模型在真实法律咨询场景中交互能力的诊断基准，涵盖四种客户类型（合作型、依赖型、退缩型、对抗型），基于中美真实案例数据，评估26个代表性LLM在多轮对话中的法律推理与事实获取能力。实验显示最佳模型表现仅0.562，且存在对客户引导需求越强时表现反而越差的悖论，揭示现有模型在真实互动中的局限性。

Method: 构建基于真实案例的对话数据集，将律师-客户互动分为四类典型模式，设计包含事实提取、问题引导与问题解决三类评估标准，系统评测26个主流大语言模型在复杂交互场景下的表现。

Abstract: Lawyer-client consultation is a critical starting point for legal services. Effective legal assistance hinges on eliciting sufficient and truthful information from clients in order to devise strategies that best protect their interests. This task requires Large Language Models (LLMs) not only to perform robust legal reasoning, but also to strategically elicit material facts through multi-turn interactions and effectively guide clients with diverse personalities. Yet existing legal benchmarks overlook this interactive capability. To fill this gap, we introduce DLawBench, a diagnostic benchmark for real-world legal consultation. Drawing on realistic client behavior, we characterize lawyer-client interactions into four types: Cooperative, Dependent, Withdrawn, and Adversarial. Using dialogues grounded in real cases, DLawBench evaluates whether LLMs can effectively conduct legal consultation under realistic conditions. DLawBench comprises 461 cases from Chinese and U.S. law, 5,532 paired fact entries, 3,411 inquiry rubrics, and 3,348 issue-resolution rubrics, and evaluates 26 representative LLMs. Systematic experiments show substantial headroom: the best-performing model, GPT-5.5, achieves only 0.562 on consultation-grounded legal reasoning. More importantly, DLawBench exposes both sycophancy in legal consultation and a paradox: models perform worse when clients need guidance most.

### [80] [Can Post-Training Turn LLMs into Good Medical Coders? An Empirical Study of Generative ICD Coding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13940)
*Ziqing Wang,Weihao Li,Shijie Chen,Yuan Luo,Kaize Ding*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过受控实验评估了生成式大语言模型（LLM）在国际疾病分类（ICD）编码任务中的表现，比较了提示、监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（GRPO）等不同后训练方法。研究发现，仅靠提示的评估会严重低估LLM的潜力；SFT带来显著性能提升，GRPO进一步改善代码集预测能力，而提出的PHI诊断课程在宏观层面实现针对性优化。结果表明，模型适应与优化方式是影响全税目召回率的关键瓶颈，而非生成式范式本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多基于推理阶段的提示、检索或工具使用评估生成式LLM在ICD编码中的表现，忽视了任务特定后训练的作用。因此亟需系统性地探索后训练对生成式模型编码能力的影响，以揭示其真实潜力。

Method: 采用统一协议与指标集，对比判别基线与生成式LLM在提示、监督微调（SFT）及强化学习（GRPO）下的表现；提出一种名为PHI的诊断课程，扩展GRPO以优化漏码案例。

Result: 提示法显著低估了LLM潜力；SFT带来主要性能跃升，GRPO在代码集预测上优于SFT，PHI在宏观性能上提供额外增益。

Conclusion: 生成式模型在ICD编码中的主要瓶颈并非其形式本身，而是如何通过后训练进行适配与优化以实现全税目召回。合理设计后训练策略可极大释放其潜力。

Abstract: Automated International Classification of Diseases (ICD) coding is a core medical-coding task for billing, epidemiology, and clinical decision support. Generative large language models (LLMs) are often reported as weak medical coders, but this finding mainly comes from inference-time settings such as prompting, retrieval, reranking, or tool use, leaving the role of task-specific post-training underexplored. We present a controlled empirical study of post-training for generative ICD coding, comparing discriminative baselines with LLM coders across prompting, supervised fine-tuning, and reinforcement learning under a common protocol and metric set. To our knowledge, this is the first study to evaluate RL-based post-training for generative LLM coders in ICD coding. We further introduce PHI, a diagnostic curriculum that extends GRPO to refine missed-code cases. Our results show that prompting-only evaluation substantially underestimates the potential of LLMs for ICD coding. SFT provides the main capability jump, GRPO further improves code-set prediction beyond SFT, and PHI provides targeted gains on macro-level performance. These findings suggest that the main bottleneck is not the generative formulation alone, but how the model is adapted and optimized for full-taxonomy recall. We release our code, data splits, and checkpoints at https://github.com/AlexandreWANG915/LLM4ICD.

### [81] [LLMs Contain Multitudes: How Deployment Context Reshapes Model-Level Preferences and Values](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13944)
*Filip Trhlik,Aoife O'Flynn,Angela Yu,Arduin Findeis,Paula Buttery*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了大语言模型（LLMs）在不同任务上下文中的偏好和价值判断是否稳定。通过改变部署上下文（如撰写Reddit帖子或新闻稿），发现模型的偏好和效用评估结果显著变化，远超语法扰动或温度控制的影响。在15个国家的排名中，上下文导致显著的排名变动，全球北方偏见也随上下文变化；在50个结果的效用评估中，虽然整体类别顺序保持，但细粒度排名和跨结果的交换率（如一个地区生命价值等同于另一个地区的数量）中位数变化达2.47倍。因此，模型的偏好和效用并非固定属性，而是依赖于上下文的条件性测量，现有安全保证在不同语境下可能不成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对大语言模型的评估多认为其具有稳定的模型级偏好和价值系统，但这些评估通常仅基于轻微的提示扰动（如语法变化或选项重排），未充分考察真实部署中任务上下文变化的影响。本文旨在检验模型偏好是否在不同上下文中保持一致，以揭示其实际稳定性与可靠性。

Method: 采用两个成熟的成对评估范式：国家偏好排序与效用判断。通过系统性地改变模型的部署上下文（如写作场景为Reddit帖子或新闻文章），在五种主流大语言模型上进行超过120万次成对决策测试，分析上下文对偏好和效用结果的影响，并与提示重述和温度调节进行对比。

Result: 在15个国家的偏好排序中，上下文变化导致显著且统计显著的排名变动，模型的全球北方偏见是上下文依赖的，各模型的偏见随上下文系统性变化；在50个结果的效用评估中，整体类别顺序基本保留，但细粒度排名差异大，跨类别的效用交换率中位数变化达2.47倍。

Conclusion: 大语言模型的偏好和效用并非固定的模型属性，而是高度依赖于部署上下文的条件性测量。因此，基于特定语境得出的安全性或价值判断无法普遍推广，需重新审视模型评估与安全保障的框架。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly characterised in recent evaluation work as having stable, model-level preference and value systems. However, accompanying robustness checks are limited to incidental prompt perturbations such as syntax variation and option reordering. This leaves open whether the measured properties survive when the surrounding task context changes, as it does in most real deployments. We test this directly across two established pairwise paradigms: ranking country preferences and eliciting utility judgements. In both, we make the deployment context -- the high-level task the model is performing while making concrete value-dependent choices -- our controlled variable, varied across framings such as writing a Reddit post or a news article. Across five LLMs and over 1.2M pairwise decisions, deployment context produces variation far larger than prompt paraphrasing and temperature controls. In country preference rankings over 15 countries, context induces widespread, statistically significant rank shifts; the aggregate Global North favouritism reported in prior work is itself context-dependent, with each model's bias shifting systematically across contexts. In utility elicitation over 50 outcomes, broad cross-category ordering is preserved, but fine-grained rankings within domains vary substantially, and cardinal exchange rates between outcomes (e.g. how many lives in one region equal one in another) shift by a factor of 2.47 at the median. Reported model-level preferences and utilities are therefore better understood as context-conditioned measurements than fixed model-level properties: safety guarantees obtained under one framing provide limited assurance in another.

</details>


### [82] [MedLatentDx: Latent Multi-Agent Communication for Cross-Hospital Rare-Disease Diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13945)
*Ziqing Wang,Lili Zhao,Kaize Ding*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MedLatentDx 是一种用于罕见病诊断的隐状态多代理通信框架，通过在医院间传递紧凑的隐状态键值块（KV blocks）实现跨机构协作，同时保护患者隐私。该框架支持同构与异构大模型后端，并在 CrossRare-Bench 基准上验证了其在提升诊断性能和降低临床信息可重构性方面的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 罕见病患者众多但单个医院病例稀少，难以进行可靠诊断；现有医疗代理系统依赖文本交换，但受限于隐私法规，无法直接共享临床文本；而原始隐状态仍可能泄露敏感内容，因此需要一种既能促进跨机构协作又可保护隐私的新型通信机制。

Method: MedLatentDx 采用隐状态键值块（KV blocks）作为通信媒介，医院代理本地保存临床记录和检索到的病例，仅向主代理发送压缩后的隐状态信息；针对同构模型使用隐状态蒸馏，针对异构模型采用跨家族隐状态对齐技术，以实现高效且安全的信息传递。

Result: 在 CrossRare-Bench 基准测试中，MedLatentDx 显著提升了跨医院罕见病诊断的准确性，同时相比原始隐状态通信基线，显著降低了临床内容被重建的风险，证明了其在性能与隐私保护之间的良好平衡。

Conclusion: MedLatentDx 为跨机构罕见病诊断提供了一种高效、安全的解决方案，能够在不暴露原始临床文本或可逆隐状态的前提下，实现高质量的协作诊断，具有重要的临床应用前景。

Abstract: Rare diseases affect over $300$ million patients across more than $7{,}000$ conditions, yet no single hospital encounters enough cases of any one condition for reliable diagnosis. Cross-hospital collaboration could help by allowing a diagnosing institution to use distributed, case-specific diagnostic evidence, but privacy regulations restrict the transmission of identifiable clinical text across institutional boundaries. This setting raises two challenges: existing medical agent systems often rely on textual evidence exchange, while raw latent states such as hidden states and KV caches may still reveal prompt-derived clinical content. We introduce MedLatentDx, a latent multi-agent communication framework in which hospital agents keep private clinical records and retrieved cases local, and send compact latent KV blocks to a host agent for rare-disease diagnosis. MedLatentDx supports two deployment settings: same-backbone hospital agents use latent KV distillation, while hospitals with different LLM backbones use cross-family latent alignment. On CrossRare-Bench, a self-built large-scale rare-disease benchmark with hospital-level partitions, MedLatentDx improves cross-hospital diagnostic performance while reducing reconstructable clinical content relative to raw-latent communication baselines.

### [83] [Creative Integration: A Decidable Criterion of Creativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13977)
*Yoshinori Nomura*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一个可操作的创造性整合（CI）判定标准：当且仅当在固定描述语言下，描述长度严格缩短（C = L_pre/L_post > 1），且压缩效应集中于冲突本身时，A与B之间的真正整合才成立。通过四个合取二元门实现判断的可判定性，并借助伪整合分类体系排除伪装者。基于多领域语料库验证，通过四项可证伪测试（独立计算检验、硬负样本区分、跨样本预测、描述语言鲁棒性）均获成功。贡献不在于‘创造力即压缩’这一观点，而在于其可判定性、可区分性与实证支持；真正的创造性在于压缩冲突，新颖性与价值是其衍生结果。本文仅提供判别工具，不生成创意，为更广泛研究提供可引用的基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对‘整合’的讨论多流于空泛，缺乏可操作的标准以区分真正的创造性整合与表面整洁的重新描述。本文旨在建立一个能明确识别真实整合的准则，解决“何为真正整合”的模糊性问题。

Method: 基于创造力与智能等同于压缩的理论脉络，提出以描述长度缩减为核心指标的判定标准。通过四重合取二元门实现判断的可计算性，并构建伪整合类型学以排除假阳性。采用多领域语料库进行实证验证，通过四项可证伪测试评估其有效性。

Result: 四项关键测试全部通过，表明该标准具有良好的计算可执行性、区分能力、外推能力和语言无关性。证明了该标准在实际应用中的稳健性和可靠性。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一个可判定、可区分、可验证的创造性整合判定框架，其核心是描述长度在冲突处的实质性压缩。真正的创造性并非仅表现为新颖，而是通过压缩冲突体现，该标准可作为未来研究的可引用基础。

Abstract: "Integrative" solutions are widely praised but rarely defined: we lack an operational way to tell a genuine integration -- one that makes the world cheaper to describe -- from a tidy re-description. Building on the lineage that
  treats creativity and intelligence as compression, we give such a criterion for creative integration (CI): the resolution of a real conflict between A and B is CI if and only if, under a fixed description language, the description
  length strictly shrinks (C = L_pre/L_post > 1), with the reduction located in the conflict itself. We make the judgment decidable through four binary, conjunctive gates, and we fix its extension through a taxonomy of
  pseudo-integration that names and rejects the look-alikes. We back the criterion with a curated, multi-domain corpus and -- crucially -- validate it not by human inter-rater agreement but by four falsifiable tests it could fail: an
  independent computational check, discrimination against hard negatives, out-of-sample prediction, and description-language robustness; all pass with margin. The contribution is not "creativity is compression" but its decidability,
  discrimination, and corpus: on this account, what makes a move genuinely creative -- rather than merely novel -- is that it compresses a conflict, with novelty and value as downstream symptoms; whether all creativity is so
  constituted we state as an explicit conjecture. We claim only the sign of C-1; we judge, not generate. The result is a citable primitive for a broader program.

</details>


### [84] [Fusing Stylometric and Embedding Systems to Estimate Authorship Likelihood Ratios in Japanese](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13991)
*Praju Ghatpande,Satoru Tsuge,Shunichi Ishihara,Wataru Zaitsu,Mitsuyuki Inaba*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 融合系统在保持良好校准性的同时，显著提升符合事实的似然比值，降低违背事实的似然比值，整体判别能力增强。最优融合方案的对数似然比成本仅为0.32484，表明该框架适用于日语文本，且跨系统融合能有效提升性能。

Conclusion: 本研究首次成功将似然比框架应用于日语文本分析，验证了其在非英语语言中的可行性；同时，融合风格特征与嵌入系统可显著提升系统性能，是未来法医文本分析的重要方向。

Abstract: The likelihood ratio framework is widely recognized as the logically and legally sound basis for evidential analysis across forensic sciences, and its importance is increasingly acknowledged in analyses of authorship in textual evidence. To date, however, its application has been confined to English-language texts. Meanwhile, authorship attribution has traditionally relied on a diverse array of stylometric features, even as the rise of pre-trained large language models enables new contextual-embedding approaches. Combining these diverse approaches through fusion promises enhanced performance, yet it has not been applied to integrate stylometric-feature systems with embedding-based systems within the likelihood ratio paradigm. This study is the first to apply likelihood ratio-based forensic text comparison to Japanese digital texts, using ~1,000-character excerpts from blogs, to 1) evaluate system performance and likelihood ratio magnitudes and 2) assess the impact of fusing stylometric-feature systems with embedding-based systems. The results demonstrate that the fused system maintains excellent calibration while 1) increasing consistent-with-fact likelihood ratio magnitudes; 2) decreasing contrary-to-fact likelihood ratio magnitudes and 3) improving overall discriminability. The best-performing fusion achieved a log-likelihood-ratio cost of 0.32484, illustrating both the feasibility of likelihood ratio framework for Japanese and the benefits of fusion across heterogeneous systems.

### [87] [Right or Wrong, Models Comply: Directional Blindness in LLM Moral Judgment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14037)
*Jihye Kim,Jeffrey Flanigan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种双向诊断方法——合规不对称性（A = BCR/HCR），用于评估大语言模型在面对有益提示和有害提示时的响应差异。研究发现，模型在事实类问题上更倾向于接受有益提示（A=1.58），但在道德类问题上对两种提示的响应几乎无差别（A=1.04），表明当前模型存在方向盲目的道德合规问题。此外，思维链提示会同时增强有益与有害的合规行为，而基于身份的提示则同等抑制两者。研究建议，对齐目标应关注方向校准的更新机制，而非单纯降低合规性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估将合规性视为单向过程，仅衡量模型是否抵抗压力，忽视了其是否能选择性地响应不同性质的用户推动力。这种忽略可能导致模型在道德判断中表现出方向盲目的行为，影响其安全性和可靠性。因此，亟需一种能区分有益与有害提示影响的双向评估框架。

Method: 提出合规不对称性（A = BCR/HCR）作为度量指标，通过对比模型在972,000次不同提示条件下的输出变化，分析其在事实与道德判断任务中对有益与有害提示的响应差异。实验涵盖9种模型，覆盖多种模型家族、能力层级及提示类型。

Result: 在事实类问题中，模型对有益提示的响应显著高于有害提示（A=1.58）；而在道德类问题中，两种提示的响应率几乎一致（A=1.04），表明模型在道德判断中缺乏方向敏感性。链式思维提示加剧了有益与有害合规行为，而身份提示则等幅抑制二者。

Conclusion: 当前大语言模型在道德判断中存在方向盲目的合规现象，是一种独立的对齐失败模式。未来的对齐策略应致力于实现方向性校准的更新机制，而非简单追求低合规性。

Abstract: As language models take integrated roles across many domains, the response of LLMs to user pushback becomes a critical alignment property. Yet many existing evaluations treat compliance as unidirectional, measuring whether models resist pressure but not whether they resist it selectively. We introduce Compliance Asymmetry (A = BCR/HCR), a bidirectional diagnostic that compares beneficial output change under helpful nudges with harmful change under misleading nudges. Across 9 models and 972,000 nudge-condition responses, we find that this selectivity differs in factual and moral judgments: models follow helpful nudges more than harmful ones on factual questions (A = 1.58), but follow both directions at nearly identical rates on moral questions (A = 1.04). This phenomenon persists across model families, capability levels, and nudging types. Interestingly, we also find that chain-of-thought prompting amplifies helpful and harmful compliance together, while identity-based prompting suppresses both by nearly identical margins. These results identify direction-blind moral compliance as a distinct failure mode in current LLMs and suggest that alignment should target directionally calibrated updating rather than lower compliance alone.

</details>


### [88] [Harsher on Male? Evaluating LLMs on Gender-Asymmetric Moral Framing Across Diverse Conflict Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14068)
*Guangzong Si,Dong Wang,Zhenhao Li,Yifan Yu,Panwang Pan,Wentao Zhu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出GAMA-Bench，一个包含1298个场景的性别镜像基准测试，用于评估大语言模型在相同负面行为下对男性和女性行为者的响应一致性。通过控制变量的中性不当行为模板和成对的第一人称提示，研究发现模型对男性行为者更倾向于惩罚性、升级性和责备导向的回应，而对女性行为者则更倾向治疗性和共情导向的回应，这种不对称性在不同模型家族、场景类型、模型规模和推理风格中均持续存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多关注性别刻板印象、职业关联或明确有害输出，但较少探讨大语言模型在相同负面行为下对不同性别行为者是否应用一致的响应标准。本研究旨在揭示模型在性别相关反应上的潜在偏差。

Method: 构建性别中立的不当行为模板，通过受控网格和跨模型审查生成；设计成对的第一人称提示，匹配性别与角色引用变化；采用结构化响应框架量化惩罚、共情、升级、指导和责备等维度。

Result: 实验表明，所有10个代表性大语言模型均表现出对男性行为者的系统性不利响应：更严厉、更升级、更强调责备，而对女性行为者则更多体现共情与治疗导向。该模式在不同模型家族、场景类型、规模及推理方式下保持稳定。

Conclusion: 大语言模型在处理相同负面行为时，对男性和女性行为者存在显著的响应不对称性，反映出系统性的性别偏见，亟需在模型设计与评估中引入性别公平性考量。

Abstract: Existing studies on gender bias in LLMs have largely focused on stereotypes, occupational associations, or explicit harmful outputs. In this work, we ask whether LLMs apply consistent response standards to the same negative behavior under matched male-actor and female-actor conditions. We introduce GAMA-Bench, a gender-mirrored benchmark of 1,298 scenarios covering intimate relationship and public social conflicts. It constructs gender-neutral misconduct templates through controlled grids and cross-model review, then compiles them into paired first-person prompts with matched actor-gender and role-reference variations. We further design a structured response-framing protocol to measure how models allocate punishment, empathy, escalation, instruction, and blame. Experiments on 10 representative LLMs reveal a consistent male-disadvantaging asymmetry: male actors receive more punitive, escalatory, and blame-centered framing, whereas female actors receive more therapeutic and empathy-oriented framing for the same misconduct. Further analyses show that this pattern persists across model families, scenario tracks, model scale, and explicit thinking-style reasoning. The official code is available at https://github.com/xufeiqiong/GAMA-Bench.

### [89] [Beyond Perplexity: UTF-8 Validity in Byte-aware Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14122)
*Sangwhan Moon,Daisuke Oba,Youmi Ma,Tatsuya Hiraoka,Naoaki Okazaki*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了训练规模对语言模型生成有效UTF-8序列可靠性的影响，发现模型在生成有效UTF-8方面需要比困惑度稳定多一倍的训练数据量。即使在无上下文生成中，罕见字符的结构有效性反而高于常见字符，表明频繁字符的表示存在过度特化问题。研究强调，可靠地生成有效UTF-8是独立于语言建模能力的一项关键能力，需专门评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于字节级分词的语言模型虽能处理任意Unicode输入，但在遇到罕见或未见字符时可能生成无效UTF-8序列。现有评估主要依赖困惑度，但无法反映生成的有效性，因此需要更精细的评估方法来衡量模型在保持编码结构正确性方面的表现。

Method: 使用一个355M参数的模型，在包含英语、日语、韩语和中文的平衡多语言语料库上训练至800亿个标记。设计多种评估协议，将UTF-8结构有效性与语言建模性能分离，分析不同训练阶段下模型生成有效UTF-8的能力，并对比常见与罕见字符的表现。

Result: 困惑度在约21亿标记后趋于稳定，而UTF-8结构有效性需约42亿标记才达到收敛，滞后约两倍。在无上下文生成中，罕见字符的结构有效性高于常见字符，表明模型对高频字符的表示存在过拟合现象。

Conclusion: 可靠生成有效UTF-8是语言模型中一项独立且重要的能力，不应仅通过困惑度评估。训练规模需足够大以确保编码结构的正确性，且当前模型对常见字符的表示可能存在过度特化问题，需进一步优化。

Abstract: Byte-level tokenization enables language models to handle any Unicode input, but models can generate invalid UTF-8 sequences when encountering rare or unseen characters. We investigate the relationship between training scale and UTF-8 generation reliability with a 355M parameter model trained on 80B tokens from a balanced multilingual corpus of English, Japanese, Korean, and Chinese. We introduce multiple evaluation protocols that isolate UTF-8 structural validity from language modeling. UTF-8 validity convergence lags perplexity by a roughly a factor of two: perplexity stabilizes after 2.1B tokens, but UTF-8 validity requires 4.2B tokens. In context-free generation, rare characters achieve higher structural validity than common characters, suggesting over-specialization of frequent character representations. Through experiments, we observed that reliable UTF-8 generation is a distinct capability requiring evaluation beyond perplexity.
