### [90] [Implicit Reasoning for Large Language Model-based Generative Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14142)
*Yinhan He,Liam Collins,Bhuvesh Kumar,Jundong Li,Neil Shah,Donald Loveland*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为PauseRec的轻量级隐式推理范式，用于解决大语言模型（LLM）在生成推荐（GR）中因使用语义ID（SID）导致的世界知识利用不足的问题。现有方法依赖复杂的多阶段推理流程，成本高且效果受限。PauseRec避免了昂贵的推理轨迹获取和对齐训练，显著提升效率与性能，相比标准显式思维链（CoT）方法最高提升6.22%，训练成本降低65%，推理速度加快71.3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM-based GR方法使用未在预训练中见过的语义ID（SIDs），破坏了自然语言推理能力，而现有解决方案依赖复杂、昂贵的多阶段推理管道，缺乏对各阶段必要性的理解，且存在世界知识表达弱化、嵌入空间错配及对推理质量敏感等问题。

Method: 系统分解显式推理训练流程，识别三大局限性；提出轻量级隐式推理框架PauseRec，通过避免显式推理轨迹生成与对齐训练，实现高效、有效的推荐生成。

Result: PauseRec在推荐性能上优于标准显式思维链方法最多6.22%，训练成本降低65% GPU小时，推理速度提升71.3%，展现出更高的效率与实用性。

Conclusion: PauseRec提供了一种更高效、更实用的LLM-based GR方案，克服了显式推理的瓶颈，为大规模应用提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly adopted as backbones for Generative Recommendation (GR), promising access to pretrained world knowledge. Yet reliably invoking this knowledge for GR remains poorly understood. A key obstacle is that LLM-based GR typically represents items with Semantic IDs (SIDs), disrupting LLMs' natural-language reasoning interface because these tokens are unseen by the LLM during pretraining. Existing approaches address this with expensive multi-stage pipelines that ground SIDs and elicit explicit rationales, but offer limited insight into when and why each stage is necessary. In this work, we systematically decompose explicit reasoning training pipelines for LLM-based GR, revealing three key limitations: weakened world-knowledge verbalization, misalignment between SID and natural-language token embedding spaces, and sensitivity to rationale quality, all of which hurt explicit reasoning performance. To circumvent these issues, we propose PauseRec, a lightweight implicit reasoning paradigm tailored for GR. PauseRec is exceptionally practical, avoiding costly reasoning trace acquisition and reasoning alignment training, leading to a multitude of benefits: (1) it outperforms standard explicit CoT methods by up to 6.22%, (2) it reduces training cost by up to 65% GPU hours, and (3) it speeds up inference by up to 71.3%. These results position PauseRec as a lightweight alternative to explicit rationale generation, enabling more effective and efficient LLM-based GR.

### [91] [Personal Care Utility: Health as Everyday Infrastructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14145)
*Mahyar Abbasian,Elahe Khatibi,Saba A. Farahani,Nitish Nagesh,Arshia Ilaty,Hooman Sajjadi,Amir Rahmani,Ramesh Jain*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出个人护理实用程序（PCU），一种分层、事件驱动的架构，旨在填补日常健康领域缺乏基础设施的空白。PCU通过‘个人体’（Personicle）将连续的个人信号组织成语义上有意义的生活事件，基于个人基线动态估计健康状态，推理因果关系与背景，并通过编排器将临床决策逻辑、行为策略选择和自然语言表达分离。该设计使大型语言模型可用于推理与沟通，同时确保关键临床决策基于验证证据。以2型糖尿病为例，整合CGM、饮食、活动、用药、睡眠、压力和临床数据，生成血糖事件、个性化状态估计、因果解释和知识支持的干预措施。一个典型日场景展示其可实时推送提醒、周报、用药确认或确定性安全警报，依情境与风险而定。研究还探讨了PCU在其他慢性病中的泛化潜力及始终在线的个人健康服务所涉及的治理问题。最终，PCU提供了一个蓝图，将个性化视为日常健康指导的架构属性，而非仅作为消息传递的末端层。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前医疗体系高度依赖短暂的临床接触，而8759小时的日常生活时间中，饮食、睡眠、运动、用药和压力等真正影响长期健康，却缺乏相应支持系统。现有挑战并非数据或计算能力不足，而是缺少持续性的个人健康基础设施。因此，亟需构建一种类似支付、网络、电力的‘通用服务’，用于日常健康管理。

Method: 提出并设计个人护理实用程序（PCU），采用分层、事件驱动的架构；通过‘个人体’（Personicle）整合多源连续数据（如CGM、饮食、活动、药物、睡眠、压力等），识别语义生活事件；建立个人基线，动态估计健康状态；利用因果推理分析上下文与原因；通过编排器解耦临床决策、行为策略与语言表达模块；借助大语言模型增强推理与沟通能力，但保留临床决策的安全性与证据基础。

Result: 在2型糖尿病场景下成功实现从原始数据到血糖事件、个性化健康状态、因果解释和干预建议的转化；在典型日场景中展示了灵活响应：实时提醒、周度总结、用药确认、静默处理或安全警报；证明该架构具备可扩展性，适用于其他慢性病；提出了一种将个性化嵌入系统架构的新型范式，为未来智能健康系统提供蓝图。

Conclusion: PCU是一种具有普遍意义的个人健康基础设施，它将个性化从消息层提升为系统架构属性。该框架不仅提升了健康管理的持续性与智能化水平，也揭示了始终在线健康服务所需的治理挑战。这标志着从被动诊疗向主动、持续、个性化的健康模式的根本转变。

Abstract: Healthcare is essential, expert, and episodic by design - built around the roughly one hour per year a person spends with a clinician. The 8,759 hours outside clinical settings, where eating, sleeping, movement, medication, and stress actually shape long-term health, have no comparable infrastructure. The bottleneck for personalized health is not raw data or reasoning capability; it is the absence of that infrastructure layer. This paper introduces the Personal Care Utility (PCU): a layered, event-driven architecture proposed as the missing utility for everyday health, in the way that payments, networks, and power are utilities for their domains. PCU organizes continuous personal signals into semantically meaningful life events through a Personicle, estimates dynamic health state against personal baselines, reasons about cause and context, and routes guidance through an orchestrator that separates clinical decision logic, behavioral strategy selection, and natural-language expression. This separation lets large language models support reasoning and communication while keeping safety-critical clinical decisions grounded in validated evidence. We instantiate PCU for Type 2 Diabetes - turning CGM, meal, activity, medication, sleep, stress, and clinical data into glycemic events, individualized state estimates, causal explanations, and knowledge-grounded interventions. A day-in-the-life scenario shows the same infrastructure producing real-time nudges, weekly summaries, medication check-ins, silence, or deterministic safety alerts depending on context and risk. We close with how PCU generalizes to other chronic conditions and the governance questions any always-on personal health utility must address. The result is a blueprint that treats personalization not as a final messaging layer, but as an architectural property of everyday health guidance.

</details>


### [92] [CacheRL:Multi-Turn Tool-Calling Agents via Cached Rollouts and Hybrid Reward](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14179)
*Md Amirul Islam,Sumiran Thakur,Huancheng Chen,Su Min Park,Jiayun Wang,Gyuhak Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CacheRL 是一种训练小型代理基础模型的系统，在多步工具调用任务上达到 92% 的过程准确率，接近 GPT-5 的 94%，但仅需其 1/100 的计算量。它通过三项创新解决实际代理训练中的三大挑战：大规模迁移大模型的工具调用知识、在无需昂贵实时工具执行的情况下进行强化学习、以及从噪声缓存环境中稳健学习。该系统采用混合思维轨迹管道增强代理轨迹，引入 LLM 生成的推理路径，使模型不仅学会调用工具，还理解原因；通过三层次模糊缓存机制（CacheAgentLoop）消除实时执行开销，同时使用标记级掩码保持轨迹保真度；设计缓存层级感知奖励机制，动态调整答案质量权重，避免因缓存限制惩罚模型。通过迭代式监督微调（SFT）与组相对策略优化（GRPO），Qwen3-4B-Thinking 的验证奖励从 0.43 提升至 0.78。在公开的代理工具调用基准测试中，模型性能可媲美前沿模型如 GPT-5。消融实验表明，移除知识迁移导致性能下降 41%，而缓存感知奖励带来 17% 的提升。有趣的是，强化学习虽提升了训练稳定性，但超越强监督微调的增益有限，表明数据质量和奖励设计比复杂优化方法对构建实用小模型更为关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有小型代理模型在多步工具调用任务中性能受限于训练成本高、无法高效利用大模型知识、以及依赖昂贵实时工具执行等问题。需要一种低成本、高效率且能从噪声环境中学到鲁棒行为的训练方法，以实现小型模型接近大型模型的表现。

Method: 提出 CacheRL 系统，包含三项核心创新：（1）混合思维轨迹管道，结合真实轨迹与 LLM 生成的推理路径，丰富训练样本的语义信息；（2）CacheAgentLoop 缓存机制，采用三层次模糊缓存并配合 token 级掩码，实现无实时执行的高效训练；（3）缓存层级感知奖励函数，根据缓存状态动态调整奖励权重，缓解缓存带来的偏差影响。整体采用迭代 SFT 与 GRPO 进行优化。

Result: Qwen3-4B-Thinking 模型在验证集上的奖励从 0.43 提升至 0.78；在多个公开工具调用基准上达到 92% 的过程准确率，接近 GPT-5 的 94%；消融实验证明知识迁移贡献最大（下降 41%），缓存感知奖励贡献次之（+17%）；强化学习虽稳定训练，但增益有限，说明数据与奖励设计更关键。

Conclusion: CacheRL 成功实现了在极低算力下训练高性能的小型代理模型，证明了高质量数据和合理奖励设计是构建实用小型智能体的核心因素，而非复杂的优化算法。该方法为低成本、可扩展的智能体训练提供了新范式。

Abstract: We present CacheRL, a system for training small agent foundation models that achieves 92 percent process accuracy on multi-step tool-calling tasks, approaching GPT-5's 94 percent while requiring 100 times less compute. Our approach addresses three challenges in practical agent training: transferring tool-calling knowledge from large models at scale, enabling reinforcement learning without costly live tool execution, and learning robustly from noisy cached environments. CacheRL introduces three key innovations. First, a hybrid thinking trajectory pipeline augments agent trajectories with LLM-generated reasoning traces, producing training examples that teach models not only what tools to call but also why. Second, the CacheAgentLoop eliminates live execution costs through a three-tier fuzzy cache while preserving trajectory fidelity using token-level masking. Third, a cache-tier-aware reward dynamically adjusts answer-quality weights to avoid penalizing models for cache-induced limitations. Through iterative supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), CacheRL improves Qwen3-4B-Thinking's validation reward from 0.43 to 0.78. On public agentic tool-calling benchmarks, our model achieves competitive performance against frontier models such as GPT-5. Ablation studies show that removing knowledge transfer reduces performance by 41 percent, while cache-aware rewards contribute a 17 percent improvement. Interestingly, reinforcement learning improves training stability but yields limited gains beyond strong supervised fine-tuning, suggesting that data quality and reward design play a more important role than complex optimization methods in building practical small agent models.

</details>


### [93] [OdysSim: Building Foundation Models for Human Behavior Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14199)
*Xuhui Zhou,Weiwei Sun,Weihua Du,Jiarui Liu,Haojia Sun,Qianou Ma,Tongshuang Wu,Yiming Yang,Maarten Sap*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: OdysSim 是对行为基础模型的最大规模开源系统性研究，提出 SOUL 五维能力分类框架（CONV, SS, COG, ROLE, EVAL），整合62个数据集和23个基准任务。构建了包含2140万交互、100亿词元的 OdysSim 语料库，并开发 SOUL-Index 基准与端到端训练流程（含中段训练、任务特定强化学习与专家蒸馏）。8B 开源模型 OSim 在23项任务中8项排名第一或并列第一，尤其在对话与社交任务上表现突出，输出更接近人类行为特征，在 τ-bench 上实现零样本泛化，反应对齐度达93.2（真实用户为93.5）。研究还发现 LLM 作为裁判的强化学习易引发奖励黑客问题，可通过检测器缓解。结论指出需重新思考大模型训练范式，并开放全部资源以推动后续研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在作为人类模拟器用于交互评估和社会模拟时，因以帮助性为导向的后训练导致行为趋同、过度顺从，产生仿真与现实之间的差距。为弥合该差距，亟需构建能真实模拟人类行为的行为基础模型。

Method: 提出SOUL分类框架，整合62个数据集与23个任务；构建大规模OdysSim语料库（21.4M交互，10B tokens），并引入回溯生成的社会上下文；设计SOUL-Index基准；开发融合中段训练、任务特定强化学习与专家蒸馏的端到端训练方法。

Result: 8B开源模型OSim在23项任务中有8项排名第一或并列第一，优于任何单一前沿模型；在对话与社会任务上提升显著；输出更贴近人类在长度、格式和用词上的特征；在τ-bench上实现零样本外分布用户模拟，反应对齐度达93.2（真实用户93.5）；验证了基于LLM作为裁判的RL存在奖励黑客现象，且可通过检测器有效缓解。

Conclusion: 行为基础模型的构建要求重新审视现有的大语言模型训练范式，当前方法难以维持多样性和真实性。通过系统性框架、大规模数据与新型训练策略，可显著提升模型的人类行为模拟能力。所有成果均已开源，支持未来研究。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly deployed as human simulators for interactive evaluation and social simulation. Yet helpfulness-driven post-training pulls them toward a homogeneous, overly agreeable assistant register, creating a behavioral Sim2Real gap. We present OdysSim, the largest open systematic investigation of behavioral foundation models, i.e., models trained to simulate human behavior at scale. We propose SOUL, a taxonomy of five capability axes (CONV, SS, COG, ROLE, EVAL) that unifies 62 datasets and 23 benchmark tasks under one framework. Specifically, we curate the OdysSim corpus (21.4M interactions, 10B tokens, retrofitted with back-generated social contexts), construct the SOUL-Index benchmark, and develop an end-to-end training recipe combining midtraining, task-specific RL, and expert distillation. The resulting open 8B OSim model ranks first or tied-first on 8 of 23 tasks, outperforming any individual frontier model by this count, with the strongest gains on conversational and social tasks. Its outputs are also more human-like in length, formatting, and word choice, and it transfers zero-shot to out-of-distribution user simulation on $τ$-bench, nearly matching real users on reaction alignment (93.2 vs. 93.5). We further show that LLM-as-judge RL induces reward-hacking patterns, and that our detectors can mitigate them during post-training. Together, our findings suggest that behavioral foundation models require rethinking the LLM training paradigm. We release all artifacts to support future research.

</details>

In the case of parliamentary texts, the guidelines on disclosure of AI use are more vague. However, in order to maintain transparency and retain public trust, it is generally recommended that parliamentarians should state whether or not they have used AI when writing texts, such as parliamentary motions. Here, we train an interpretable (glass-box) text classifier using pre-LLM parliamentary texts and LLM-generated versions of such texts. ### [95] [Decoupled Mixture-of-Experts for Parametric Knowledge Injection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14243)
*Baoqing Yue,Weihang Su,Qingyao Ai,Yichen Tang,Changyue Wang,Jiacheng Kang,Jingtao Zhan,Yiqun Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Decoupled Mixture-of-Experts (DMoE)，一种模块化参数知识注入架构，通过将外部知识库转换为可独立更新的专家模块，并使用轻量级不确定性感知路由器在基础模型知识不足时激活相关专家，实现高效、灵活的知识增强。该方法仅在最后一层前馈网络附加专家，保留KV缓存复用能力，支持高效的自回归推理，在知识密集型任务上优于检索和适配器基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识注入方法在灵活性与集成度之间存在权衡：检索增强生成仅提供提示级增强，而基于微调的方法易导致灾难性遗忘、知识冲突和高昂更新成本。因此需要一种既能灵活更新又能避免副作用的参数化知识注入方案。

Method: 提出DMoE架构，将外部知识转化为独立可更新的专家模块，采用轻量级不确定性感知路由器动态激活专家，仅在基础模型知识不足时介入；专家仅部署于模型最后一层前馈网络，保持KV缓存可用性，支持高效自回归推理。

Result: 在多个知识密集型基准测试中，DMoE consistently 提升了答案质量，优于检索增强和适配器基线方法。

Conclusion: DMoE实现了灵活、高效且可扩展的知识注入，通过解耦专家与路由机制，有效缓解了传统方法中的遗忘与冲突问题，同时保持推理效率，是参数化知识注入的有效解决方案。

Abstract: Knowledge injection aims to equip large language models (LLMs) with external, domain-specific, or time-sensitive knowledge. Existing approaches typically face a trade-off between flexibility and integration: retrieval-augmented generation keeps knowledge outside the model but only provides prompt-level augmentation, whereas post-training based methods encode new knowledge into shared parameters but may introduce catastrophic forgetting, knowledge conflict, and costly updates. In this paper, we propose Decoupled Mixture-of-Experts (DMoE), a modular architecture for parametric knowledge injection that decouples both experts and the router from the base model. DMoE converts external knowledge corpora into independently updatable expert modules and uses a lightweight uncertainty-aware router to activate relevant experts only when the base model lacks sufficient knowledge during generation. To support efficient auto-regressive inference, DMoE attaches experts only to the final-layer feed-forward network, preserving KV-cache reuse while enabling parameter-level knowledge augmentation. Experiments on knowledge-intensive benchmarks show that DMoE consistently improves answer quality over retrieval and adapter-based baselines.

The linguistics olympiads (LOs) have become a worldwide phenomenon with 43 different territories taking part in the International Linguistics Olympiad (IOL) 2025. While the typology and solving strategies of LOPs have been analysed, their scientific facet and connections to academic linguistics have yet to be explored. LOPs are directly connected to many linguistic fields, e.g., linguistic typology, linguistic relativity, and linguistics fieldwork. Recently, LOPs have become a research focus as benchmarks for large language models, thus highlighting their usefulness in computational linguistics. Nevertheless, they have not yet been integrated into mainstream linguistics research. This paper attempts to open new directions of including this particular type of puzzle in academic research by offering a structured evaluation of LOPs as linguistic data sources and proposes criteria for their responsible use in academic research. ### [97] [Does the Judge Prefer English? Evaluating Language-Switching Invariance in LLM-as-a-Judge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14278)
*Shaojie Yin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出Judge-LS，一种轻量级元评估协议，用于检验大语言模型（LLM）作为自动评判者时是否受语言表达形式影响。通过将LLMBar中的回答对转换为英文、中文及中英混杂版本，测试评判者在语义不变但语言变化下的偏好一致性。实验表明，中文和中英混杂版本导致10.7%至14.4%的偏好翻转，所有模型在英文下表现最佳。然而，在语义等价的平局探测中，并未发现系统性偏向英文的现象，多数判断为平局，非平局决策反而更倾向中文。研究使用API调用完成，无需训练，可在普通硬件上运行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型广泛用作开放性指令遵循任务的自动评判工具，虽具可扩展性和语义感知优势，但其可靠性存疑：评判结果可能受比较表述的语言形式影响，而非真实答案质量。需建立一种方法检验评判者的语言无关性。

Method: 提出Judge-LS元评估协议，将原始英文回答对转换为中文、中英混合版本，保持语义不变；通过对比不同语言版本下的评判偏好，检测评判者是否因语言变化而改变判断，从而评估其可靠性。

Result: 在419个样本上进行13,408次有效两两判断，结果显示中文与中英混合版本引发10.7%–14.4%的偏好翻转，所有模型在英文下准确率最高；语义等价的平局探针中，多数被判定为平局，非平局决策中更倾向于中文，未发现系统性英文偏好。

Conclusion: 现有LLM自动评判者存在语言敏感性问题，尤其在非英文环境下易产生偏差。尽管无系统性英文偏好，但语言形式仍显著影响判断结果，提示应谨慎使用跨语言评估，未来需开发更具语言鲁棒性的评判机制。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are now widely used as automatic judges for open-ended instruction-following evaluation. This practice is convenient, scalable, and often more semantically aware than reference-based metrics, but it also introduces a new reliability question: does a judge evaluate the quality of an answer, or does it also react to the language in which the comparison is presented? We propose Judge-LS, a lightweight meta-evaluation protocol that transforms LLMBar response-pair items into English, Chinese, and Chinese-English language-switched variants. A reliable judge should preserve its preference under label-preserving language transformations and should not prefer a language when two answers are translation-equivalent. We evaluate four API-accessible judges on the full 419-item LLMBar benchmark, producing 13,408 successful pairwise judgments. Across models, Chinese and language-switched presentations induce 10.7--14.4% preference flips relative to English, and all judges achieve their highest accuracy in English. However, translation-equivalent tie probes do not reveal a systematic English preference: most probes are judged as ties, and non-tie decisions more often favor Chinese. We add confidence intervals, paired significance tests, and an automatic transformation audit with a sensitivity analysis that excludes mechanically flagged high-risk variants. The experiment requires no model training, uses only API calls, and is feasible on modest local hardware.

### [98] [Retrospective Progress-Aware Self-Refinement for LLM Agent Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14302)
*Xinbei Ma,Congmin Zheng,Jiyang Qiu,Jiale Hong,Yao Yao,Xiangmou Qu,Jiaxin Yin,Xingyu Lou,Jun Wang,Weiwen Liu,Weinan Zhang,Zhuosheng Zhang,Hai Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: RePro是一种基于回顾性进展感知的训练框架，通过前向执行后反思的滚动范式，使大语言模型代理能够自动生成进度信号，从而提升长时程任务表现。该方法先通过少量外部示范进行反思格式预热，再通过复合奖励机制实现无需持续外部监督的自我生成信号训练，在WebShop、ALFWorld和Sokoban任务中显著提升Qwen系列模型性能，最高成功率提升达12%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出RePro框架，采用前向执行-回顾反思的滚动策略：代理先在线执行动作，再根据完整轨迹和已知结果回顾评估每一步进展；包含两个阶段：初始的回顾预热（Retrospection Warmup）以学习反思格式，后续使用RePro-PO通过复合奖励机制实现无外部监督的自我生成进度信号训练。

Conclusion: RePro通过引入回顾性进展感知机制，弥补了传统强化学习训练中代理缺乏元认知的问题，为构建具备自我评估与规划能力的智能体提供了新路径，尤其适用于复杂、长周期的任务场景。

Abstract: LLM-based agents trained with reinforcement learning optimize step-wise action prediction but lack metacognitive awareness of task progress, inducing a gap that hinders long-horizon scaling. A pilot study reveals that online progress prompting hurts performance while retrospective demonstrations help, yet this capability cannot emerge from outcome-reward training alone. We present RePro, Retrospective Progress-Aware Training, a framework that trains agents to self-generate progress signals via a forward-then-reflect rollout paradigm: the agent executes actions online, then retrospectively reassesses its step-wise progress given the completed trajectory and known outcome. RePro initializes with a Retrospection Warmup that teaches reflection format from minimal external demonstrations, then further trains through RePro-PO with a composite reward that produces self-generated signals without continuous external supervision. Experiments on WebShop, ALFWorld, and Sokoban show that RePro enhances the Qwen family's performance, with up to $12\%$ absolute success rate gains.

### [100] [Learning to Hear Hesitation: Continual Learning for Disfluency-Aware ASR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14391)
*Henri-Leon Kordt,Theresa Pekarek Rosin,Jae Hee Lee,Stefan Wermter*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用持续学习框架，先在预训练ASR模型中引入显式不流畅标记，建立稳定标记机制，随后在多个具有不同不流畅分布的额外数据集上进行增量训练，通过分析训练过程中的模型动态，探索性能与标记学习之间的平衡。

Conclusion: 通过引入显式不流畅标记并结合持续学习策略，该方法能够在不牺牲通用语音识别能力的前提下，显著提升对口语不流畅现象的处理能力，为构建鲁棒的语音识别系统提供了新思路。

Prior work has focused on verbatim transcription and the integration of disfluency markers, but adapting models on limited datasets can lead to catastrophic forgetting of general-domain knowledge. We address this gap by leveraging continual learning (CL) with explicit disfluency tokens. We first introduce these tokens into a pretrained ASR model to establish stable token mechanisms, and then continue training on additional datasets with varying disfluency distributions. Through a detailed analysis of model dynamics during training, we identify a trade-off between marker learning and ASR performance, and a consistent cross-attention head mechanism shared across CL methods.

*Şevval Çakıcı*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究利用超过一百万条土耳其语推文，分析2023年2月6日土耳其地震后人们的应对方式，并在真实时间尺度上检测这些行为。基于Lazarus和Folkman的应对理论，研究开发了一个多标签BERTurk分类器，用于识别三种应对风格（问题导向、情绪导向、意义建构），并划分四个理论驱动的危机阶段。BERTurk模型的宏F1得分为0.693，显著优于零样本mDeBERTa基线（宏F1=0.324）。结果表明，问题导向应对在紧急阶段占主导地位并迅速下降，情绪导向应对上升并趋于稳定，而意义建构则持续增长。愤怒与意义建构高度相关（Spearman r = 0.387），表明愤怒更多是归责动员而非实际行动的动力。研究证明应对理论可在真实数字危机数据中可靠应用，有助于人道组织根据公众心理状态调整响应策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 了解灾难发生后人们如何应对，并能否通过其在线文字表达实时、大规模地检测这些应对方式，以帮助人道组织更精准地制定响应策略。

Method: 基于Lazarus和Folkman的应对理论，构建一个多标签Berturk分类器，用于识别问题聚焦、情绪聚焦和意义建构三种应对风格，并结合四个危机阶段进行分析。使用超过一百万条土耳其语推文作为数据集，比较BERTurk与零样本mDeBERTa模型的表现。

Result: BERTurk模型的宏F1达到0.693，远超mDeBERTa的0.324；在时间序列上，问题聚焦应对在紧急阶段主导但迅速下降，情绪聚焦应对上升并稳定，意义建构持续增加；愤怒与意义建构高度相关（r=0.387），表明愤怒更倾向于激发责任归因而非实际行动。

Conclusion: 应对理论可有效应用于真实世界的数字危机数据中，通过自动化检测公众的应对模式，为灾害响应提供科学依据，帮助人道组织根据民众心理状态动态调整干预策略。

Abstract: How do people cope when disaster strikes and can we detect it at scale, in real time, from what they write? This study addresses that question using over one million Turkish-language tweets posted in the aftermath of the February 6, 2023 earthquake in Turkiye, which unfolded in a deeply polarized political context just months before a national election. Drawing on Lazarus and Folkman's (1984) coping theory, we develop a multi-label BERTurk classifier to detect three coping styles (problem-focused, emotion-focused, and meaning-making) across four theoretically motivated crisis phases. BERTurk achieves a macro F1 of 0.693, substantially outperforming a zero-shot mDeBERTa baseline (macro F1 = 0.324). Applied to the full corpus, the classifier reveals a clear temporal trajectory: problem-focused coping dominates the urgency phase and declines sharply, emotion-focused coping rises and stabilizes, and meaning-making increases monotonically. Anger correlates most strongly with meaning-making (Spearman r = 0.387), suggesting it functions as a mobilizing force toward blame attribution rather than practical action. These findings demonstrate that coping theory can be reliably operationalized in real-world digital crisis data and that doing so can help humanitarian organizations tailor their responses to where a population actually is.

### [102] [MoDiCoL: A Modular Diagnostic Continual Learning Dataset for Robust Speech Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14459)
*Theresa Pekarek Rosin,Matthias Kerzel,Stefan Wermter*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ASR系统在标准基准上表现优异，但在真实世界分布偏移（如录音条件、口音、语音障碍、噪声等）下性能下降。现有数据集通常孤立处理这些因素，忽略了它们在实际应用中的共现，导致模型鲁棒性评估不充分。因此亟需一种能模拟真实复杂场景的持续学习框架，以研究模型鲁棒性的动态演化过程。

Method: 提出MoDiCoL数据集，支持对语言内容、说话人特征和声学环境的模块化控制；设计一种真实世界启发的持续学习课程，模拟增量更新过程；采用三种持续学习策略进行实验，分析模型在动态条件下的鲁棒性获取、转移与遗忘行为。

Result: 实验表明，不同持续学习策略在应对多因素共现的分布偏移时表现各异；所提出的框架能够有效揭示鲁棒性随时间演化的规律，为构建更具适应性的语音识别系统提供了可解释的训练范式。

Conclusion: 模型鲁棒性并非静态属性，而是一种可通过持续学习动态发展的能力。通过合理设计数据集与学习课程，可以系统地研究并提升ASR系统在真实复杂环境中的长期适应性。

Abstract: Modern Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) systems have made remarkable progress on standard benchmarks, yet performance gaps have emerged under real-world distribution shifts, caused by recording conditions, accents, speech impairments, and noise. Existing datasets and benchmarks typically isolate these factors, which overlooks their co-occurrence in real-world applications. In this paper, we argue that model robustness can be treated as a dynamic capability that continually develops, and we introduce MoDiCoL, a Modular Diagnostic Continual Learning dataset designed for controlled analysis of linguistic content, speaker characteristics, and acoustic environments. Furthermore, we propose a real-world-inspired continual learning curriculum to simulate incremental updates and study how robustness is acquired, transferred, and forgotten. We evaluate three continual learning strategies and provide detailed insights into robustness under evolving conditions.

### [103] [A Computational Audit of Demographic Association Encoding in ClinicalBERT Language Predictions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14460)
*Kehinde Temitayo Soetan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究系统审计了ClinicalBERT模型中的表征偏差，通过两种互补的探测方法（LPBA和MLM）发现模型内部的偏差放大是主要机制，而非直接继承训练数据中的偏差。65.6%的显著发现与语料库分布矛盾，对黑人患者和代理权归属的探测中这一比例更高，表明模型在推理过程中主动放大了社会人口学偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示基于Transformer的临床语言模型在决策支持系统中如何将医疗记录中的社会人口学关联传播到概率分布，评估其表征偏差的来源，推动健康公平性改进。

Method: 采用Log Probability Bias Analysis (LPBA) 和 Masked Language Model-based analysis (MLM) 两种探测方法，分析98个真实临床句式模板和8种交叉种族-性别组合中的代理权归因编码，并结合语料库频率分析区分统计差异与偏差放大。

Conclusion: ClinicalBERT中的表征偏差主要由模型内部机制放大所致，而非单纯反映训练数据中的统计分布，强调需在算法审计中关注模型推理过程中的偏差生成机制，以促进临床AI系统的公平性。

Abstract: Transformer-based clinical language models are increasingly integrated into high-stakes clinical decision support pipelines, yet the computational mechanisms through which demographic associations encoded in medical documentation propagate into model probability distributions remain empirically underspecified. We present a systematic computational audit of representational bias in ClinicalBERT (Alsentzer et al., 2019), a BERT-based model pretrained on MIMIC-III discharge summaries, employing two complementary probing methodologies: Log Probability Bias Analysis (LPBA), which quantifies demographic descriptor-induced shifts in masked token probability distributions across behavioral and evaluative semantic categories, and Masked Language Model-based analysis (MLM), which probes internal representational structure for demographic agency attribution encoding across 98 real clinical sentence templates and eight intersectional race-gender combinations. Corpus frequency analysis operationalizes the distinction between statistical disparity and bias amplification by benchmarking model outputs against empirical term frequencies in the MIMIC-III training corpus. Of 32 statistically significant findings, 65.6% contradict observed corpus distributions, rising to 80% for Black patients and 87.5% for agency attribution under MLM probing, providing direct empirical evidence that representational bias in ClinicalBERT operates predominantly through model-internal amplification rather than training data inheritance. ### [104] [Fodor and Pylyshyn's Systematicity Challenge Still Stands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14512)
*Michael Goodale,Salvador Mascarenhas*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文质疑神经网络是否真正解决了认知科学中关于系统性（systematicity）的挑战。尽管有研究声称神经网络通过元学习实现组合性可解释人类的语言系统性，但本文指出这些结论过于乐观。作者发现该模型在分布外任务上表现不佳，且在部分分布内任务上也表现出非系统性行为，因此认为弗多尔和皮利申的挑战仍未被神经网络克服。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨神经网络是否能解释人类语言与思维中的系统性现象，特别是针对弗多尔和皮利申提出的经典挑战。

Method: 通过实验评估 Brenden Lake 与 Marco Baroni 提出的元学习组合性协议在分布内与分布外任务上的表现，检验其是否具备系统性行为。

Result: 模型在略微偏离训练数据分布的任务上表现差，且在许多分布内任务中也表现出非系统性行为，说明其无法可靠复制人类的系统性认知特征。

Conclusion: 目前的神经网络模型尚未满足弗多尔和皮利申对系统性的要求，该挑战依然未被解决。

Abstract: The recent successes of neural networks producing human-like language have caused significant stir in cognitive science, with many researchers arguing that classical puzzles about human cognition and challenges to artificial intelligence are being solved by neural networks. A notable case is the argument from systematicity due to Jerry Fodor and Zenon Pylyshyn, argues that humans display systematic biconditional dependencies. For example, someone can understand the sentence "John saw Mary" just in case that they understand the sentence "Mary saw John." Symbolic systems explain this systematicity of language and thought, while neural networks offer no immediate explanation. Several recent articles argue that this challenge has now been met by neural networks. In particular, Brenden Lake and Marco Baroni argue that their meta-learning for compositionality protocol matches and perhaps explains human systematicity. We demonstrate that these conclusions are premature. Among other results, we found that their model struggles to learn rules that are even slightly out of distribution compared to their training data. Furthermore, the model behaves unsystematically even on many within-distribution problems. We conclude that Fodor and Pylyshyn's challenge to neural networks remains unmet.

</details>


### [105] [BayLing-Duplex: Native Full-Duplex Speech Dialogue with a Single Autoregressive LLM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14528)
*Qingkai Fang,Shoutao Guo,Yang Feng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: BayLing-Duplex 是一种原生全双工语音语言模型，无需外部语音活动检测（VAD）模块，通过少量特殊标记实现听、说、停止的自主决策，仅用40万条全双工样本微调即在多项评测中达到92%的对话成功率和100%的打断成功率，同时提升语音响应质量，且性能不逊于传统单向模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语音语言模型仍为单向交互，依赖外部语音活动检测（VAD）模块判断用户说话结束，限制了真实场景下的自然互动能力。为实现真正的实时全双工语音交互，需构建无需外部辅助模块、能自主管理听与说行为的模型。

Method: 在标准自回归大语言模型基础上，引入少量特殊控制令牌以实现全双工行为决策，使模型自主决定何时倾听、何时说话、何时停止；仅需微调和轻量级直接偏好优化（DPO）训练，无需架构修改即可适配现有模型与服务系统。

Result: 在InstructS2S-Eval上达到92%的对话成功和100%的打断成功率，语音响应评分从2.17提升至3.39（优于Moshi），同时在多个基准测试中表现不低于或超过其单向对应模型。

Conclusion: BayLing-Duplex 实现了无需外部模块的原生全双工语音交互，具备高自然度、强实时性，且可无缝集成到现有系统中，为下一代智能语音助手提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Real-time, full-duplex speech interaction is a key feature of next-generation spoken chatbots, allowing the model to listen and speak at the same time and to handle natural phenomena such as overlap, hesitation, and barge-in. Existing speech language models (SpeechLMs) such as LLaMA-Omni and GLM-4-Voice are still turn-based and rely on an external Voice Activity Detection (VAD) module to mark the end of the user's turn, which fundamentally limits their interactive ability. In this paper, we introduce BayLing-Duplex, a native full-duplex SpeechLM where a single autoregressive LLM decides when to listen, when to speak, and when to stop, with no auxiliary turn-taking module. The design adds only a few special tokens to the standard vocabulary, so it transfers across LLMs and reuses existing training and serving stacks with no architectural adaptation. Starting from the public GLM-4-Voice checkpoint and using only 400K full-duplex samples for fine-tuning followed by a lightweight DPO stage, BayLing-Duplex reaches 92% turn-taking success and 100% interruption success on InstructS2S-Eval, while improving the speech-response score from 2.17 to 3.39 over Moshi. BayLing-Duplex also matches or surpasses its turn-based counterpart on Llama Questions, Web Questions, and Alpaca-Eval, showing that simultaneous listen-and-speak modeling does not sacrifice response quality.

### [106] [SIMMER: Benchmarking Latent Failures in LLM Executable Planning with a World Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14574)
*Xiaoxin Lu,Ranran Haoran Zhang,Rui Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出SIMMER基准，用于评估大语言模型（LLM）在家庭环境中作为自主代理规划器时的潜在失败问题。现有基准仅关注计划能否成功执行，忽视了不立即显现但会悄悄破坏目标达成的潜在失败，严重时可能导致不可逆伤害。SIMMER基于厨房场景构建了一个由77个动作、262个物体和约46,800种语义合理的交互组成的符号化世界模型，并通过状态机执行器检测即时前提违规、潜在风险和不可逆失败。实验表明，即使前沿模型也仅有最多17%的无错误计划，高达56%的计划存在潜在失败，多数导致不可逆后果。通过引入反事实前瞻模拟进行显式状态推理，可使潜在失败减少72%，不可逆情况减少75%，证明该方向对提升LLM规划鲁棒性具有潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估基准未能涵盖大语言模型在家庭环境中作为规划器时可能发生的潜在失败，这类失败不会立即触发反馈，却可能在后期悄然导致任务失败甚至不可逆损害，因此亟需一种能够识别和衡量此类风险的新评估框架。

Method: 构建一个基于真实烹饪脚本的符号化世界模型，包含77个动作、262个物体和约46,800种语义合理的交互；设计状态机执行器，用于验证计划是否违反即时前提、是否存在潜在危害或造成不可逆失败；在六种大语言模型上进行测试，并引入反事实前瞻模拟进行状态推理以对比效果。

Result: 实验结果显示，即便最先进模型也仅能生成最多17%无错误的计划；高达56%的计划含有潜在失败，其中多数导致不可逆后果；采用反事实前瞻模拟进行显式状态推理后，潜在失败减少72%，不可逆案例减少75%。

Conclusion: 潜在失败是影响大语言模型规划可靠性的关键挑战，通过引入反事实前瞻模拟等显式状态推理机制，显著提升了规划的安全性和鲁棒性，为未来更安全的自主智能系统设计提供了重要方向。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as planners for autonomous agents in household environments. While existing benchmarks evaluate whether LLM-generated plans execute successfully, they overlook a critical type of failure: latent failures. Unlike immediate failures that trigger instant feedback at execution time and enable timely correction, latent failures do not immediately halt plan execution but silently compromise goal achievement. In severe cases, they cause irreversible harm. To address this gap, we introduce SIMMER, a benchmark for evaluating latent failures in LLM planning through a human-curated symbolic world model grounded in the kitchen domain. SIMMER defines a world model comprising 77 actions, 262 unique objects, and approximately 46,800 possible interactions that are semantically realistic, derived from real-world cooking scripts. It then leverages a state machine executor that validates plans against the world model and detects immediate precondition violations, latent hazards, and irreversible failures. Experiments across six LLMs show that even frontier models achieve at most 17% error-free plans. Moreover, up to 56% of plans contain latent failures, the majority of which lead to irreversible consequences. We further demonstrate that explicit state reasoning via counterfactual foresight simulation can reduce latent failures by up to 72% and irreversible cases by up to 75%, suggesting a promising direction for more robust LLM planners.

### [107] [Persuasion Index: A Theory-Guided Framework for Persuasion Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14580)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: PI为理解与说服相关的修辞模式提供了可解释、可扩展且可审计的框架，适用于人类与AI沟通的多场景分析，推动了可信人工智能和有效传播研究的发展。

Abstract: Identifying persuasive rhetorical cues is critical across domains, from detecting information manipulation and improving AI safety to advancing public health communication. We propose Persuasion Index (PI), a taxonomy of 15 dimensions grounded in persuasion theories from psychology and communication, and one transparent implementation using 55 sub-features built from lexicons and rule-based detectors. The taxonomy is modular: individual detectors can be replaced while preserving the theoretical structure. By evaluating PI on four public datasets varying in domain, style, and outcome measures, we show that PI provides a shared feature space for interpreting rhetorical patterns associated with persuasion-related outcomes. Linear models show that PI features carry meaningful predictive signal while remaining computationally lightweight. Dimension-level analyses reveal recurring associations between PI dimensions and persuasion outcomes across datasets, while also highlighting topic- and stance-specific variation. We release PI as an open-source package and web interface for principled and auditable analysis of human and AI-mediated communication.

### [108] [LoSoNA: A Benchmark for Local Social Norm Adaptation in Group Conversations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14600)
*Mateusz Winiarek,Maksymilian Bilski,Mateusz Jacniacki*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LoSoNA 是一个用于评估大语言模型在多用户聊天中适应局部社交规范能力的基准测试。该基准通过提供包含隐含社交规范的对话记录，并设计触发性问题来检验模型是否能推断并遵循这些规范。实验表明，大多数模型在简单提示下表现不佳，而显式提示有助于部分模型（如 Gemini 3.1 Pro 达到 84.2%，Claude Fable 5 达到 81.6%），但效果不一，部分模型甚至出现性能下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型在在线群聊这种具有隐性本地社交规范的环境中，缺乏对规范的理解与适应能力，亟需评估其社会交互能力。

Method: 构建 LoSoNA 基准，包含多个基于真实群聊数据的场景，每个场景由一段展示隐藏社交规范的对话和一个需要模型响应的触发句组成，通过不同提示策略（如显式提醒模型参考上下文）评估模型表现。

Result: 大多数模型在默认提示下表现有限；显式提示提升了部分先进模型的表现，其中 Gemini 3.1 Pro 达到 84.2%，Claude Fable 5 达到 81.6%，但其他模型提升不明显或出现退化。

Conclusion: LoSoNA 为评估大模型在复杂社交语境中的规范推理与适应能力提供了有效工具，揭示了当前模型在理解隐性社交规则方面的局限性，强调未来需更注重社会认知能力的训练与评估。

Abstract: Online group chats are social spaces with local conversational norms that are rarely stated explicitly. The ability and willingness of LLM-based agents to recognize and adapt to these norms remains mostly unexplored. We introduce LoSoNA, a benchmark for local social norm adaptation in multi-party chat. Each scenario gives a subject model a curated group-chat transcript in which non-subject participants demonstrate a hidden local norm, followed by a final elicitor turn that forces a response revealing whether the subject has inferred that norm. We evaluate eight frontier and open-weight models under four prompting conditions that vary how explicitly the model is told to treat the prior conversation as evidence for how it should answer. Naive prompting remains limited for most models; explicit norm-aware prompting helps unevenly, with Gemini 3.1 Pro reaching $84.2\%$ and Claude Fable 5 reaching $81.6\%$, while several other models show small gains or regressions. LoSoNA contributes to recent calls for evaluating LLM social capabilities by testing whether models can infer local conversational norms from precedent and use them in a one-turn group-chat response.

</details>


### [109] [GAGPO: Generalized Advantage Grouped Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13217)
*Siyuan Zhu,Chao Yu,Rongxin Yang,Zongkai Liu,Jinjun Hu,Qiwen Chen,Yibo Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为GAGPO的无评论家强化学习方法，用于多轮对话中精确的时间信用分配。通过从采样轨迹构建非参数分组价值代理，计算类似TD/GAE的时序优势，并递归地将结果监督回传至时间序列中的各个步骤。结合组内优势归一化和动作级重要性比率，直接从多轮轨迹中提取稳定且局部化的优化信号。在ALFWorld和WebShop上的实验表明，GAGPO优于现有强基线方法，具有更快的早期学习速度、更高的交互效率和更平稳的优化动态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多轮环境中，强化学习代理面临稀疏的轨迹级奖励问题，难以确定哪些中间动作导致成功或失败，而依赖昂贵的辅助价值模型进行信用分配存在局限性。因此需要一种无需评论家、能精准实现时间对齐信用分配的方法。

Method: 提出GAGPO方法，利用采样轨迹构建非参数分组价值代理，计算时序优势并递归传播结果监督；结合组内优势归一化与动作级重要性比率，生成稳定且局部化的优化信号。

Result: 在ALFWorld和WebShop任务上，GAGPO显著优于多个强化学习基线方法，表现出更快的早期学习、更高的交互效率和更平滑的优化过程。

Conclusion: GAGPO是一种简单但有效的多轮智能体强化学习框架，能够实现精确的时间信用分配，无需依赖额外的价值模型，适用于复杂多轮任务。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning has become a powerful paradigm for post-training large language model agents, yet credit assignment in multi-turn environments remains a challenge. Agents often receive sparse, trajectory-level rewards only at the end of an episode, making it difficult to determine which intermediate actions contributed to success or failure. As a result, propagating delayed outcomes back to individual decision steps without relying on costly auxiliary value models remains an open problem. We propose Generalized Advantage Grouped Policy Optimization (GAGPO), a critic-free reinforcement learning method for precise, step-aligned temporal credit assignment. GAGPO constructs a non-parametric grouped value proxy from sampled rollouts and uses it to compute TD/GAE-style temporal advantages, recursively propagating outcome supervision backward through time. Combined with group-wise advantage normalization and an action-level importance ratio, GAGPO extracts stable, localized optimization signals directly from multi-turn trajectories. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop show that GAGPO outperforms strong reinforcement learning baselines. Further analyses demonstrate faster early-stage learning, improved interaction efficiency, and smoother optimization dynamics, suggesting that GAGPO offers a simple yet effective framework for multi-turn agentic reinforcement learning.

</details>


### [110] [Characterizing Cultural Localization in AI-Generated Stories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14626)
*Shaily Bhatt,Supriti Vijay,Jeremiah Milbauer,Fernando Diaz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种方法来衡量人工智能生成故事时采用模板化文化本地化的程度。通过识别区分不同国家故事的词汇标记，并分析去除这些标记后剩余叙事的相似性，发现仅9-17%的词汇导致国家间差异，且剩余部分存在重复的多词序列，表明存在共享的跨文化叙事模板。同时，研究还评估了文化标记的刻板印象性和冒犯性，发现来自19个主要位于全球南方国家的文化标记平均更具冒犯性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着人工智能在全球范围内的广泛应用，对生成具有文化适应性的内容（如故事）的能力日益关注。文化本地化可分为模板化本地化（仅替换文化标记）和整体化本地化（涉及情节、价值观和主题的变化）。现有方法难以准确区分这两种方式，因此需要一种量化工具来评估生成内容中模板化本地化的程度。

Method: 识别用于区分不同国家故事的关键词汇标记；在去除这些标记后，计算剩余叙事的相似性；利用多词序列重复性判断是否存在共享的文化无关叙事模板；对文化标记进行刻板印象性和冒犯性评估。

Result: 仅9-17%的词汇导致国家间故事差异；去除这些词汇后，剩余叙事表现出高度重复的多词序列，表明存在通用叙事模板；来自19个全球南方国家的文化标记平均更具有冒犯性。

Conclusion: AI生成的故事在很大程度上依赖于模板化本地化，而非真正意义上的文化深度适配。这提示当前生成模型可能缺乏对文化内涵的深层理解，且部分文化标记存在刻板与冒犯风险，需警惕其潜在偏见与伦理问题。

Abstract: The global use of artificial intelligence has increased interest in assessing the ability to generate culturally localized content, including stories. Cultural localization in stories often occurs through either templated localization -- the use of cultural markers (e.g., names, locations) in a generic narrative -- or holistic localization -- the variation of plots, values, and themes, in addition to cultural markers. We propose a method to measure the degree to which content was generated through templated localization. Specifically, we identify the lexical tokens that distinguish stories across nationalities and measure the similarity of the narratives that remain after removing them. In stories generated by five models on 125 topics for 193 nationalities, our method is able to detect that only a small subset (9-17%) of the vocabulary accounts for the variation across nationalities and that the narratives that remain after removing them contain repeated multi-word sequences, suggesting the presence of a shared culturally-agnostic narrative template. Finally, we characterize the cultural markers for their stereotypicality and offensiveness, finding that markers from 19 countries, mostly located in the Global South, are on average offensive.

### [111] [AgentSpec: Understanding Embodied Agent Scaffolds Through Controlled Composition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14674)
*Jixuan Chen,Jianzhi Shen,Haoqiang Kang,Zhi Hong,Qingyi Jiang,Soham Bose,Yiming Zhang,Leon Leng,Amit Vyas,Lingjun Mao,Siru Ouyang,Kun Zhou,Lianhui Qin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出AgentSpec框架，用于标准化多智能体系统中感知、记忆、推理、反思、动作和学习等模块的接口，实现组件的可替换与重组，以研究模块间交互对智能体行为的影响。在多个环境上验证了该框架的有效性，发现性能主要由架构兼容性和模块间相互作用决定，而非单一模块能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体系统多为紧密耦合的流水线，难以分离各组件贡献、比较不同设计或理解模块间交互机制。需要一种模块化、标准化的框架来支持可组合、可比较的智能体研究。

Method: 设计AgentSpec框架，将智能体建模为具有标准接口的可重用策略组件的类型化组合，支持在控制条件下交换和重组组件，并在DeliveryBench、ALFRED、MiniGrid和RoboTHOR等多个环境中进行实验验证。

Result: 实验证明，智能体性能主要受架构兼容性及模块间交互效应影响；结构化的多粒度记忆有助于长时状态追踪；推理与记忆在不同环境中表现出非均匀交互；反思机制存在纠错与开销之间的权衡；强化学习训练的策略在部署时针对特定架构优化后表现最佳。

Conclusion: AgentSpec提供了一个可控的基础平台，可用于研究、比较和设计可组合的LLM智能体，推动智能体系统从黑箱式集成向模块化、可解释的设计演进。

Abstract: LLM agents are increasingly built not as single model calls, but as scaffolded systems that combine reasoning, memory, reflection, action execution, and learning. While such scaffolds often improve performance, they are often embedded in tightly coupled pipelines, making it difficult to isolate component contributions, compare alternative designs, or understand how module interactions shape agent behavior. We introduce AgentSpec, a modular specification framework that represents embodied agents as typed compositions of reusable policy components with standardized interfaces. AgentSpec standardizes the interfaces among perception, memory, reasoning, reflection, action, and optional learning, enabling components to be swapped and recombined under controlled conditions. We instantiate this framework across DeliveryBench, ALFRED, MiniGrid, and RoboTHOR, and analyze reasoning, memory, reflection, and reinforcement-learning modules across model backbones. Our results show that agent performance is governed by scaffold compatibility and interaction effects rather than isolated module strength. In particular, structured multi-granularity memory improves long-horizon state tracking, reasoning and memory interact non-uniformly across environments, reflection trades off correction and cost, and RL-trained policies compose best when optimized with deployment-time scaffold structure. AgentSpec provides a controlled foundation for studying, comparing, and designing composable LLM agents. Our code, baselines and interactive playground are publicly available at https://agentspec-embodied.github.io.

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has successfully elicited the reasoning capabilities of large language models, motivating its extension to multimodal scenarios. Existing methods primarily focus on improving the visual coverage of reasoning traces and mitigating visual hallucinations, but underestimate the semantic inconsistency between the reasoning process and the final answer. In this paper, we delve into thinking-answer inconsistency in RLVR for large vision-language models (LVLMs), showing thorough analyses of rollouts collected throughout Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) training process and post-RLVR evaluation outputs that this issue persists during training and remains present during inference. Motivated by the analysis, we propose Consistency-Oriented Reasoning Alignment (CORA), which introduces thinking-answer semantic consistency into RLVR through a lightweight plug-and-play consistency reward model, and further incorporates Hybrid Reward Advantage Splitting (HRAS) to stably coordinate task and consistency optimization. ### [113] [AdaSR: Adaptive Streaming Reasoning with Hierarchical Relative Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14694)
*Junlong Tong,Wenqi Xu,Yingqi Fan,Anhao Zhao,Xuan Lu,Yang Tan,Xiaoyu Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: AdaSR提出一种自适应流式推理框架，使大模型在输入流中动态推理并完成最终思考，通过HRPO优化分层推理过程，实现灵活的思考时机与计算分配，提升推理准确率、计算效率与流延迟的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实场景如音视频流具有动态性，传统静态推理范式不适用；现有流式推理依赖监督模仿，灵活性差，需更自适应的推理机制。

Method: 提出AdaSR框架，结合分层相对策略优化（HRPO），将策略优化分解为流式推理与深度推理阶段，通过格式、准确率和自适应思考奖励，实现细粒度优势分配与计算资源合理分配。

Result: 实验表明AdaSR在推理准确率、计算效率和流延迟之间取得更好平衡，优于监督微调基线。

Conclusion: AdaSR通过自适应流式推理与分层优化策略，有效应对动态输入场景，提升了大模型在实时流式任务中的性能与灵活性。

Abstract: Large reasoning models typically follow a read-then-think paradigm: they observe the complete input, reason over a static context, and then produce the answer. Yet many real-world scenarios are inherently dynamic, such as audio and video stream, where information arrives as a continuous stream and models must reason, update, and respond under partial observations. Recent streaming reasoning methods allow models to think while reading, but they largely rely on supervised imitation of pre-constructed trajectories, which limits their flexibility. In this paper, we propose AdaSR, an adaptive streaming reasoning framework that enables models to reason during input streaming and perform final deliberation once the stream is complete, learning when to think, and how much computation to allocate across different stages. To optimize this hierarchical reasoning process, we introduce Hierarchical Relative Policy Optimization (HRPO), which decomposes policy optimization into streaming reasoning and deep reasoning phases, providing more fine-grained advantage assignment instead of uniformly distributing a single sequence-level advantage over all tokens. HRPO integrates format, accuracy, and adaptive thinking rewards to enforce valid reasoning protocols, preserve final task performance, and encourage latency-aware computation allocation. Experiments show that AdaSR achieves a better balance among reasoning accuracy, computational efficiency, and streaming latency compared with supervised fine-tuning baseline. We release our code at https://github.com/EIT-NLP/StreamingLLM/tree/main/AdaSR.

### [114] [Can Editing 1 Neuron Fix Repetition Loops in LLMs?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13705)
*Aristotelis Lazaridis,Aman Sharma,Dylan Bates,Brian King,Vincent Lu,Jack FitzGerald*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了Gemma 4模型在长篇事实枚举任务中出现的重复循环问题，发现其根源在于少数MLP神经元或专家模块。通过微小的权重编辑（如单个符号反转）可有效消除此类循环，且不影响模型整体性能。然而，对于更复杂的‘绝望循环’（模型反复自我修正却无法得出答案），权重修改仅部分缓解，因本质是知识缺失而非可修复的电路问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大型语言模型在长篇事实列举任务中出现的重复循环现象是否可通过局部权重修改解决，以验证生成缺陷的可定位性与可修复性。

Method: 采用逐层消融、逐神经元归因分析，结合全生成扫描确认关键神经元；对识别出的异常神经元实施静态权重编辑，评估其对生成行为的影响。

Result: 小规模权重修改可有效抑制重复循环，但对知识缺失导致的非收敛性‘绝望循环’效果有限；表明某些生成问题源于知识不足，而非模型内部可修复的路径错误。

Conclusion: 权重手术可定位并消除特定生成故障，但无法弥补缺失的知识，提示模型改进需兼顾知识完整性与生成逻辑可靠性。

Abstract: Yes. Can it cure doom loops? Probably not.
  The Gemma 4 instruction-tuned models share a reproducible failure: on long factual enumeration prompts, such as listing every episode of a TV series, the 88 IAU constellations, or the 151 original Pokemon, they collapse into repetition, either a tight verbatim loop or a list whose entries decay onto a single answer. These loops occur at rates as high as 95% and survive prompt rewording, inference-engine changes, and most sampling adjustments. In this paper we explore whether this behavior is localized enough to remove by weight edits. To localize the cause, we use per-layer ablation and per-neuron attribution, then confirm the strongest candidates with full-generation sweeps. The loops trace to a small set of MLP neurons (or, in the 26B-A4B Mixture-of-Experts model, a few routed experts) which we suppress with static weight edits. These "surgeries" can be as small as a single sign-inverted neuron (in the E2B model). The size of the effective edits grows with model scale, but in all cases, the loop patterns can be addressed at normal generation budgets while preserving general-purpose benchmark scores. However, the edits do not solve everything: we also study longer thinking budgets, where the two larger models most visibly enter doom looping, i.e. a non-convergent regime in which the model self-corrects in circles over a fact it cannot recall, exhausting the budget without committing to a final answer. We show this residual failure is reduced but not eliminated by the same edits, and argue it is fundamentally a knowledge-precision problem rather than a removable circuit; weight surgery can delete a loop, but it cannot supply a missing fact. Our results are both a feasibility demonstration, that is, evidence that a concrete generation pathology can be localized to a few parameters and edited out, and a delineation of where that approach stops.

</details>


### [115] [Efficient On-Device Diffusion LLM Inference with Mobile NPU](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13740)
*Tuowei Wang,Yanfan Sun,Ju Ren*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: llada.cpp 是首个面向智能手机上扩散型大语言模型（dLLMs）的NPU感知推理框架，通过三种技术优化移动端NPUs的计算效率：多块推测解码填补后期块推理负载空缺；双路径渐进修订确保已提交令牌可回溯并避免阻塞NPU执行；交换优化内存运行时压缩NPU可见地址布局，重叠数据预加载与NPU计算以减少重映射和传输开销。在多种硬件平台和dLLM任务上评估显示，相比CPU基线，llada.cpp将LLaDA-8B生成延迟降低17x–42x，同时保持生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 移动设备上的扩散型大语言模型（dLLMs）虽能并行去噪提升生成速度，但重复去噪带来大量计算开销。现有移动神经处理单元（NPUs）虽具备高吞吐密集矩阵运算能力，却因令牌绑定导致每块有效工作量下降、令牌修订增加KV缓存复用难度、有限的NPU可见地址空间引发昂贵的数据重映射与传输开销，难以高效利用。因此亟需一种针对移动端NPU特性的dLLM推理框架。

Method: 提出llada.cpp框架，包含三项核心技术：(1) 多块推测解码：在后期当前块解码中引入推测的未来块令牌以填充缩减的工作负载；(2) 双路径渐进修订：允许已提交令牌保持可修订性，通过CPU侧路径刷新不稳定的令牌，避免阻塞NPU密集计算；(3) 交换优化内存运行时：紧凑化NPU可见地址布局，并将数据搬运与NPU计算重叠，减少重映射和数据迁移开销。

Result: 在多种硬件平台和dLLM工作负载上，llada.cpp实现了对LLaDA-8B生成延迟17倍至42倍的显著降低，相较于CPU基线，在保留生成质量的前提下大幅提升了推理效率。

Conclusion: llada.cpp成功将dLLMs的并行去噪优势与移动NPU的高性能计算能力结合，通过针对性架构设计克服了移动端推理中的关键瓶颈，为低延迟大模型生成提供了可行且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Diffusion large language models (dLLMs) accelerate generation by denoising multiple tokens in parallel, making them attractive for latency-sensitive mobile inference. However, repeated denoising introduces substantial computation on smartphones. Mobile neural processing units (NPUs) offer high-throughput dense matrix computation, but efficiently exploiting them remains challenging: token commitment shrinks per-block effective workloads, token revision complicates KV cache reuse, and limited NPU-visible address space incurs costly remapping and data transfer overheads.
  In this paper, we propose llada.cpp, the first NPU-aware inference framework for accelerating dLLMs on smartphones. llada.cpp aligns block-wise dLLM inference with the execution characteristics of mobile NPUs through three techniques. (1) Multi-Block Speculative Decoding fills the shrinking workload in late-stage current-block decoding with speculative future-block tokens. (2) Dual-Path Progressive Revision keeps committed tokens revisable until stable and refreshes unstable tokens through a CPU-side path without stalling dense NPU execution. (3) Swap-Optimized Memory Runtime compacts NPU-visible address layouts and overlaps data staging with NPU computation to reduce remapping and transfer overheads. We implement llada.cpp as an end-to-end framework and evaluate it across diverse hardware platforms and dLLM workloads. llada.cpp reduces LLaDA-8B generation latency by 17x-42x over the CPU baseline with prefix KV cache reuse, while preserving generation quality.

</details>


### [116] [High-Frequency Pricing at Scale for E-Commerce](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13741)
*Stefan Birr,Tobias Huelden,Mones Raslan,Adele Gouttes,Andreas Schmitt,Mateusz Koren,Johannes Stephan,Robert Streek,Manuel Kunz,Tim Januschowski*

Abstract: This paper presents the design, development, and implementation of a specialized forecast-then-optimize algorithmic pricing tool for sales campaigns in fashion e-commerce. ### [117] [A fully GPU-based workflow for building physics emulators of hypersonic flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13742)

Abstract: The ability to resolve complex physical phenomena with high fidelity and at low computational cost is central to addressing key challenges in modern engineering. A prime example lies in hypersonic flows, where the precise prediction of the full flowfield topology, in particular with respect to shock wave location and intensity, is critical. Yet supersonic and hypersonic flows continue to be a stumbling block for traditional reduced-order models and neural emulators that struggle to capture steep gradients in flow states with physical consistency in applications of industrial relevance. To that end, we introduce a fully GPU based workflow that integrates accelerated data generation with the training of neural emulators augmented by uncertainty quantification and physics-aware refinement. Our workflow is enabled by a differentiable high-fidelity solver (JAX-Fluids) which we employ for rapid dataset creation and residual-based improvement of the neural emulator to enhance physical consistency. Building on this framework, we first present a suite of model architectures and analyze their scaling behavior to expose their strengths and shortcomings. We then show that residual-based refinement enables training on cases where only mesh and input parameters are available, substantially reducing residuals and improving physical consistency. Together, differentiable simulation and residual-based refinement yield physics emulators that remain reliable beyond their training distribution, a key requirement for deploying surrogates in real-world engineering design loops.

### [118] [FedSPC: Shared Parameter Correction for Personalized Federated Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13748)
*Kannanthodath Induchoodan Ajay Menon,Christian Prehofer,Yunfei Xu,Toru Hirano*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FedSPC 是一种用于个性化联邦学习（PFL）的模块化修正方法，通过仅对共享参数应用控制变量修正，解决因客户端优化不同局部目标导致的共享更新不一致问题。该方法可集成到多种PFL设置中，并在多个数据集和模型上显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决个性化联邦学习中共享参数因客户端优化目标差异导致的更新不一致问题，从而削弱共享表示能力。

Method: 提出FedSPC，采用控制变量修正仅作用于共享参数，保持个性化参数不变，适用于共享特征提取器、共享分类器及全共享模型等常见PFL设置。

Result: 在CIFAR-100和Tiny-ImageNet上，使用ViT、ResNet-34和VGG-11进行实验，表明FedSPC在多个代表性PFL方法（如FedPer、FedRep、FedBABU、LG-FedAvg、Ditto）中均有效提升性能。

Abstract: Personalized federated learning (PFL) is one of the important approaches in federated learning for addressing statistical heterogeneity while enabling client-specific adaptation. Many PFL methods split the model into shared and personalized parameters, which are jointly trained on each client. However, this creates an optimization issue: shared parameters are updated by clients optimizing different local objectives, which can lead to inconsistent shared updates and weaken the shared representation. To address this problem, we propose Federated Shared Parameter Correction (FedSPC), a modular correction method for PFL. FedSPC applies control-variate correction only to the shared parameters of a given PFL method, while leaving personalized parameters unchanged. It can be integrated into three common PFL settings: shared feature extractors, shared classifiers, and fully shared models with local regularization. Experiments on CIFAR-100 and Tiny-ImageNet with ViT, ResNet-34, and VGG-11 show that FedSPC improves performance across representative PFL methods, including FedPer, FedRep, FedBABU, LG-FedAvg, and Ditto.

### [119] [The Weight Norm Sets the Grokking Timescale: A Causal Delay Law](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13753)
*Truong Xuan Khanh,Doan Hoang Viet,Luu Duc Trung,Phan Thanh Duc*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过干预神经网络训练过程中的权重范数，解决了关于权重范数是否导致神经网络延迟泛化（grokking）的争议。实验发现，在自由训练下，当权重范数达到一个几乎不变的临界值Wc时，网络会经历grokking；而当范数被固定在某个倍数rho×Wc时，虽然仍会发生grokking，但延迟时间T_grok随rho呈指数增长（比例系数alpha≈7.5，R²=0.996）。这表明权重范数对grokking延迟有决定性影响。此外，若移除层归一化（LayerNorm），这种指数依赖关系重新出现，说明层归一化通过解耦权重尺度与网络函数，抑制了该效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究权重范数是否是导致神经网络延迟泛化（grokking）的关键因素，现有研究对此存在分歧：部分研究认为存在一个临界范数，另一些则观察到无固定范数下的grokking。因此需要通过主动干预范数而非仅观测，来厘清其作用机制。

Method: 在不同模数条件下，分别采用自由训练（带权重衰减）和固定范数（钳制范数至rho×Wc）两种策略，系统地改变学习率、初始范数和层归一化结构，记录网络开始泛化的延迟时间，并分析其与范数的关系。同时通过引入或移除层归一化，验证其对范数依赖性的调节作用。

Result: 在自由训练中，权重范数达到稳定临界值Wc时发生grokking，且该值在不同随机种子和学习率下变化极小（CV 1-2%）。当范数被钳制于rho×Wc时，延迟时间T_grok随rho呈指数增长，指数系数alpha≈7.5，跨四种模数拟合良好（R²=0.996）。范数钳制的影响远大于学习率变化（约19倍对比2倍）。保持范数高于Wc虽延缓但不阻止grokking。移除层归一化后，指数依赖关系恢复。

Conclusion: 权重范数是控制grokking延迟的核心机制之一。当范数被固定时，延迟遵循指数规律，与自由收缩范数的对数延迟形成互补。层归一化可通过解耦权重尺度与网络功能，消除这种依赖，揭示了归一化技术在动态训练行为中的关键作用。

Abstract: Grokking is the delayed onset of generalization in neural networks, arising long after they fit the training data. Whether the weight norm causes this delay is disputed: some studies report a critical norm at the transition, others observe grokking with no fixed norm at all. We settle this by intervening on the norm during training rather than only observing it. Under free training with weight decay, networks grok when the weight norm reaches a value Wc that varies little across seeds and learning rates (CV 1 to 2 percent) and grows with the modular base as a power law. When we instead clamp the norm to a fixed multiple rho of Wc and hold it there, the network still groks, but the delay follows T_grok proportional to exp(alpha rho). One exponent, alpha near 7.5, fits this delay across four moduli (R^2 = 0.996). Over the swept ranges the held norm moves the delay by about 19x and the learning rate by only about 2x, and holding the norm above Wc slows grokking rather than preventing it. A final LayerNorm removes the dependence by decoupling weight scale from the network function; without it the exponential law returns. This pinned-norm delay is the exponential counterpart to the logarithmic delay predicted for a freely contracting norm.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing machine learning and deep learning methods for anomaly detection require large labeled datasets, have high computational costs, and face scalability issues in edge and high-dimensional settings. There is a need for efficient, interpretable, and low-latency anomaly detection frameworks suitable for real-time and resource-limited applications such as IoT and TinyML.

Method: D2H-AD leverages Hyperdimensional Computing by representing data using high-dimensional distributed vectors. It introduces a unified framework combining distance-based similarity and density-aware encoding for enhanced anomaly representation. The method enables binary computations, compact memory usage, and low-latency inference, making it ideal for edge deployment.

Result: D2H-AD achieves up to 5.4% higher ROC-AUC than direct density-distance scoring in original feature space. It consistently outperforms HDAD, ODHD, One-Class SVM, Isolation Forest, and Autoencoders across all datasets. Abstract: Anomaly detection is a fundamental component of intelligent systems with applications in healthcare, cybersecurity, smart grids, and IoT environments. This paper presents D2H-AD, a novel anomaly detection framework based on Hyperdimensional Computing (HDC), a brain-inspired paradigm that represents information using high-dimensional distributed vectors. Unlike existing HDC-based methods, D2H-AD integrates distance-based similarity and density-aware encoding within a unified framework, improving anomaly representation and detection performance. Ablation studies show that hyperdimensional encoding alone yields up to 5.4% higher ROC-AUC than applying the same density-distance scoring directly in the original feature space. Furthermore, D2H-AD consistently outperforms five established baselines, namely HDAD, ODHD, One-Class SVM, Isolation Forest, and Autoencoders, across all evaluated datasets. The framework is lightweight, interpretable, and computationally efficient, making it suitable for resource-constrained and real-time applications. We validate D2H-AD on five benchmark datasets and demonstrate superior F1-score and ROC-AUC performance, together with robustness to class imbalance, noise, and data complexity. In addition to improved accuracy, D2H-AD offers scalability, a small memory footprint, and low-latency operation enabled by binary computations and a compact design. These properties make it particularly attractive for TinyML and edge AI deployments. The proposed framework highlights the potential of HDC for accurate, interpretable, and energy-efficient anomaly detection in dynamic environments.

### [121] [Beyond LoRA: Is Sparsity-Induced Adaptation Better?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13767)
*Elijah Cadenhead,Cristian McGee,Xin Li,El Houcine Bergou,Aritra Dutta*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨了低秩适应（LoRA）及其变体在参数高效微调（PEFT）中的表现，提出通过引入稀疏性改进现有LoRA方法，如Cheap LoRA（cLA）、单低秩因子训练及链式循环变体${c}^3$LA。研究从信息论角度推导了这些方法的泛化误差界，并在10个预训练模型和14个数据集上评估了11种微调方法，结果表明稀疏结构化的低秩更新在保持性能的同时显著降低计算开销（最高节省15%显存、10%训练时间），且理论与实证分析提供了更一致、更合理的成本效益评估框架。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LoRA及其变体虽高效，但其泛化能力与结构限制对性能的影响尚不清晰；如何在不牺牲性能的前提下进一步提升效率并提供可解释的理论支持，是亟待解决的问题。

Method: 提出三种基于稀疏性的新方法：cLA（结构化非对称LoRA）、单低秩因子训练（确定或随机）、以及${c}^3$LA（链式循环）。结合信息论推导泛化误差边界，并通过损失景观、谱分析等工具进行多维度实证评估。

Conclusion: 通过在低秩更新中引入稀疏性和结构化约束，可在保持强泛化能力的同时显著降低资源消耗，为高效微调提供了更具原则性的设计路径。

Abstract: Low-rank adaptation (LoRA) and its variants provide a memory- and compute-efficient alternative to full fine-tuning of pre-trained models. However, questions remain about the comparative generalizability of these approaches and how the structural restrictions on low-rank updates preserve effective adaptation performance. We present a historical framing, covering the past (full fine-tuning and original LoRA), the present (different variants of LoRA), and propose simpler, cheaper, parameter-efficient extensions by inducing sparsity within existing LoRA variants: Cheap LoRA (cLA), training a single low-rank factor with the other fixed (deterministically or, in its randomized variant, stochastically), and the chained circulant variant, ${c}^3$LA. We frame cLA as a structured instance of asymmetric LoRA, serving as a controlled column-subspace restriction of full fine-tuning. We derive information-theoretic generalization error bounds for these variants, marking one of the first endeavors in this area. Empirically, we evaluate 11 fine-tuning methods across 10 pre-trained models and 14 datasets, analyzing the fine-tuned models' performance and generalization using tools such as loss landscapes and spectral analysis. Despite the sensitivity of fine-tuned models to the pre-trained model, datasets, and other factors, our study suggests that restricting LoRA-based PEFT methods' adaptation to a sparse, structured column space remains competitive across tasks with their parameter-matched baselines while reducing up to 10% training time and peak GPU memory up to 15%, even with a naïve, non-optimized, sparse implementation. Our theoretical and empirical generalization measures provide a more consistent and principled approach to their cost-effective adaptation than commonly used analytical tools. Overview and code are available at: https://elicaden.github.io/Beyond_LoRA/.

### [122] [Diffusion Policy Optimization without Drifting Apart](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13795)
*Haozhe Jiang,Haiwen Feng,Pieter Abbeel,Jiantao Jiao,Angjoo Kanazawa,Nika Haghtalab*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出DiPOD框架，通过在每次扩散策略梯度更新中引入在线策略ELBO正则项，实现自蒸馏与策略更新的交替，维持紧界行为。

Result: 在扩散语言模型后训练和连续控制任务中，DiPOD显著提升了训练稳定性，并获得比先前方法更高的奖励表现。

Conclusion: DiPOD通过保持紧密的代理边界，有效解决了扩散策略优化中的双漂移问题，是一种简单且高效的实用算法。

Abstract: RL post-training has become increasingly pivotal for improving diffusion policies, but existing diffusion policy-gradient methods are often unstable and cannot achieve reliable policy improvement. We identify the cause as the double-drift phenomenon: optimizing a variational surrogate can let the ELBO separate from the true log-likelihood, which then makes the resulting proxy policy gradient misaligned with the true policy gradient of expected return. We propose \textbf{DiPOD}, a diffusion policy optimization framework that maintains tight-bound behavior throughout training by interleaving self-distillation with policy-improving gradient updates. This leads to a simple and practical algorithm: augmenting each diffusion policy-gradient update with an on-policy ELBO regularizer. Across diffusion language model post-training and continuous-control diffusion policies, DiPOD substantially stabilizes training and reaches higher rewards than previous methods.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分析在修改输入与原始输入下激活值的协方差，评估不同类型的噪声结构对网络鲁棒性的影响。

Abstract: Neural responses in cortex exhibit substantial trial-to-trial variability in response to repeated stimuli, while peripheral sensory neurons respond far more consistently, leading many to wonder whether stochasticity may carry meaning. Existing work has argued that noise and signal correlations may be optimized for discrimination in animals, whereas artificial neural network (ANN) studies have shown similar benefits of noise in machine learning tasks, although most ANN work has neglected the effects of correlations. Here we investigate whether correlated noise improves the robustness of artificial neural networks to adversarial attacks and naturalistic image modifications. Using the covariance of activations under modified versus clean inputs, we find that structured noise may significantly improve network robustness. Robustness to naturalistic image modifications benefits most from structure, but this structure transfers poorly across modification types. In contrast, noise structure from adversarial attacks can generalize to other kinds of attacks. These results suggest that structured noise in ANN activations generally improves robustness, establishing a biologically plausible strategy for creating robust artificial neural networks that only relies on local information.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在许多工业和科学应用中，强制执行如单调性和凸性等函数不等式约束是一个基本挑战。传统的一侧惩罚方法和基于互补松驰的原始对偶方法仅在违反位置提供约束梯度，导致约束满足性脆弱；而通过构造保证可行性的架构则受限于简单情况并引入额外归纳偏置。

Method: 引入神经松弛变量，通过主网络与联合学习的辅助网络耦合，使约束强制转化为回归问题。辅助网络作为主网络约束量的有效目标，诱导可行性与规则性。

Result: 在密集网格的单调性和凸性测试中实现零测量违规，显著优于惩罚和原始对偶基线方法；成功应用于无套利波动率曲面学习，解决量化金融中的一个开放挑战。

Conclusion: 神经松弛变量提供了一种有效、鲁棒且无需额外归纳偏置的约束强制方法，在复杂约束场景下表现出色，适用于实际工业应用。

Abstract: Enforcing functional inequality constraints such as monotonicity and convexity in neural networks is a fundamental challenge in many industrial and scientific applications. Classical one-sided penalty methods, along with primal-dual methods gated by complementary slackness, provide constraint gradients only at violated locations, resulting in fragile satisfaction. Architectures that guarantee feasibility by construction, on the other hand, remain largely limited to elementary cases and impose additional inductive biases. We introduce neural slack variables, a deep learning native primal-side approach that converts constraint enforcement into a regression problem by coupling the primary network with a jointly learned auxiliary network. The auxiliary network serves as a valid target for the primary network's constraint quantities, inducing feasibility and regularity. Neural slack variables achieve zero measured violations on dense-grid monotonicity and convexity test cases, where penalty and primal-dual baselines leave residual violations, and enable arbitrage-free learning of volatility surfaces, an open industrial challenge in quantitative finance.

Abstract: This thesis investigates how Bayesian principles can deepen our understanding of modern deep learning systems. While neural networks achieve remarkable predictive performance, their ability to generalize and to quantify uncertainty remains only partly understood. This thesis approaches this challenge from both methodological and theoretical angles: unifying Bayesian inference, function-space modeling, and large-deviation theory under a common probabilistic perspective.
  On the methodological side, the thesis introduces the Deep Variational Implicit Process (DVIP), a scalable Bayesian framework that extends implicit processes to deep architectures. Complementing this, two post-hoc methods -- the Variational Linearized Laplace Approximation (VaLLA) and the Fixed-Mean Gaussian Process (FMGP) -- are proposed to equip pretrained deterministic networks with calibrated uncertainty estimates.
  The theoretical contributions focus on one of the central open questions in modern machine learning: why do large, over-parameterized neural networks generalize so well? To address this, the thesis develops a unified probabilistic framework that connects three key mechanisms -- diversity, smoothness, and stochasticity -- within the language of PAC-Bayesian and large-deviation theory.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将IPTB估计问题重构为未观测个体治疗效应符号的二分类任务，利用协变量相似性进行成对比较生成伪标签，并通过注意力机制或核回归进行聚合，支持多个离散剂量水平。

Abstract: Estimating the probability that a treatment outperforms a control for an individual patient, called the Individual Probability of Treatment Benefit (IPTB), offers a clinically intuitive alternative to population-average metrics. However, existing methods for IPTB estimation are largely confined to binary treatment settings, despite the prevalence of dose-varying interventions in clinical practice. We propose a general framework for IPTB estimation with ordinal outcomes under discrete dose assignments, called Dose-AIPTB (Dose Attention-based IPTB). Our approach recasts the problem as binary classification over the unobserved sign of the individual treatment effect, constructing pseudo-labels from covariate-similar pairwise comparisons and aggregating them via attention mechanisms or Nadaraya-Watson kernel regression. This formulation naturally accommodates multiple discrete dose levels, extending beyond the binary treatment paradigm. Through numerical experiments on real-world and synthetic data under covariate shift, varying sample sizes, and heterogeneous outcomes, we demonstrate that attention-based aggregation consistently outperforms kernel alternatives. The framework provides a foundation for personalized dose selection grounded in individual-level benefit probabilities. Codes implementing the model are publicly available at https://github.com/NTAILab/AIPTBDose.

### [127] [A Stationarity-and-Coupling Criterion for Training-Free Time-Lagged Spectral Embeddings of Multivariate Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13823)
*Siddharth Pal,Viktoria Rojkova*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究无需训练的固定长度多变量时间序列描述符，提出一个可验证的适用性准则。核心贡献不在于描述符 $D(τ)$ 本身，而在于其适用条件：当信号近似平稳且类别信息体现在跨通道时序耦合而非单通道功率时，$D(τ)$ 才有效。通过理论推导得出三个结论：可区分性条件、静态协方差（τ=0）退化为随机水平、以及仅靠功率差异的平稳范式会破坏该描述符。提出了一个两步预检测试——增强型Dickey-Fuller平稳性检验与功率基线饱和检验——可在无训练前提前预测适用性。在满足条件的四个数据集（Sleep-EDF, BCI-IV-2a, MIT-BIH, ESC-50）上表现媲美强基线，成本极低，在单线程下于Sleep-EDF上达到88.5±4.5%准确率；而在违反条件的三个非平稳或功率主导的场景中，其失败与预测一致，反而是更具信息量的结果。强调 $D(τ)$ 并非最精确表示，其价值在于紧凑、免训练且适用范围事先可知。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法多依赖训练，难以预知适用边界。本文旨在探索一种无需训练的固定长度描述符是否可用，并明确其何时能工作，从而提供可验证的适用性判断标准。

Method: 基于平稳高斯VAR(1)模型，构建从时滞相关矩阵截断至Marchenko-Pastur边缘的特征值选择机制，保留信号成分；利用余弦相似度对类别中心进行分类，零参数设计。提出并验证两阶段预检流程：增强型Dickey-Fuller检验（检测平稳性）和功率基线饱和检验（检测功率主导性）。

Result: 在满足适用性条件的四类数据集上，$D(τ)$ 表现优于或媲美有训练的强基线，准确率达88.5±4.5%（睡眠数据集，20人留一法），且仅需单线程运行；在三类违反条件的数据中，其性能完全失效，与预判一致，反证了准则的有效性。

Conclusion: $D(τ)$ 的价值不在于最高精度，而在于其紧凑、免训练特性及其适用范围可预先确定。本文提出的适用性准则具有操作性，为描述符的选择提供了理论依据与实践指导。

Abstract: We study training-free fixed-length descriptors for multivariate time series and ask not merely whether such a descriptor performs well, but when it can be expected to work at all. Our object of study is $D(τ)$, built from a time-lagged correlation matrix truncated at the Marchenko-Pastur edge so that only signal-bearing eigenvalues survive and classified by cosine similarity to class centroids with zero learned parameters. The central contribution is not the descriptor but a falsifiable applicability criterion for it. Working from a stationary Gaussian VAR(1) model, we argue that $D(τ)$ separates two classes when the signals are approximately stationary and the class information lives in their cross-channel temporal coupling rather than in marginal per-channel power. We derive, semi-formally, three consequences: a distinguishability condition, why the static ($τ=0$) covariance collapses to chance, and why a stationary but power-discriminated paradigm defeats the descriptor. The criterion is operational: a two-part pre-flight test -- an augmented Dickey-Fuller stationarity check and a power-baseline saturation check -- predicts applicability before any training. We validate both halves on a mixed assortment. On four paradigms that satisfy the criterion (Sleep-EDF, BCI-IV-2a, MIT-BIH, ESC-50) the descriptor is competitive with strong baselines at a fraction of their cost, reaching $88.5\pm4.5\%$ under 20-subject leave-one-subject-out on Sleep-EDF on a single CPU thread. On three that violate it -- non-stationary ERPs, and financial-volatility and wearable-stress regimes that are power-discriminated -- it fails exactly as the pre-flight predicts, and these negatives are the more informative half. We are explicit that $D(τ)$ is not the most accurate representation; its value is a compact, training-free embedding whose domain of validity is known in advance.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将连续的CoT token对压缩为单一潜在表示，并通过轻量级多标记预测（MTP）模块每步解码两个标记，从而在保持训练阶段离散标记监督的同时提升推理效率。结合置信度自适应机制，在不确定时回退至标准解码以保障可靠性。

Conclusion: SuperThoughts有效平衡了推理效率与准确性，通过潜在空间压缩与多标记预测，在不牺牲性能的前提下大幅降低长链推理的计算开销，适用于大规模复杂问题求解。

Abstract: Long Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning improves LLM problem-solving but is computationally expensive due to sequential token generation. While recent works explore reasoning in continuous latent spaces to bypass discrete token generation, they often struggle with training stability and fail to scale to complex, long-horizon tasks due to lack of supervision signal. We propose SuperThoughts, which compresses pairs of consecutive CoT tokens into single latent representations and decodes two tokens per step via a lightweight Multi-Token Prediction (MTP) module. This preserves discrete token supervision at training time while doubling throughput at inference time. We finetune Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B-Instruct, Qwen2.5-Math-7B-Instruct, Qwen2.5-Math-14B-Instruct, and evaluate on MATH500, AMC, OlympiadBench, and GPQA-Diamond. With a confidence-based adaptive mechanism that falls back to standard decoding when uncertain, SuperThoughts achieves $\sim$20--30\% CoT length reduction while maintaining accuracy with minimal degradation (1-2 points accuracy drop on most tasks).

### [129] [Muon$^p$: Muon with Fractional Spectral Powers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13867)
*Yihe Dong,Will Sawin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Muon$^p$ 是一种新型优化器，通过引入分数阶谱幂更新 $US^pV^	op$（$p \in (0,1)$）在 Muon 和梯度下降之间进行插值，保留了奇异值信息以提升微调性能。研究证明分数阶谱幂无法通过固定的一元多项式迭代计算，并提出了基于低阶奇数双变量递推的近似方法，仅使用矩阵乘法，保持了 Muon 的计算结构与复杂度。实验表明，Muon$^p$ 在百亿规模模型微调中显著提升验证困惑度和下游任务表现；同时分析了其适用边界，揭示了保留奇异谱在特定谱几何条件下带来的收益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有优化器 Muon 通过完全平坦化奇异谱丢弃了可能对自适应重要的奇异值信息。为平衡谱平滑与信息保留，需要一种可调节的谱处理机制，从而在优化过程中更灵活地利用奇异值结构。

Method: 提出分数阶谱幂更新 $US^pV^	op$（$p \in (0,1)$），设计低阶奇数双变量递推关系以近似该操作，仅依赖矩阵乘法实现，保持原有计算效率；理论分析其在 Schatten $q$-norm（$q=1+1/p$）下最大化线性损失改进。

Result: Muon$^p$ 在大规模模型微调任务中显著优于基线，提升验证困惑度与下游性能；理论证明其在特定范数下最优；揭示了保留奇异谱在特定谱几何结构下的有效性边界。

Conclusion: Muon$^p$ 提供了一种兼顾计算效率与谱信息保留的优化框架，为理解奇异谱在优化中的作用提供了新视角，并在实际应用中展现出显著优势。

Abstract: Muon is an increasingly widely used optimizer that replaces a gradient $G=USV^\top$ with its polar factor $UV^\top$, thereby flattening the singular spectrum. However, full flattening discards singular-value information that may matter for adaptation. We introduce Muon$^p$, a Muon-style optimizer that instead uses fractional spectral-power updates $US^pV^\top$ for rational $p\in(0,1)$, interpolating between Muon and gradient descent. To make it practical, we prove that fractional spectral powers cannot be computed by any fixed univariate polynomial iteration, and furthermore derive low-degree odd bivariate recurrences that approximate $US^pV^\top$ using only matrix multiplications, preserving Muon's matrix-multiplication-only structure and compute complexity. We show that Muon$^p$ maximizes the linear improvement in loss under the Schatten $q$-norm for $q=1+\frac{1}{p}$. Empirically, Muon$^p$ is especially effective for finetuning: on billion-scale models, Muon$^p$ improves validation perplexity and downstream task performance. We further analyze when Muon$^p$ is less suitable, through the lens of spectral geometry. Our results reveal important insights on when preserving the singular spectrum can bring significant gains, and introduce a principled way to achieve them.

### [130] [Natively Unlearnable Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13873)
*Gaurav R. Ghosal,Pratyush Maini,Aditi Raghunathan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: NULLs 是一种新型大模型架构，通过共享骨干神经元与稀疏激活的“数据池”（sinks）实现源级可遗忘性。训练时，特定来源的信息自然聚集在对应sink中，而跨源共享信息则积累在骨干网络中。部署时仅需关闭某来源对应的sink即可实现无梯度、无需原始数据的高效去学习，且能保持模型整体性能。该方法成功应用于约600万篇维基百科文章，单篇文章去学习后仍保留相关语义知识，效果接近从头训练。同时，NULLs对对抗提取和反向重学具有鲁棒性，且语言能力与标准Transformer相当，证明了源级可遗忘性可天然融入大模型训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有去学习方法难以分离不同训练数据源的贡献，因各源信息在模型中高度纠缠；若强行隔离则阻碍联合学习。需要一种既能分离源贡献又不牺牲共享表示学习优势的新范式。

Method: 提出NULLs框架：包含共享骨干神经元和一组稀疏激活的源专属数据池（sinks）。训练过程中，每篇文档的信息自动流入其对应sink，共享知识则集中在骨干网络。部署时通过禁用特定源的sink实现无梯度、无需原始数据的去学习。

Result: NULLs成功扩展至600万维基百科文章规模，单篇去学习后保留语义关联知识，效果接近从头训练；对对抗性知识提取和反向重学具备鲁棒性；在下游任务上语言能力与标准Transformer持平。

Conclusion: 源级去学习不必作为事后补救措施，可通过NULLs等原生设计嵌入大模型训练过程，在保证共享表示学习优势的同时实现高效、安全的可控遗忘。

Abstract: Unlearning aims to remove the influence of specific training data sources, but this has proved challenging because the contributions of different sources are entangled within the model. Isolating source contributions to disjoint parameters makes removal easier, though it obstructs joint learning across sources. We propose NULLs (Natively Unlearnable LLMs), a model class that satisfies the two opposing goals of isolating source-specific contributions and learning jointly across sources, by training a set of shared backbone neurons alongside a pool of sparsely activated sinks. During training, information specific to a source naturally concentrates in its sinks while information shared across sources accumulates in the backbone. A source is then unlearned at deployment by disabling its corresponding sinks, with no gradient updates and no access to the retained data. We show that NULLs scales to Wikipedia's ~6M articles, isolating each as an independent source. Unlearning a single article removes knowledge specific to it while preserving facts shared with semantically related articles, closely matching retraining from scratch. We note that unlearning with NULLs is also robust: in a case study of unlearning the Harry Potter books, NULLs resists both adversarial extraction and relearning that reverses post-hoc unlearning. Finally, NULLs preserves general language capabilities, matching a standard transformer on downstream benchmarks. Together, these results suggest that source-level unlearning need not be an afterthought. It can be built natively into LLM training while retaining the benefits of shared representation learning.

</details>

*Bright Kwaku Manu,Beckett Sterner,Petar Jevtic*
