### [174] [Flood and Harvest: The Provable Necessity of Trivia for Generating Valuable Mathematics via the Lens of Language Generation in the Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14688)
*Xiaoyu Li,Andi Han,Dai Shi,Zheng Gao,Jiaojiao Jiang,Junbin Gao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在形式数学生成中，如何在验证器（proof checker）约束下生成具有价值的数学内容。核心问题在于：验证器虽能确保形式正确性，但无法判断内容的价值；因此需在可验证语言 $F$ 中识别出真正有价值的子集 $H$。研究提出四点结论：1）验证器不具备审美能力，其生成能力与无验证器模型一致，由Angluin条件刻画；2）验证器能实现可靠覆盖——即覆盖所有未见的有价值命题，且仅输出有效陈述；3）关键发现是存在一个尖锐的二分现象：若生成器只允许有限数量的平凡内容，则最优覆盖率为 $\alpha/2$；而一旦允许无限数量的平凡内容（即使速率趋于零），覆盖率跃升至 $1-\alpha/2$（两者均紧致），且存在单一生成器可同时达到两端；4）该现象在数学压缩模型中可被实例化。结论表明：完美验证器无法替代人类品味，因为为了覆盖未记录的有价值内容，必须产生无限但渐近可忽略的正确但无价值的陈述，这是不可避免的数学必然性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI系统能大规模生成形式化数学，但验证器只能检查形式正确性，无法判断数学价值，导致生成内容的价值瓶颈成为主要限制。如何在保证形式正确性的前提下最大化生成有价值数学的比例，成为核心挑战。

Method: 通过构建一个嵌套语言生成模型，将有价值的数学语言 $H$ 视为隐藏于可验证语言 $F$ 中的子集，利用对抗性枚举核心集合 $C \subseteq H$ 的密度 $\alpha$ 来建模文献规模。研究引入验证器作为成员查询预言机，分析不同生成策略下的覆盖性能，并基于形式逻辑与概率推导，对生成器的平凡输出数量进行分类分析，揭示覆盖率与平凡内容数量之间的非连续转变。

Result: 1）验证器不具审美，其生成能力受限于无验证器模型；2）验证器可实现可靠覆盖，避免虚假陈述，仅将错误转移至平凡陈述；3）存在一个尖锐的二分现象：有限平凡输出时最优覆盖为 $\alpha/2$，无限平凡输出时跃升至 $1-\alpha/2$，二者皆紧致；4）该现象在数学压缩模型中可实现。最终证明：无限但渐近可忽略的正确但无价值陈述是覆盖未记录有价值内容的必要代价。

Conclusion: 验证器不能替代人类对数学价值的判断。在形式化数学生成中，为了覆盖未被记录的有价值命题，必须接受无限量但渐近可忽略的正确但无价值输出，这是不可规避的理论结果，而非工程缺陷。

Abstract: AI systems coupled to proof assistants now generate formal mathematics at scale, and the gap between what a checker can verify and what a mathematician would value has become the binding constraint. We model the generation of valuable mathematics as nested language generation in the limit: a verifiable formal language $F$, accessed through a membership oracle (the proof checker), contains an unknown valuable language $H \in \mathcal{H}$ revealed only through an adversarial enumeration of a core $C \subseteq H$ of exact density $α$ (the literature). Every output is valuable ($\in H$), trivial ($\in F \setminus H$), or a hallucination ($\notin F$). We settle four questions. First, the verifier is not taste: the collections admitting generation with breadth are exactly those of the oracle-free model, characterized fiber-wise by Angluin's condition. Second, the verifier does buy sound coverage, covering all unseen valuable statements while asserting only valid ones: possible with it, impossible without it; it relocates unavoidable errors from false to trivial. Third, and centrally, a sharp dichotomy on the tight family: generators emitting finitely many trivia achieve optimal coverage $α/2$, while any infinite trivia allowance, even at vanishing rate, jumps the optimum to $1-α/2$ (both tight, for cores presented as the candidate intersection), and one generator attains both ends. The transition is in trivia count, not rate; the gap $1-α$ is the unrecorded mass. Fourth, both regimes instantiate in a compression model of mathematics. A perfect verifier cannot substitute for taste: the unbounded stream of correct-but-worthless statements is not an engineering accident but a provable necessity, since covering unrecorded valuable mathematics requires an infinite, but asymptotically negligible, stream of certified trivia.

</details>


### [175] [SemPiper: Interactive Code Synthesis for Semantic Operators in Machine Learning Pipelines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14361)
*Olga Ovcharenko,Luciano Duarte,Sebastian Schelter*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SemPipes 是一种新的编程模型，通过声明式、基于大语言模型（LLM）的语义数据操作符扩展机器学习（ML）管道。它允许开发者用自然语言指定数据操作，同时无缝集成标准数据科学库中的任意Python代码。在管道训练时，系统根据数据特征和上下文合成专用实现，从而实现灵活且可控的LLM能力整合。演示工具SemPiper提供交互式界面，可视化计算图、生成的操作符实现及优化轨迹，支持用户修改管道、查看代码并观察操作符的合成与迭代优化过程。该方法显著提升了ML管道开发的可控制性、可优化性和生产适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ML管道开发涉及复杂的数据准备、特征工程和异构数据源集成，过程繁琐且易出错。尽管大语言模型在编程辅助方面表现良好，但传统的基于聊天的接口缺乏对管道行为的控制，生成的代码难以优化或集成到生产系统中。因此需要一种既能利用LLM能力，又能保证可控性、可优化性和生产可用性的新方法。

Method: 提出SemPipes编程模型，引入声明式语义数据操作符，通过自然语言指令描述数据操作；在管道训练阶段，基于数据集特征和上下文自动合成专用实现；结合演化搜索算法优化操作符性能；通过SemPiper交互界面可视化计算图、合成过程和优化轨迹。

Result: SemPipes成功实现了将自然语言指令转化为可执行、可优化、可集成的ML管道操作；实验表明，其生成的代码具有良好的可控性与生产适用性；用户可通过交互界面灵活修改、调试和优化管道，显著提升开发效率与质量。

Conclusion: SemPipes通过融合声明式语义操作符与自动化合成机制，为机器学习管道开发提供了更高效、可控且可优化的新范式，使大语言模型的能力能够以安全、可管理的方式融入实际生产流程。

Abstract: Machine learning (ML) pipelines require extensive data preparation, feature engineering, and integration across heterogeneous sources, making them tedious and error-prone to develop. While large language models (LLMs) have recently shown promise for assisting programming tasks, chat-based interfaces provide limited control over pipeline behavior and often produce code that is difficult to optimize or integrate into production systems. We demonstrate SemPipes, a novel programming model that extends ML pipelines with declarative, LLM-powered semantic data operators. SemPipes allows developers to specify high-level natural language instructions for data-centric operations, while seamlessly combining these operators with arbitrary Python code from standard data science libraries. For the semantic operators, it synthesizes specialized implementations at pipeline training time, conditioned on dataset characteristics and pipeline context, enabling the flexible yet controlled integration of LLM capabilities. We demonstrate SemPipes through SemPiper, an interactive interface that visualizes computational graphs of the pipelines, synthesized operator implementations, and optimization trajectories produced by an evolutionary search procedure. Attendees can explore three end-to-end scenarios, modify pipelines, inspect generated code, and observe how semantic operators are synthesized and iteratively optimized. The demonstration highlights how declarative semantic operators enable controllable, optimizable, and practical integration of LLMs into ML pipeline development.

</details>


### [176] [Persona-Pruner: Sculpting Lightweight Models for Role-Playing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14695)
*Jinsu Kim,Jihoon Tack,Noah Lee,Jongheon Jeong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出Persona-Pruner框架，通过从单个角色描述中提取特定于角色的子网络，实现轻量级角色扮演模型的构建。实验表明，相比现有最先进的大语言模型剪枝技术，该方法在保持角色扮演性能方面显著更优，使性能下降减少高达93.8%（以RoleBench中的LLM-as-a-judge得分为基准），同时仍保留通用大模型能力。代码已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语言模型在角色扮演应用中表现出色，但在大规模真实场景（如多个非玩家角色同时交互）中存在计算成本过高的问题。作者质疑为单一角色分配完整通用模型是否必要，认为角色身份仅需模型总容量的一小部分，但现有剪枝方法无法区分冗余知识与核心角色特征，导致性能严重下降。

Method: 提出Persona-Pruner框架，通过分析角色描述，识别并提取与特定角色相关的子网络，从而构建轻量化、专注的角色扮演模型，避免对通用能力的过度破坏。

Result: 在多种评估指标下，Persona-Pruner显著优于现有剪枝方法，在保持角色扮演一致性的同时大幅降低计算开销；在RoleBench的LLM-as-a-judge得分上，性能损失比最强基线减少93.8%；且模型仍具备一定的通用语言理解与生成能力。

Conclusion: 角色扮演任务并不需要完整的通用语言模型，通过精准剪枝提取角色专属子网络，可在极低计算成本下实现高性能角色扮演，为大规模多角色交互系统提供了高效可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Language Models (LMs) have shown remarkable potential as role-playing chatbots, delivering consistent, stylized interactions when given a specification of a character or user persona. However, applying these capabilities to real-world applications (e.g., ecosystems with numerous NPCs interacting simultaneously) exposes a critical inefficiency due to the excessive computational cost. In this paper, we question the necessity of dedicating a full, generalist model to a single persona, hypothesizing that a specific character identity relies on only a fraction of the model's total capacity. We observe that naively pruning LMs often severely degrades the role-playing performance for a specific persona; it does not distinguish between redundant knowledge and essential character traits. We propose Persona-Pruner, a framework that sculpts a lightweight role-playing model by isolating persona-specific sub-networks from a single description. Our experiments consistently show that Persona-Pruner preserves role-playing performance substantially more effectively than existing state-of-the-art LLM pruning techniques, reducing the performance drop from the dense model by up to 93.8% over the strongest baseline on RoleBench in LLM-as-a-judge score, while still maintaining general LLM capabilities. Code is available at https://github.com/jsu-kim/Persona-Pruner.

### [177] [Discovery under Hypothesis Redundancy: A Geometric Theory of Discovery Bottlenecks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14386)
*Li Xia,Baoxun Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出混合发现系统中非局部探索的几何条件，强调仅在谱压缩、正交逃逸和残差信号对齐同时满足时，非局部探索才能带来优势。通过合成环境、A股因子发现和符号回归任务验证了这些条件，并指出新颖性本身不足以提升性能，需具备预测对齐性。混合优势集中在弱表示但含目标信号的方向，且在假设空间接近满秩时消失。该框架将LLM引导的发现从泛化新奇搜索转变为可诊断的定向非局部探索决策工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当新假设不再提供独立信息时，科学发现趋于饱和，即使假设空间仍很大。现有方法难以有效利用大空间中的潜在有效假设，尤其在非局部探索中缺乏指导原则，因此需要明确何时以及如何结合局部搜索与大模型生成的非局部提案以实现高效发现。

Method: 提出并形式化“搜索压缩假说”，定义三个关键几何条件：谱压缩、正交逃逸和残差信号对齐；通过控制合成实验、大规模真实因子数据集（A股）及符号回归基准测试验证机制；引入信号植入和定向/随机对比实验评估不同探索策略的效果，并进行公开表格操作合理性检查以验证预算分配逻辑。

Result: 实证结果显示，只有当三个几何条件同时满足时，混合方法才表现出优势；在弱表示但含目标信号的方向上获得显著增益，而当假设空间接近满秩时优势消失；随机跳跃虽扩大覆盖范围，但无预测对齐则无法提升产出；框架能有效判断何时应采用定向非局部探索。

Conclusion: LLM引导的发现不应仅依赖新颖性，而应基于几何条件进行诊断性决策。本框架为混合发现系统提供了理论基础与实践工具，使非局部探索更具针对性和有效性，从而避免无效搜索浪费计算资源。

Abstract: Scientific discovery saturates when new hypotheses cease to provide independent information, even if the nominal hypothesis space remains large. We study hybrid discovery systems that combine structured local search with LLM-generated non-local proposals and pose the Search Compression Hypothesis: non-local exploration helps only when three geometric conditions co-occur: spectral compression, orthogonal escape from the explored span, and residual signal alignment with the target. We formalize these conditions, derive necessary conditions for hybrid advantage, and test the mechanism in controlled synthetic environments, large-scale A-share factor discovery, and symbolic-regression benchmarks; a public tabular operational sanity check tests the associated budget-allocation implication. Signal-planting and directed-versus-random experiments show that novelty alone is insufficient: random orthogonal jumps expand coverage but do not improve yield without predictive alignment. Across compression sweeps, real factor archives, and LLM-SRBench tasks, hybrid gains concentrate in weakly represented but target-bearing directions and vanish as the hypothesis space approaches full rank. The framework turns LLM-guided discovery from generic novelty search into a diagnostic procedure for deciding when directed non-local exploration is warranted.

### [178] [A Low-Rank Subspace Analysis of LLM Interventions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14388)
*Angira Sharma,Christian Schroeder de Witt,Philip Torr,Anisoara Calinescu,Jialin Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种诊断框架，用于分析大语言模型中不同行为之间的相互作用。通过将行为建模为激活空间中的低秩子空间，发现不同行为共享内部表示，干预某一行为会以非对称方式影响其他行为。某些行为作为上游控制点，其干预具有广泛传播效应，而其他行为则相对孤立。实证表明，行为间子空间重叠度越高、源行为子空间与决策子空间夹角越小，干预的跨行为影响越大。这揭示了实现精准行为控制的挑战：行为难以独立修改，因共享表示和不对称交互导致干预效果扩散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前针对大语言模型中特定行为（如拒绝或迎合）的干预措施常引发其他行为的意外变化，缺乏目标控制能力，阻碍了可靠安全机制的设计与实施。因此亟需理解这些副作用的内在机制。

Method: 将行为建模为激活空间中的低秩子空间，利用主方向之间的平均平方余弦角衡量子空间重叠度，并计算行为子空间与决策子空间之间的夹角，以分析干预对其他行为的影响。在多个指令微调模型（7B-70B）及拒绝、越狱、迎合等场景下进行实验验证。

Result: 不同行为之间存在共享表示；干预一个行为会以非对称方式影响其他行为；高子空间重叠度和较小的决策子空间夹角会导致更大的跨行为影响；部分行为作为上游控制点，其干预具有广泛传播性。

Conclusion: 行为在模型内部具有高度耦合性，难以独立调控。干预措施易通过共享表示和不对称交互产生连锁效应，这对实现精确、可靠的模型行为控制构成根本挑战。

Abstract: Interventions designed to modify a particular behavior in LLMs, such as refusal or sycophancy, often produce unintended changes in other behaviors. This lack of targeted control makes it difficult to design and implement reliable safety controls. To understand these side-effects, we introduce a diagnostic framework for analyzing interacting behaviors in LLMs. We model behaviors as low-rank subspaces in activation space, and study how interventions influence across behaviors. Across multiple instruction-tuned models (7B-70B) and across refusal, jailbreak, and sycophancy settings, we find that different behaviors share internal representations, and intervening on one behavior alters others in asymmetric ways. Some behaviors act as upstream control points whose interventions propagate broadly across other behaviors, while others remain more isolated. We relate these effects to two geometric quantities: (i) the overlap between behavior subspaces, measured as the average squared cosine of principal angles, and (ii) the angle between each behavior subspace and the decision subspace (capturing the model's final decision e.g., refuse vs. comply). Empirically, intervention effects on other behaviors tend to be larger for behavior pairs with higher subspace overlap, and for source behaviors whose subspaces lie closer (smaller angle) to the decision subspace. These findings highlight a challenge for targeted behavior control: behaviors are difficult to modify independently, as interventions can propagate through shared representations and asymmetric interactions.

</details>

*Mykola Vysotskyi,Runqi Lin,Grzegorz Biziel,Michal Zakrzewski,Sebastian Montagna,Damian Rynczak,Shreyansh Padarha,Kumail Alhamoud,Zihao Fu,William Lugoloobi,Kai Rawal,Hanna Yershova,Xander Davies,Taras Rumezhak,Guohao Li,Fazl Barez,Baoyuan Wu,Arkadiusz Drohomirecki,Yarin Gal,Chris Russell,Christopher Summerfield,Adam Mahdi,Volodymyr Karpiv,Philip Torr,Adel Bibi*

Result: 前沿智能体在GauntletBench上平均成功率为19.1%，远低于非专家人类超过80%的成功率，表明当前智能体在时间感知、图形理解与3D推理等维度存在严重不足，其泛化能力仍远未达到人类水平。

Conclusion: GauntletBench 有效揭示了当前智能体在复杂现实任务中的根本性缺陷，强调需关注被忽视的核心能力，并推动下一代智能体在多模态理解与跨域泛化方面取得突破。

Abstract: As agentic systems continue to evolve and are widely deployed in real-world scenarios, there is a growing demand to faithfully evaluate their capabilities. However, current benchmarks are typically built on popular applications with relatively simple tasks and focus on a narrow set of capabilities while overlooking broader dimensions, resulting in saturated performance on modern agents and failing to probe their limitations. To this end, we introduce GauntletBench, a web-based benchmark for evaluating agent generalisation in challenging scenarios, focusing on three underexplored capabilities (temporal perception, graphical understanding, and 3D reasoning), across five less-covered professional applications (Video Editor, Workflow Builder, 3D Modeller, Flight Analyser, and Circuit Designer), each with 20 vision-intensive tasks (100 in total). Our benchmark provides a modular pipeline that comprises an environment compatible with both open- and closed-source agent frameworks, a controlled web-based application, a well-structured task suite, and an automated evaluation engine with diverse metrics. Contrary to widespread expectations, our empirical results reveal that frontier agentic systems remain far from achieving human-level performance. Even the state-of-the-art agent achieves only a 19.1% success rate on our GauntletBench, highlighting the limitations in these overlooked capabilities and generalisation. By comparison, non-expert human annotators achieve over 80% success on our challenging yet feasible tasks, revealing the substantial gap between current agent capabilities and those required for complex real-world scenarios.

### [180] [A theoretical model for task routing in mixture-of-expert transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14398)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 理论证明表明，单层MoE Transformer能够通过任务特定专家实现高效知识编码，专家规模仅依赖于任务内在复杂度；实验结果显示，不同损失函数对模型性能有显著影响，支持理论假设的有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究为自然语言处理中的MoE模型提供了首个基于离散语言模型的理论解释框架，成功揭示了任务专家特异性的成因，为理解大规模MoE模型的知识组织机制提供了坚实基础，并推动了从经验观察向理论建模的跨越。

Abstract: Mixture-of-experts (MoE) layers enable the scaling of transformer models while keeping the inference compute fixed. While task-expert specialization has been observed in empirical studies of frontier MoE transformer models, existing theoretical work analyzes this using continuous mixture models that cannot be used to model natural language effectively. An important open question is to \textit{theoretically explain task-expert specialization in transformer MoE models using discrete models of language}. To address this, we represent structured knowledge via syntactic templates and finite key-value dictionaries, and prove formally that a single-layer MoE transformer can encode knowledge by using experts that specialize in the corresponding tasks. Our construction shows how queries are routed to unique, task-specific experts whose size depends solely on the intrinsic complexity of the given task (i.e. the combined size of its syntactic templates and factual dictionary). Our construction provides a theoretical support for empirical results on localized knowledge circuits in MoE models. We support our theoretical findings with experiments evaluating model performance under varying MoE loss functions.

### [181] [Federated Learning for Feature Generalization with Convex Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14416)
*Dongwon Kim,Donghee Kim,Sung Kuk Shyn,Kwangsu Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FedCONST 是一种用于联邦学习（FL）的自适应参数调制方法，通过基于全局模型参数强度调节更新幅度，防止对已充分学习的参数过度强调，同时增强欠发展参数的学习。该方法利用线性凸约束确保训练稳定性，并保留本地学习的泛化能力。通过梯度信噪比（GSNR）分析验证了其在提升特征可迁移性和鲁棒性方面的有效性。实验表明，FedCONST 能有效对齐局部与全局目标，缓解过拟合问题，在多样化联邦学习环境中实现更强的泛化性能，达到当前最优水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习中由于客户端数据异构性，本地模型容易过拟合本地数据分布，且共享特征在聚合过程中可能被扭曲，导致泛化能力下降。因此需要一种机制来平衡本地学习与全局聚合之间的关系，以提升整体模型的泛化性能。

Method: 提出 FedCONST，通过分析全局模型中各参数的强度，自适应地调整本地更新的幅度；引入线性凸约束以保证训练过程的稳定性；利用梯度信噪比（GSNR）进行理论分析，评估特征转移能力和鲁棒性。

Result: FedCONST 在多个异构联邦学习场景下表现出色，显著提升了模型的泛化能力，有效缓解了过拟合问题，实现了优于现有方法的性能，达到当前最佳水平。

Conclusion: FedCONST 通过自适应调制更新幅度和引入结构化约束，成功解决了联邦学习中因数据异构带来的泛化难题，为构建更具鲁棒性和可迁移性的联邦学习系统提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Federated learning (FL) often struggles with generalization due to heterogeneous client data. Local models are prone to overfitting their local data distributions, and even transferable features can be distorted during aggregation. To address these challenges, we propose FedCONST, an approach that adaptively modulates update magnitudes based on the parameter strength of the global model. This prevents over-emphasizing well-learned parameters while reinforcing underdeveloped ones. Specifically, FedCONST employs linear convex constraints to ensure training stability and preserve locally learned generalization capabilities during aggregation. A Gradient Signal to Noise Ratio (GSNR) analysis further validates the effectiveness of FedCONST in enhancing feature transferability and robustness. As a result, FedCONST effectively aligns local and global objectives, mitigating overfitting and promoting stronger generalization across diverse FL environments, achieving state-of-the-art performance.

### [182] [EM-NeSy: Expectation Maximization for Neurosymbolic Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14463)
*Annegret Seibt,Luc De Raedt,Giuseppe Marra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EM-NeSy proposes a novel framework for neurosymbolic learning by leveraging the Expectation-Maximization algorithm, enabling probabilistic inference without requiring differentiability of symbolic components. It allows approximate reasoning and maintains compatibility with standard end-to-end training under exact inference.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing neurosymbolic models require differentiable symbolic components, which limits their ability to use approximate inference methods. This restriction hinders flexibility and scalability in real-world applications.

Method: EM-NeSy formulates neurosymbolic learning as an EM algorithm: in the expectation step, posterior over symbols is computed via probabilistic inference given labels; in the maximization step, neural parameters are updated using gradient descent through the neural component only.

Result: The approach achieves scalable and computationally efficient learning, supports approximate reasoning without modifying the symbolic component, and recovers standard end-to-end training when exact inference is used.

Conclusion: EM-NeSy effectively unifies probabilistic inference with neural learning, offering greater flexibility and efficiency in neurosymbolic AI systems without imposing differentiability on symbolic parts.

Abstract: Neurosymbolic (NeSy) models integrate neural networks and symbolic reasoning for robust and interpretable AI. State-of-the-art NeSy models require that the symbolic component is expressed in a differentiable way, often complicating the use of approximate inference. We propose EM-NeSy which casts probabilistic NeSy learning as an instance of the Expectation-Maximization (EM) algorithm. In the expectation step, we compute the posterior over the neurally predicted symbols conditioned on the label via probabilistic inference. In the maximization step, we update the neural parameters based on this posterior using gradient descent only through the neural component. This formulation unlocks the full potential of the EM algorithm for NeSy learning. It allows NeSy to extend naturally to approximate reasoning without any additional modifications or differentiability requirements of the symbolic component. Furthermore, it recovers the standard end-to-end gradient-based NeSy setting under exact inference. Our experimental results demonstrate the scalability and computational efficiency of EM-NeSy.

</details>


### [183] [Recipe-Controlled Decoder Audit for Structural Knowledge-Graph Completion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14492)
*Xihang Shan,Ye Luo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种受控解码器审计（RCDA）方法，用于结构化归纳知识图谱补全（KGC），通过在相同训练配方下更换解码器来评估其影响。研究发现，在标准数据集上，ComplEx与DistMult的性能差异较小但一致；而在小规模数据集上，解码器选择对结果影响显著且受配方和数据溯源影响。此外，解码器与编码器深度存在交互作用，并验证了在特定条件下模型能达到较高性能。最终建议：报告匹配的解码器结果，记录小数据集的溯源信息，并在做出编码器层面结论前系统性测试解码器与深度组合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识图谱补全研究中，难以区分模型性能提升是来自编码器改进还是训练配方或解码器选择的影响。为更准确评估编码器贡献，需要一种可控制的审计机制，以隔离解码器的作用。

Method: 采用受控实验设计，固定训练配方（recipe），在ComplEx与DistMult之间切换解码器，辅以RotatE/TransE进行验证，对七个基准数据集进行评估。通过多轮种子实验、不同数据溯源版本对比及编码器深度变化分析，系统考察解码器的影响。

Conclusion: 解码器的选择在知识图谱补全中具有重要影响，尤其在小规模数据集上，其效果受训练配方和数据溯源敏感。因此，应建立标准化审计流程：报告匹配解码器结果，追踪小数据集的来源信息，并在评估编码器性能前系统测试解码器与深度组合。

Abstract: We present a recipe-controlled decoder audit (RCDA) for structural transductive knowledge-graph completion (KGC). The audit asks a simple reporting question: before attributing gains to an encoder or training recipe, what changes when the decoder is swapped under the same recipe? Using ComplEx and DistMult as the primary controlled pair, with targeted RotatE/TransE spot-checks, we evaluate seven benchmarks. On five standard KGs, ComplEx-vs-DistMult differences are modest but consistent under our recipe (+0.005 to +0.012 MRR), whereas CompGCN-style encoder effects vary more by dataset. On small KGs, decoder effects become the main diagnostic: Kinship shows a stable ComplEx advantage of +0.143 MRR (6 seeds), while UMLS favours ComplEx by +0.022 MRR in a clean 6-seed server rerun but reverses in an earlier provenance variant. We therefore treat small-KG decoder choice as recipe- and provenance-sensitive rather than as a fixed dataset winner. We further show that decoder choice interacts with encoder depth on WN18RR, and that under our recipe L=0 ComplEx on YAGO3-10 reaches 0.6971 +/- 0.0048 MRR at d=128. The result is a compact audit protocol: report matched decoder rows, log small-KG provenance, and sweep decoder x depth before making encoder-level claims.

Abstract: Macrocyclic peptides are promising therapeutic candidates for intracellular targets, but their design requires simultaneous control over non-natural monomer chemistry, ring topology, membrane permeability, and target binding. Existing SMILES- or HELM-string generative models either operate in long atom-level sequence spaces or treat monomers as symbolic tokens with limited chemical grounding. We introduce PepALD, an Autoregressive Latent Diffusion (ALD) foundation model for \textit{de novo} macrocyclic peptide generation. The model represents HELM monomers with structured chemical embeddings, generates each residue through context-conditioned diffusion in chemically informed latent space, predicts R-group-aware ring closures during autoregressive generation, and aligns the denoiser to affinity rewards using winner-protected diffusion-adapted preference optimization. ### [185] [Behavioral Audit of Machine Unlearning Has a Privacy Cost](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14518)
*Liou Tang,James Joshi,Ashish Kundu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了机器学习模型中数据移除（机器遗忘，MU）的审计问题，指出在模型所有者与审计者相互不信任的场景下，仅通过查询模型行为信号进行通用审计存在隐私与审计效果之间的固有权衡。对于凸模型，任何依赖行为信号的审计方案都无法在不泄露保留数据成员信息的情况下识别未充分遗忘的模型。实验证明该权衡在非凸模型中同样存在，强调需重新审视隐私保护审计设计中的威胁模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究未能建立可信的机器遗忘审计机制，在模型所有者可能伪造证据、审计者可能利用有限访问推断敏感信息的背景下，缺乏对互不信任场景下审计可行性的分析。

Method: 采用信息论方法证明：对于凸模型，仅基于模型行为信号的审计方案必然导致隐私泄露；通过实验验证该结论在凸与非凸模型中的普遍性。

Result: 揭示了在互不信任环境下，机器遗忘审计面临无法避免的隐私-审计权衡；实验证实该权衡在多种模型结构中均成立。

Conclusion: 当前的审计设计必须更审慎地考虑隐私与审计能力之间的矛盾，未来应发展兼顾隐私保护与可审计性的新型审计框架。

Abstract: The removal of learned data from Machine Learning models through Machine Unlearning (MU) has been widely studied; however, there has yet to be an agreed-upon scheme for auditing MU. Existing work has shown that a dishonest model owner can falsify evidence to avoid executing MU, while curious auditors (and adversaries) can infer the privacy-sensitive properties of the model and its training data even with limited access. Yet auditing of MU under mutual distrust between the model owner and the auditor remains unexplored. We provide an information-theoretic proof for this scenario: for convex ML models, a generic audit scheme that relies solely on querying the model for \textit{behavioral} signals cannot identify insufficiently unlearned models without revealing membership information of the retained set. Therefore, auditing MU under the assumption of a dishonest model owner and an honest-but-curious auditor faces an inherent privacy-audit tradeoff. Our empirical results on convex models strongly supports this result, while further experiments demonstrate that this privacy-audit tension persists in non-convex models. Our results call for a more careful consideration of the privacy-audit tension under a realistic auditor threat model, and serve as a foundation for more scrutiny of designs of privacy-preserving audit schemes for the MU pipeline. We also release our code implementation at https://github.com/LiouTang/Behavioral-Unlearn-Audit.

### [186] [Code Correctness Signals in LLM Hidden States: Pre-Generation Probing and Repair Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14530)
*Carlo Di Cicco*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了Qwen3-4B-Instruct-2507模型在生成代码前及修复失败尝试时，其隐藏状态中是否可读取代码正确性信息。通过444个LiveCodeBench任务进行分析，发现首次生成代码的正确性可线性解码，准确率高达0.931（去提示长度干扰后仍达0.911），而修复过程中的隐藏状态变化虽具统计显著性，但经残差化控制后不再成立，表明其受修复上下文影响而非独立的修复理解特征。研究强调方法论严谨性，既报告正结果也揭示负结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究大型语言模型隐藏状态中代码正确性信息的可读性，特别是在首次生成与修复失败代码过程中，以评估模型内部表征的理解能力。

Method: 采用嵌套交叉验证选择探测层，使用残差化方法消除提示长度等混杂因素影响，对提示末尾隐藏状态进行线性解码，并分析修复前后隐藏状态的差异方向，结合分半检验和标签随机置换对照验证结果可靠性。

Result: 首次生成代码的正确性可被高度准确地从隐藏状态中解码（AUC=0.931，去提示长度后仍为0.911）；修复过程中的隐藏状态变化虽有统计显著性，但经残差化控制后不再显著，说明其受修复上下文驱动而非模型自身修复理解能力。

Conclusion: 该研究不仅揭示了模型在预生成阶段能有效编码代码正确性信息，更强调方法论上的诚实性：通过残差化控制工具识别出看似有意义的修复方向实为上下文混杂所致，从而避免误读模型认知机制。此工作兼具方法论贡献与实证价值。

Abstract: Large language models encode rich information in their hidden states. This work asks whether code correctness is legible in the hidden states of Qwen3-4B-Instruct-2507, before it generates and as it repairs a failed attempt, studied on 444 LiveCodeBench tasks. It reports two findings connected by a single confound-control tool: residualization. First, the correctness of the model's first-attempt code is linearly decodable from the prompt-final hidden state, with a leakage-free held-out AUC of 0.931 +/- 0.008 across 50 outer splits. After the linear effect of prompt length is removed from each hidden state dimension, the probe still reaches 0.911 +/- 0.010, well above a prompt-length baseline of 0.754 +/- 0.014. Second, on 236 cleaned cases where the model attempts to repair a failed first attempt, the hidden state shift from the failing attempt to its repair carries a statistically detectable contrastive direction, significant on both a magnitude and a split-half test against label-shuffled nulls. This direction does not survive a conditional residualization against repair-context covariates that differ between successful and failed repairs, marking it as a correlate of repair success driven by the repair context rather than an isolated repair-comprehension feature. The probe layer is selected by nested cross-validation, and the same residualization approach that upholds the pre-generation correctness result overturns the repair-direction interpretation. The contribution is as much methodological as empirical: a diagnostic honest enough to report a negative result alongside a positive one.

### [187] [The Risk Shadow of Principal Component Analysis: When 99.9999% Variance Preservation Causes Catastrophic Decision Errors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14533)
*Hamidou Tembine*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PCA fails to preserve information about rare, high-impact events despite retaining most variance. This paper introduces Risk Shadow concept and proposes ExPCA and TP-PCA to reweight data covariance toward tail risks, proving ExPCA outperforms PCA theoretically and validating it on synthetic and real-world fraud detection data.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard PCA maximizes variance but ignores rare catastrophic events, leading to loss of critical information for high-impact failure detection in high-stakes applications.

Method: Introduce Expectile PCA (ExPCA) and Tail-Preserving PCA (TP-PCA), which reweight data covariance to emphasize high-impact events, addressing the mismatch between variance maximization and tail risk awareness.

Result: ExPCA strictly outperforms PCA in preserving rare-event information; experiments confirm improved detection performance on synthetic data and credit card fraud benchmark.

Conclusion: Variance-based dimensionality reduction like PCA is inadequate for high-stakes decision-making involving rare events. New methods such as ExPCA and TP-PCA are necessary to preserve tail risk information.

Abstract: Principal Component Analysis (PCA) preserves variance, not the information needed to detect rare catastrophic events. This paper proves the existence of a {\it Risk Shadow}: PCA can retain over 99.9999 percent of total variance while completely erasing all signal about rare, high-impact failures. When this happens, even the best possible classifier operating on the PCA representation reduces to a constant predictor. The root cause is a fundamental mismatch between variance maximization and tail risk awareness. To break the shadow, we introduce Expectile PCA (ExPCA) and Tail-Preserving PCA (TP-PCA), two methods that reweight the data covariance toward high-impact events. We prove theoretically that ExPCA strictly outperforms PCA in retaining rare-event information, and we validate our claims on synthetic data and a real-world credit card fraud detection benchmark. Our results call for a fundamental rethinking of variance-based dimensionality reduction in high-stakes decisions.

### [188] [Provably Safe, Yet Scalable Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14536)
*Kai S. Yun,Zeyang Li,Navid Azizan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PS2-RL 是一种可证明安全且可扩展的强化学习框架，通过两阶段设计克服了传统方法在安全性和可扩展性上的瓶颈。第一阶段利用安全到达价值函数训练一个备份策略，以在线生成隐式控制不变集；第二阶段通过可微投影层端到端训练主策略，严格保证安全性。该方法无需显式构造不变集，适用于高维状态空间，且兼容任意现有强化学习算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有安全强化学习方法要么缺乏形式化安全保证（软约束），要么因依赖显式控制不变集构造而计算复杂、保守性强，难以在高维系统中应用。本文旨在提出一种既能保证安全又能高效扩展的新方法。

Method: 提出两阶段的 PS2-RL 框架：第一阶段使用安全到达价值函数训练一个备份策略，通过前向积分系统动力学生成隐式控制不变集；第二阶段通过可微投影层将主策略训练过程与备份策略的安全性绑定，实现端到端的安全策略学习。

Result: 在状态维度高达10的机器人控制任务上验证了PS2-RL的有效性，相比以往可证明安全的RL方法，具有更高的性能和更好的可扩展性，同时保持严格的数学安全保证。

Conclusion: PS2-RL 框架实现了安全与可扩展性的统一，在不牺牲安全性的情况下显著提升了高维系统的适用性，且可无缝集成至现有RL训练流程中。

Abstract: Safe reinforcement learning (RL) aims to learn policies that optimize rewards while satisfying constraints. Predominant approaches rely on soft-constrained policy optimization, which has achieved empirical success but does not provide formal safety guarantees for the learned policy. In contrast, methods with strict guarantees typically rely on explicit certificate functions, whose construction requires the direct synthesis and verification of control-invariant sets, a process that scales poorly with state dimension and often yields overly conservative behavior. In this paper, we present the Provably Safe, yet Scalable RL (PS2-RL) framework, a novel two-phase architecture for learning provably safe policies in a scalable manner, designed to overcome the key bottlenecks of prior methods. Rather than explicitly computing invariant sets, PS2-RL leverages a learned backup policy to forward-integrate the system dynamics, generating an implicit control-invariant set online. In the first phase, the backup policy is trained with our proposed safe-arrival value function, which characterizes the optimal backup policy for invariant-set construction. In the second phase, an RL policy is trained end-to-end through a differentiable projection layer that strictly enforces the safety guarantees induced by the learned backup policy. By maximizing the volume of the implicit control-invariant set in the first phase, the resulting PS2 policy from the second phase is performant and scalable, while maintaining provable safety. Crucially, PS2-RL imposes no restrictions on the underlying RL algorithm and can be plugged into any existing training pipeline. We establish theoretical guarantees for the proposed framework and evaluate it on robotic control tasks with state dimensions up to 10, a regime in which prior provably safe RL methods struggle or become impractical.

</details>


### [189] [CARE: Controlling LLM-Generated Policies through Auditable Review of Evidence in Scientific Experimentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14581)
*Guanyu Liu,Weiyi Kong,Zeyu Wang,Boer Zhang,Baiqing Li,Peiyu Zhang,Tianyu Shi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CARE 是一种可审计的控制器，用于高通量实验（HTE）优化，通过在决策前评估证据来控制大语言模型（LLM）生成的策略，确保安全与效率。它以非LLM的现有优化器为默认路径，仅在有充分证据支持时才允许LLM提出的替代方案被采纳，从而提升实验性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接让大语言模型控制高成本、不可逆的科学实验存在安全隐患和性能不稳定问题；但完全放弃LLM的创造力又会损失优化潜力。因此需要一种既能利用LLM创新能力又能保障安全性的方法。

Method: CARE 采用一个公开证据干预门，在每次实验结果揭晓前，对比挑战者策略与现有最优策略的证据支持度，仅当已有证据支持变更时才授权选择挑战者，并将决策记录在审计日志中。

Result: 在 Minerva/Olympus 和 ChemLex 基准测试中，CARE 显著优于其他方法：Minerva/Olympus 上最佳结果从 80.0 提升至 88.5，ChemLex 上从 83.9 提升至 92.1，相对公共基准显著改进。

Conclusion: 在可审计的控制机制下，LLM 的自我演化更可靠，尤其是在扩展提案空间方面，而非直接自主选择实验。CARE 实现了安全性与创新性的平衡，是 HTE 优化的有效解决方案。

Abstract: Granting LLMs direct control over costly, irreversible scientific experiments leads to unsafe exploration and unstable performance, but discarding LLM creativity entirely sacrifices significant optimization potential. We introduce CARE (Controlling LLM-Generated Policies through Auditable Review of Evidence in Scientific Experimentation), an auditable controller for high-throughput experimentation (HTE) optimization that keeps a non-LLM incumbent optimizer as the default action path while using LLMs to revise challenger ranking policies. Before each outcome is revealed, a public-evidence intervention gate compares the challenger with the incumbent. It authorizes the challenger's selection only when the evidence available before selection supports the change, with the decision recorded in the audit log. CARE outperforms all other evaluated methods on Minerva/Olympus and ChemLex benchmarks, with final-best improving from 80.0 to 88.5 on Minerva/Olympus and from 83.9 to 92.1 on ChemLex, relative to the public incumbent. Our experiments indicate that LLM self-evolution is more reliable when it expands the proposal space under an auditable controller, rather than directly choosing experiments.

Abstract: Transformer-based neural operators have shown remarkable performance for approximating solution operators of partial differential equations on complex geometries. In this work, we investigate domain extension, namely zero-shot inference on spatial domains that are significantly larger than those encountered during training. We argue that this setting fundamentally requires spatial locality and translation equivariance. We propose to implement this locality via a decomposable bias in the attention logits computation, enabling finely controllable locality while remaining fully decomposable into query-key inner products and directly compatible with optimized attention kernels. Combined with rotary positional embeddings, it enables expressive embeddings with controllable spatial support without altering the transformer architecture. We empirically show that our approach substantially improves zero-shot generalization to larger domains across two PDE benchmarks and a 3D industrial atmospheric flow application. Our code and datasets are available at https://github.com/cerea-daml/domain-extension.

### [191] [Realizing Native INT8 Compute for Diffusion Transformers on Consumer GPUs: A Fused INT8 GEMM Kernel for Ideogram 4.0](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14598)
*Ali Asaria,Tony Salomone,Deep Gandhi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文针对扩散变压器在消费级Ampere GPU上进行后训练INT8（W8A8）量化时速度反而慢于FP8和NF4的问题，指出问题根源在于软件实现中权重和激活量化的数据被立即反量化回bf16并执行bf16矩阵乘法，未利用GPU的INT8张量核心。为此，作者提出一种融合的Triton INT8 GEMM核函数，直接在Ampere张量核心上执行int8xint8->int32计算，并引入逐令牌和逐通道的反量化及偏置折叠机制，经自动调优适配不同GEMM形状。该方法在保持与参考模型完全一致的精度（余弦相似度1.0，无NaN）的前提下，单个GEMM性能提升2.8-4.2倍；端到端推理速度在768px下提升约1.1倍（9-10%），在1024px下仅需156.5秒（优于NF4的164.5秒和FP8的172.9秒），且质量无明显损失。尽管该优化在A100和B200等高端卡上不具优势，但在消费级Ampere GPU上成功将INT8从最慢变为最快，实现了关键性能目标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在消费级Ampere GPU上，尽管后训练INT8量化旨在加速扩散模型推理，但实际表现却常慢于FP8和NF4，其根本原因在于现有实现未能有效利用GPU的INT8张量核心，导致硬件加速优势无法发挥。因此需要重新设计量化计算路径以真正激活硬件能力。

Method: 提出一种融合的Triton INT8 GEMM内核，直接在Ampere张量核心上执行int8xint8->int32运算，结合每令牌/每通道的反量化与偏置折叠，并通过自动调优适应不同GEMM尺寸。该内核替代原有的反量化至bf16再进行矩阵乘法的路径，确保计算效率最大化。

Result: 在单个RTX 3090上，1024px图像生成时间缩短至156.5秒，优于NF4（164.5秒）和FP8（172.9秒）基准；端到端速度提升约1.1倍（9-10%），且在PickScore/CLIPScore等指标上无显著质量损失；在消费级Ampere GPU上，INT8由最慢变为最快，满足主要性能目标（超越FP8约9.5%），而与NF4的差距在运行波动范围内，视为一致达成目标。

Conclusion: 通过针对性优化，使INT8量化在消费级Ampere GPU上真正发挥硬件优势，实现显著加速，成为当前最优选择；但该方案具有特定平台适用性，不适用于A100或B200等支持原生快速bf16/FP8路径的设备。

Abstract: Post-training INT8 (W8A8) quantization of diffusion transformers is widely deployed as a speed optimization, yet on consumer Ampere GPUs it is frequently slower than the FP8 and NF4 alternatives it is meant to beat. We trace this to a software artifact: the production "INT8" forward quantizes weights and activations only to immediately dequantize them back to bf16 and run a bf16 matrix multiply, never engaging the GPU's INT8 tensor cores, so the hardware's compute advantage is left entirely unrealized. We close this gap with a single fused Triton INT8 GEMM (int8xint8->int32 on Ampere tensor cores, with per-token x per-channel dequantization and bias folded into the epilogue, autotuned per GEMM shape) dropped into the Ideogram 4.0 diffusion transformer's linear layers in place of the dequantize-to-bf16 path. In the kernel, the int8xint8->int32 accumulation is bit-exact against torch._int_mm and the dequantized output matches the reference at cosine similarity 1.0 with no NaNs, running 2.8-4.2x faster than bf16 per GEMM. End to end it delivers a ~1.1x (~9-10%) speedup at 768px, and at 1024px it generates an image in 156.5 s on a single RTX 3090, faster than the single-card NF4 (164.5 s) and FP8 (172.9 s) baselines, at no measurable quality cost on these point estimates (PickScore/CLIPScore). INT8 thus goes from the slowest variant to the fastest, and 1024px becomes single-GPU feasible. The primary speed criterion (beat FP8, by ~9.5%) is comfortably met; the NF4 margin (~4.9%, single-run n=4) is within run-to-run variance we did not quantify and is best read as consistent with meeting the stretch target. We close with an honest deployment map: the win is specific to consumer Ampere, and on A100 and B200 the same kernel loses to those cards' fast native bf16/FP8 paths.

</details>


### [192] [A Statistical and Machine Learning Framework for Operational Threshold Detection and Deployable Dispatch Controller Development in Hydrogen Multi-Energy Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14601)

Method: 结合统计分析、多元回归、随机森林、序列建模及强化学习等方法，对一年高分辨率运行数据进行多维度建模与分析。

Abstract: This study presents a statistical and machine learning framework for characterizing a hydrogen-based multi-energy system (H-MES) using one year of high-resolution operational data. Statistical analysis revealed a binary operation driven by renewable surplus, with solar irradiance explaining 45.7% of rank-based variance in hydrogen production, a large effect by conventional standards. Only high-irradiance periods triggered meaningful electrolyzer engagement, while electricity demand exerted a weaker inverse suppression effect ($ε^2 = 0.126$). Multiple regression confirmed electrolyzer power as the dominant linear predictor, with a synergistic solar-wind interaction. Notably, Random Forest analysis ranked wind output first in predictive importance despite its weak bivariate correlation (r = 0.167), revealing non-linear dynamics invisible to parametric methods. A sequence model exploited strong 24-hour autocorrelation (r = 0.845) for operational forecasting, while a reinforcement learning agent optimized hydrogen revenue dispatch. The core contribution is demonstrating that statistical and machine learning approaches are complementary for H-MES modeling and control.

Our key findings are: (i) no single architecture dominates, PatchTST leads among trained models while the three runners-up (TCN, MLP, Transformer) show no meaningful performance difference; (ii) the FM TimesFM matches or exceeds trained models zero-shot, especially in low-data regimes and (iii) participant-level fine-tuning reduces per-feature RMSE by 16-60\%, with sleep benefiting most and step counts least. These results provide practical guidance on architecture selection, FM applicability and personalisation strategies for mobile health forecasting. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first study to jointly evaluate modern deep learning, FMs and personalisation for multi-horizon behavioural forecasting from wearables.

### [195] [Neither Parallel Nor Sequential: How DiffusionGemma Actually Commits Tokens](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14620)
*Ali Asaria,Tony Salomone,Deep Gandhi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过仪器化DiffusionGemma 26B模型，测量其在不同任务场景下的解码顺序，发现其并非完全并行或块自回归，而是呈现一种局部从左到右的提交偏倚，且该偏倚的显著程度取决于分析粒度。模型以大批次方式同时提交令牌，批次内部顺序实际未定义。不同任务类型（如结构化JSON、数学推理）的提交行为各异，提交置信度与数学正确性相关但与事实回忆无关。模型解码行为具有激进性，在预算步数内快速完成，且性能与自回归Gemma-4相当。研究的核心贡献在于提出一套方法论，用于准确测量解码顺序，需处理尾随EOS填充、组内混淆、非单调提交、块大小敏感性及大批量并行提交等挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开放扩散语言模型虽宣传为并行、非自回归解码，但其实际令牌提交顺序未被系统测量，导致对模型解码机制的理解存在盲区。本文旨在揭示真实解码行为，避免因测量方法不当而产生虚假结论。

Method: 通过钩子技术插入到扩散采样器的接受步骤中，记录每个画布位置的令牌提交时间、顺序及置信度；在686个提示、六种不同任务模式下进行实验，系统分析提交行为的统计特性，并设计方法应对多项测量干扰因素。

Result: 解码过程既非完全并行也非严格自回归，呈现依赖于分析粒度的局部左到右偏倚；提交以大批次形式发生，批次内顺序无定义；不同任务模式下行为差异显著，置信度仅与数学推理正确性相关；模型在有限步数内快速完成解码，性能与自回归基线相当。

Conclusion: 扩散语言模型的真实解码行为是复杂且高度依赖任务和测量尺度的，其‘块大小’是测量工具的产物而非架构本质。本文提出的方法可有效避免人为制造的虚假解码顺序结论，为未来研究提供可靠评估框架。

Abstract: Open diffusion language models are marketed as parallel, non-autoregressive decoders, yet the order in which a shipped checkpoint actually commits its tokens is almost never measured. We instrument DiffusionGemma 26B, a masked discrete-diffusion mixture-of-experts model built on Gemma 4, hooking its sampler's accept step to record which canvas positions commit, when, and at what confidence. Across a 686-prompt, six-regime probe suite we find that its decoding is neither parallel nor block-autoregressive: it follows a partial left-to-right commit bias whose apparent strength depends almost entirely on the granularity at which you look. Order is weak token by token and strengthens smoothly as the analysis is coarsened, so the model's "block size" turns out to be an artifact of the measuring ruler rather than the architecture. The model commits in large simultaneous batches, leaving much of the within-batch order genuinely undefined rather than merely unobserved. The behaviour is regime-dependent: structured JSON is committed in essentially arbitrary order, and a position's commit confidence tracks correctness on mathematical reasoning but carries no signal on factual recall. Commitment is aggressive, finishing in a short late burst well inside the step budget, while task accuracy matches the model's autoregressive Gemma-4 sibling. Beyond these findings, our central contribution is methodological: measuring decoding order honestly demands handling trailing-EOS padding, within-regime confounding, commit non-monotonicity, block-size sensitivity, and large commit-batch ties, each of which can otherwise manufacture a decoding-order result that is not really there.

### [196] [Graph Diffusion Residuals for Control-Function Instrumental Variables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14636)
*Rui Wu,Zongyuan Chen,Hong Xie,Defu Lian,Enhong Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: A-IHF 是一种用于提取灵活控制函数的确定性图扩散残差方法，通过处理治疗变量在第一阶段特征图上的信号，利用试点扩散检测大治疗跳跃，抑制这些跳跃处的导电性，并使用稀疏图预解算子计算生成的控制。其观测选择规则仅依赖于 (Z,X)，结合图广义交叉验证、粗糙度、残差化治疗相关性和图可接受性过滤。分析将误差分解为结构泄漏、残差衰减和残差化治疗变异，提供了有限样本界限、在潜在分段光滑几何下的图可接受率以及有限路径选择校准。在54个合成基准单元中，经过保护的观测A-IHF在平均结构响应均方误差上表现最佳；A-IHF家族在32个单元中优于最佳非A-IHF基线。性能在图能捕捉分段光滑第一阶段结构时最强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高容量第一阶段模型可能对治疗变量进行插值，导致结果方程中残差信息不足。因此需要一种能够有效提取残差信息的方法，以避免过度拟合并提升估计精度。

Method: 提出 Adaptive Anisotropic Instrumental Heat Flow (A-IHF)，通过图扩散机制处理治疗信号，利用试点扩散识别显著变化点，降低其导电性，进而通过稀疏图预解算子生成控制函数。采用基于图广义交叉验证、粗糙度、残差化治疗相关性和图可接受性过滤的观测选择规则。

Result: 在54个合成基准测试中，受保护的观测A-IHF在平均结构响应均方误差上表现最优；在32个测试中，A-IHF家族优于最佳非A-IHF基线。当图结构能反映分段光滑的第一阶段特性时，性能最为突出。

Conclusion: A-IHF是一种高效且稳健的控制函数残差提取方法，尤其适用于具有分段光滑结构的第一阶段建模，在多个基准测试中展现出优越性能。

Abstract: Control-function instrumental variable estimators need a first-stage residual, not merely a first-stage prediction. High-capacity first stages can interpolate treatment and leave too little residual information for the outcome equation. We study Adaptive Anisotropic Instrumental Heat Flow (A-IHF), a deterministic graph-diffusion residual extractor for flexible control functions. A-IHF treats treatment as a signal on a graph of first-stage features, uses pilot diffusion to detect large treatment jumps, attenuates conductance across those jumps, and computes the generated control with a sparse graph resolvent. Its observational selection rule uses only $(Z,X)$, combining graph generalized cross-validation, roughness, residualized-treatment relevance, and graph-admissibility filtering. The analysis decomposes error into structural leakage, residual attenuation, and residualized treatment variation, yielding finite-sample bounds, graph-admissibility rates under latent piecewise-smooth geometry, and finite-path selection calibration. Across 54 synthetic benchmark cells with tuned graph, kernel, tree, boosting, series, and neural control-function baselines, guarded observational A-IHF has the lowest average structural-response MSE; the A-IHF family beats the best non-A-IHF baseline in 32 cells. Performance is strongest when the graph captures piecewise-smooth first-stage structure.

### [197] [Online Convex Optimization with Sublinear Noisy Probes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14640)
*Simone Di Gregorio,Anupam Gupta,Stefano Leonardi,Matteo Russo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究在线凸优化（OCO）中的统一探测模型，引入子线性且含噪声的成对探测预算，证明即使在全反馈环境下，少量探测也能显著降低最坏情况下的遗憾。主要结果为：当有 $k$ 个 $δ$-噪声成对探测时，遗憾上界为 $ O\left(\min\left\{\sqrt{dT\ln T},\; \frac{dT\ln T}{k|1-2δ|}\right\} \right) $，该界在 $T$、$k$ 和 $δ$ 上紧致（仅差对数因子）。针对噪声参数 $δ$，遗憾随 $δ$ 接近 $\frac{1}{2}$ 而平滑恶化。将方法应用于有限决策集的 $d$ 专家预测问题时，所得率在所有参数上完全紧致。分析通过方差缩减效应和基于二阶（方差）的连续指数权重方法，系统化地刻画了探测带来的收益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作分别关注专家设置中的子线性最优专家查询与在线凸优化中每轮可获得成对比较反馈。本文旨在统一这两类模型，提出一个通用的探测框架，探究在有限探测预算下如何提升在线优化性能，尤其关注探测成本与信息增益之间的权衡。

Method: 提出统一的成对探测模型，结合连续指数权重算法（Continuous Exponential Weights），利用方差缩减效应进行分析，并采用二阶（方差依赖）分析方法量化探测带来的改进。通过随机化策略建模噪声探测响应，推导出基于 $k$ 个 $δ$-噪声探测的遗憾上界。

Result: 在 $k$ 个 $δ$-噪声成对探测下，得到遗憾上界 $ O\left(\min\left\{\sqrt{dT\ln T},\; \frac{dT\ln T}{k|1-2δ|}\right\} \right) $，该界在 $T$、$k$、$δ$ 上紧致（仅差对数因子）。对于有限 $K$ 的专家预测问题，结果在 $d$、$T$、$k$ 等所有参数上完全紧致。

Conclusion: 本文表明，即使在探测预算子线性且存在噪声的情况下，成对探测仍能显著改善在线凸优化中的最坏情况遗憾。所提出的统一框架与分析方法为探索非标准反馈机制下的在线学习提供了新视角，其核心在于通过方差缩减实现更优的收敛行为。

Abstract: We study Online Convex Optimization (OCO) over a convex set $K\subseteq \mathbb R^d$, where in each round $t$ the learner selects $x_t\in K$ and then observes a convex loss $f_t:K\to[0,1]$, with the goal of minimizing regret to the best fixed decision in hindsight. We introduce a unified probing model that generalizes two recent lines of work: sublinear best-expert queries in the experts setting, and pairwise (comparison-based) feedback available every round in OCO. In our framework, the learner has a budget of $k\le T$ pairwise probes; on a probed round it may query two points and learn which one has smaller loss.
  Our main result shows that even a sublinear and noisy probe budget can provably improve worst-case regret in the full feedback OCO regime. With $k$ $δ$-noisy pairwise probes, we obtain: $ \text{Reg}_T \le O\left(\min\left\{\sqrt{dT\ln T},\; \frac{dT\ln T}{k|1-2δ|}\right\}\right) $, which is tight (up to logarithmic factors in $T$) across $T$, $k$ and $δ$. Specifically regarding the noise parameter $δ\in [0,1]$, the regret guarantee smoothly degrades as the oracle response approaches a coin flip, i.e., $δ$ is close to $\frac{1}{2}$. When applying the same techniques to a finite $K$ for the prediction with $d$ experts setting, the resulting rates are instead completely tight in all parameters, including $d$.
  Our analysis gives a streamlined treatment of pairwise probing in OCO by quantifying the benefit of probing via a variance reduction effect, combined with a second-order (variance-based) analysis of Continuous Exponential Weights.

</details>

*Pedro Chumpitaz-Flores,My Duong,Juan S. Borrero,Kaixun Hua*

Abstract: Robust machine learning and optimization rely on the uncertainty model choice. We investigate which uncertainty directions a model must cover when defined by a finite dictionary and a budget constraint. Selecting a subset forms an atomic uncertainty set with a closed form support function, yielding tractable robust programs for affine objectives. We propose a data driven selection rule based on a coverage objective over evaluation directions, including gradients, adversarial perturbations, or shifts observed on held out data. We prove this objective is monotone and submodular, supporting a greedy method with a $(1-1/e)$ approximation guarantee and a matching hardness barrier. We also provide a certificate bounding the loss from the selected subset and a radius calibration rule with out of sample control.

### [200] [Beyond task performance: Decoding bioacoustic embeddings with speech features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14662)

Method: 采用88个eGeMAPS声学特征，对六个分类群的数据使用线性和非线性回归探测器，量化各模型所捕捉的声学属性，并结合特征可恢复性与物种特征显著性（NMI）进行模型选择分析。

Abstract: Pretrained audio embeddings are standard in bioacoustics, yet little is known about which acoustic features these models encode, nor which are useful for a given task. This hinders transparency and limits extension to rare species or data-scarce domains. Here we reveal which speech-like features are encoded in bioacoustic representations. Using the 88~eGeMAPS features across six taxonomic groups, we apply linear and nonlinear regression probes to quantify which acoustic properties each model captures. Results confirm a ``no free lunch'' pattern: no single model captures the full feature space. A concatenated embedding achieves the highest performance, suggesting complementary acoustic space coverage across models. Loudness features are best encoded ($R^2 = 0.76$) while F0 is hardest to recover ($R^2 = 0.33$). ### [201] [When to Write and When to Suppress: Route-Specialized Dual Adapters for Memory-Assisted Knowledge Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14668)
*Yining Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于路由的双适配器编辑方法 \method{}，通过引入相关性路由器决定是否应用编辑记忆，并在不同路径上分别使用编辑适配器和局部性适配器，以实现精准编辑与无关行为保留。在三个基准测试中，\method{} 在 Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct 和 Qwen3-8B 上均取得最优性能，尤其在 \mquake{} 上达到 0.9922 的准确率。实验表明，分离编辑注入与非直接路径抑制是性能提升的关键，而非单纯增加 LoRA 容量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识编辑系统在更新特定事实时，难以同时保持与之相关的其他行为不变。如何在正确时机应用编辑、何时抑制编辑成为核心挑战。

Method: \\method{} 采用双适配器架构：一个相关性路由器判断输入提示是否应接收编辑记忆；若被路由，则使用编辑适配器增强新对象偏好；未被路由的提示则由局部性适配器维持或恢复原始偏好。

Result: 在 \\cf{}, \\zsre{}, \\mquake{} 三个 1,000 案例协议下，\\method{} 在 Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct 和 Qwen3-8B 上均表现最佳，分别达到 0.8180、0.8946 和 0.9922 的概率偏好准确率。不同数据集的最佳路由策略不同：\\cf{} 使用词法神经路由最安全，而 \\zsre{} 与 \\mquake{} 更适合使用 BGE 嵌入路由。

Conclusion: 分离编辑注入与非直接路径抑制机制是实现高效且鲁棒知识编辑的关键，路由选择需根据数据特性优化，该方法显著优于仅提升参数容量的方案。

Abstract: Knowledge editing systems must update selected facts while preserving nearby but irrelevant behavior. This paper studies this problem in a memory-assisted setting where an edit memory is retrieved at inference time and a parameter-efficient adapter corrects the model's object preference. We argue that the central design question is not only how to write an edit, but also when to suppress it. We introduce \method{}, a route-specialized dual-adapter editor. A relevance router first decides whether a prompt should receive an edit memory. Routed prompts use an edit adapter trained to prefer the new object over the original object; unrouted non-direct prompts use a separate locality adapter trained to preserve or restore the original-object preference. We evaluate \method{} on three 1,000-case protocols, \cf{}, \zsre{}, and \mquake{}, under the same memory protocol and two 7B/8B base models. On Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct, \method{} obtains the best overall probability-preference accuracy on all three benchmarks: 0.8180 on \cf{}, 0.8946 on \zsre{}, and 0.9922 on \mquake{}. The same trend holds on Qwen3-8B. Router ablations show that the relevant memory boundary differs across datasets: a lexical neural router is safest on \cf{}, while BGE embedding routing is better on \zsre{} and \mquake{}. Component and module ablations show that the gain mainly comes from separating edit injection from off-route suppression rather than from simply increasing LoRA capacity.

### [202] [Compressed Computation is (probably) not Computation in Superposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14673)
*Jai Bhagat,Sara Molas-Medina,Giorgi Giglemiani,Stefan Heimersheim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了压缩计算（CC）模型是否属于叠加态计算。尽管CC模型仅用50个神经元实现了100个ReLU函数的计算并取得优于预期的损失，但分析表明其性能提升源于输入通过噪声残差流产生的意外混合矩阵。将训练目标分解为ReLU项和混合项后发现，性能增益与混合矩阵大小正相关，且在移除该矩阵后消失。学习到的神经元方向集中于混合矩阵前50个最大特征值对应的子空间，说明混合项主导了解决方案。此外，基于混合矩阵构建的半非负矩阵分解（SNMF）基线能复现定性损失曲线并优于先前基线，但仍未达到训练模型水平。因此，研究认为CC并非合适的叠加态计算玩具模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究压缩计算（CC）模型是否代表了计算在叠加态中的实现，以评估其作为此类计算模型的有效性。

Method: 将训练目标分解为ReLU项和混合项，分析混合矩阵对性能的影响；通过特征值分析神经元方向的分布；使用半非负矩阵分解（SNMF）基线进行对比实验。

Result: 性能增益与混合矩阵强度相关，移除后消失；神经元方向集中在混合矩阵的前50个主特征值子空间；SNMF基线可复现损失趋势但未超越训练模型。

Conclusion: CC模型的性能提升主要由输入混合导致，而非真正的叠加态计算，因此不适合作为计算在叠加态中的玩具模型。

Abstract: We study whether the Compressed Computation (CC) toy model (Braun et al., 2025) is an instance of computation in superposition. The CC model appears to compute 100 ReLU functions with just 50 neurons, achieving a better loss than expected from only representing 50 ReLU functions. We show that the model mixes inputs via its noisy residual stream, corresponding to an unintended mixing matrix in the labels. Splitting the training objective into the ReLU term and the mixing term, we find that performance gains scale with the magnitude of the mixing matrix and vanish when the matrix is removed. The learned neuron directions concentrate in the subspace associated with the top 50 eigenvalues of the mixing matrix, suggesting that the mixing term governs the solution. Finally, a semi-non-negative matrix factorization (SNMF) baseline derived solely from the mixing matrix reproduces the qualitative loss profile and improves on prior baselines, though it does not match the trained model. These results suggest CC is not a suitable toy model of computation in superposition.

### [203] [Optimal Hidden-Target Learning for Online Inventory Optimization on General Convex Sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14679)
*Anthony Pineci,Yunzong Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种针对在线库存优化（OIO）的最优方法，通过维护一个隐藏目标并将其投影到当前可行的订货点集合中，实现了在任意有界凸容量集上的最优性能。该方法结合在线梯度下降，将以往对常见需求概率的逆依赖改进为逆平方根依赖，并证明了匹配的下界。此外，该原则首次实现了强凸损失下的多项式对数级后悔率和适应欧几里得路径变化的动态后悔率。分析引入了“范数对齐”原则，即以与投影相同的范数衡量隐藏目标到可行集的距离，使该距离演化为一维队列过程，从而解决状态依赖问题，并扩展到一般凸容量集。实验验证了理论的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线库存优化面临物理内存约束，即库存转移使得可行动作集依赖于历史。现有方法在单线性容量约束下表现良好，但难以推广到一般凸容量集。因此需要一种通用且最优的方法来处理复杂容量结构下的在线决策问题。

Method: 采用在线梯度下降作为基础学习器，结合隐藏目标的投影机制；引入‘范数对齐’原则，将状态变量定义为隐藏目标到可行集的距离（使用相同投影范数），使该距离演化为一维队列模型，实现路径相关的控制分析。

Result: 在一般凸容量集上，首次实现了逆平方根依赖的后悔率，优于之前的结果；证明了匹配的下界；获得了首个多项式对数级后悔率（强凸损失）和动态后悔率适应欧几里得路径变化的保证；实验结果支持理论分析。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于范数对齐和目标投影的框架是在线库存优化在任意有界凸容量集上的最优解，其核心在于将高维状态依赖转化为一维队列控制，突破了传统逐维分析的局限，具有广泛适用性和理论优势。

Abstract: Online inventory optimization (OIO) is online convex optimization with physical memory: inventory carryover makes the feasible action set depend on the past. A natural principle, used in stochastic inventory learning and recently in OIO under a single linear capacity constraint, is to maintain a hidden target chosen by an online learner and implement its projection onto the currently feasible order-up-to set. We prove that this simple principle is optimal for OIO on arbitrary bounded convex capacity sets. With online gradient descent as the base learner, the method improves the best known regret guarantee for OIO on general convex sets from inverse to inverse-square-root dependence on the common-demand probability, and we prove a matching lower bound. The same principle gives the first polylogarithmic regret guarantee for strongly convex losses and the first dynamic regret guarantee adapting to Euclidean path variation on general convex capacity sets.
  The analysis introduces a norm alignment principle: the right state variable is the distance from the hidden target to the feasible set, measured in the same norm as the projection. Under norm alignment, this distance evolves pathwise as a scalar queue, with target movement as arrival and common demand as service. This reduction to one-dimensional queue control resolves the state dependence and extends the guarantees to general convex capacity sets, beyond the reach of prior productwise approaches. Experiments on synthetic and real-world inventory data corroborate the theory.

### [204] [A Complexity Measure for Active Learning in Multi-group Mean Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14690)
*Abdellah Aznag,Rachel Cummings,Adam N. Elmachtoub*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究多组均值估计 $d$-臂老虎机中的最大风险目标，提出一种自适应分配样本预算的主动学习方法，旨在最小化最坏情况下的不确定性指标 $\max_{k\in[d]}σ_k^2/n_k$。通过构建局部极小极大框架，首次证明了适用于任意有限方差假设类的一般下界，该下界由三个正交因素构成：预算项、异方差性指数（衡量不确定性在各臂间分布的不均衡程度）以及模型相关的复杂度度量——方差局部曲率（VLC）。对于光滑类，VLC 可重参数化为方差-费舍尔信息，且对常见分布族具有闭式表达。与现有最优上界对比表明，在广泛情形下达到近似最优，仅存在对数因子差距，并揭示了在高度异方差情形下的系统性差距。证明中引入两个关键工具：基于损失的 $\ell_1$ 几何结构和基于表示的实例生成器，将困难实例构造转化为显式随机矩阵计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多组均值估计的主动学习问题中，传统方法常忽略最坏情况下的不确定性，导致某些组别估计误差过大。为提升鲁棒性，需优化最大风险目标，即最小化最坏情况下的方差归一化样本数比 $\max_{k\in[d]}σ_k^2/n_k$，从而确保所有组别的估计精度均得到保障。然而，缺乏对这一目标的理论下界分析，尤其在异方差和复杂假设类下的性能边界尚不清晰。因此，亟需建立通用的理论框架以刻画其内在挑战与最优性能极限。

Method: 提出局部极小极大框架，结合损失诱导的 $\ell_1$ 几何结构，设计基于表示的实例生成器，将难例构造转化为随机矩阵计算；通过分析假设类的局部性质，定义并量化方差局部曲率（VLC），进而推导出适用于任意有限方差假设类的通用下界。

Result: 首次建立了针对最大风险目标的通用下界，明确分离出预算、异方差性和模型复杂度（VLC）三个独立影响因素；在光滑假设类中，VLC 与方差-费舍尔信息相关，可显式计算；与现有最优上界对比显示，算法在大多数情况下接近最优，仅差对数因子；在高度异方差场景中揭示出系统性差距，指明改进方向。

Conclusion: 本研究为多组均值估计中的最大风险主动学习提供了首个统一的理论下界，揭示了性能受限于预算、异方差性及模型复杂度三方面因素。所提出的 VLC 度量为理解假设类的信息结构提供了新视角，方法论上的创新（如 $\ell_1$ 几何与实例生成器）也为后续研究提供重要工具，推动了主动学习在高维、异质环境下的理论发展。

Abstract: We study a \emph{max-risk} objective for active learning in a multi-group mean estimation $d$-armed bandits: a learner adaptively allocates a budget of $T$ samples across $d$ groups to minimize the worst-case uncertainty index $\max_{k\in[d]}σ_k^2/n_k$, where $σ_k$ is the standard deviation of the distribution of arm $d$, and $n_k$ is the number of times arm $d$ is sampled. We develop a local minimax framework and prove the first general lower bound for this objective, valid for any finite-variance hypothesis class. The bound separates difficulty into three orthogonal factors: a \emph{budget} term, a \emph{heteroscedasticity} index measuring how unevenly the uncertainty is spread across arms, and a model-dependent complexity measure, the \emph{Variance Local Curvature} ($\mathrm{VLC}$), which captures how much information a local change of variance creates inside the hypothesis class. For smooth classes, the $\mathrm{VLC}$ is a reparametrization of a variance--Fisher information, with closed-form values for common families. Benchmarking against the strongest available upper bound shows near-optimality up to logarithmic factors in broad regimes, and pinpoints a systematic gap in highly heterogeneous instances. Our proof introduces two key ingredients: a loss-induced $\ell_1$ geometry on the decision space, and a representation-based instance generator that reduces hard-instance construction to an explicit random matrix calculation.

</details>

### [205] [A Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL)-Based Transformer Method for Solving the Open Shop Scheduling Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13682)
*Faezeh Ardali,Mwembezi A. Nyelele,Gerald M. Knapp*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种基于Transformer的开放车间调度策略，采用编码器-解码器架构和多头注意力机制，在仅使用加工时间矩阵作为输入的情况下，能够在小规模实例（4×4至10×10）上生成接近最优解的可行调度方案。模型训练后直接应用于大规模随机生成实例（40×40至100×100），无需重新训练，平均性能差距为12.89%-15.12%相对于标准下界，优于传统规则如SPT、LPT，并与EST相当，表明该方法具备良好的泛化能力，可作为特征简洁的新型学习型调度策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放车间调度问题在工业和服务场景中普遍存在，但随着作业和机器数量增加，求解变得极其困难。传统精确算法难以处理大规模问题，而经典调度规则和元启发式方法需要大量调参以维持高质量解，因此亟需一种无需复杂调参、能有效扩展到大规模问题的学习型调度方法。

Method: 提出基于Transformer的编码器-解码器架构，利用多头注意力机制建模作业与机器间的依赖关系；仅以加工时间矩阵为输入进行端到端训练，通过强化学习或监督学习方式优化调度策略；训练完成后直接部署于大规模未见过的实例，评估其泛化性能。

Result: 在小规模Taillard基准实例上，所提方法生成的调度方案使完工时间（makespan）通常位于已知最优值的15%-30%以内；在大规模随机实例（40×40至100×100）上，平均相对下界差距为12.89%-15.12%，显著优于SPT和LPT，与EST相比保持竞争力，证明了模型在规模外推上的有效性。

Conclusion: 基于Transformer的调度策略能够从较小规模实例中学习并有效推广至更大规模问题，提供了一种无需复杂特征工程、参数调优少的轻量级学习型调度方案，为开放车间调度提供了新的高效替代方法。

Abstract: The open shop scheduling problem (OSSP) arises in many industrial and service settings but remains computationally challenging as the number of jobs and machines increases. While exact methods quickly become intractable, classical dispatching rules and metaheuristics may require substantial tuning to maintain solution quality at large scales. This study develops a Transformer-based scheduling policy for OSSP using an encoder-decoder architecture with multi-head attention. The model is trained on Taillard benchmark instances (4x4, 5x5, 7x7, and 10x10) using only the processing-time matrix as input and produces feasible schedules with makespans typically within 15-30% of best-known values. To evaluate scalability, the trained policy is applied without retraining to randomly generated instances from 40x40 to 100x100 and compared against classical dispatching heuristics, including SPT, LPT, MWKR, and EST. Across these large instances, the Transformer achieved average gaps of 12.89-15.12% relative to a standard lower bound. Compared with EST, the Transformer remained competitive, typically within a modest margin, while substantially outperforming SPT and LPT. These results indicate that a Transformer policy trained on small OSSP instances can generalize to substantially larger problems and provide a feature-light, learning-based alternative to classical dispatching rules.

</details>


### [206] [UP-NRPA: User Portrait based Nested Rollout Policy Adaptation for Planning with Large Language Models in Goal-oriented Dialogue Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13683)
*Hui Wang,Fafa Zhang,Meng Liu,Xiangyu Chen,Chaoxu Mu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出UP-NRPA框架，结合用户画像（性格、偏好、目标）与实时用户反馈，通过大语言模型实现在线策略自适应，无需离线训练即可动态调整对话策略。

Result: 在多个对话任务中实现100%成功率，谈判任务中销售比（SL）提升56.41%，显著优于传统方法，验证了其对多样化用户需求的高效适应能力。

Conclusion: UP-NRPA无需依赖离线训练即可实现对话策略的动态个性化，有效提升了对话系统对用户特征的适应性，具备良好的应用前景。

Abstract: To address the challenge that current dialogue policy planning methods struggle to dynamically adapt to diverse user characteristics, this paper proposes a User Portrait based Nested Rollout Policy Adaptation (UP-NRPA) online framework with Large Language Models. In contrast to conventional approaches dependent on model training and require offline reinforcement learning policy models for user groups, UP-NRPA enables dynamic customization of dialogue strategies through an adaptive mechanism. This is achieved by leveraging real-time user feedback alongside personality, preferences, and objectives mapped from the current user portrait, thereby adapting to user characteristics without offline reinforcement learning. In collaborative and non-collaborative dialogue benchmarks, UP-NRPA demonstrated considerable benefits, achieving an impressive 100% success rate in multiple dialogue tasks. Particularly in negotiation tasks, the sale-to-list ratio (SL) increased by 56.41%. This demonstrates that UP-NRPA can adapt to diverse user needs without requiring a training mechanism, enabling the dialogue system to adapt to user characteristics.

### [208] [Orchestra-o1: Omnimodal Agent Orchestration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13707)
*Fan Zhang,Vireo Zhang,Shengju Qian,Haoxuan Li,Hao Wu,Jinyang Wu,Donghao Zhou,Zhihong Zhu,Zheng Lian,Xin Wang,Pheng-Ann Heng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Orchestra-o1的多模态智能体编排框架，旨在解决现有框架在异构模态共存与交互场景下的泛化能力不足问题。该框架通过统一的编排机制实现模态感知的任务分解、在线子智能体专业化及并行子任务执行，显著提升复杂现实任务处理能力，在OmniGAIA基准上比次优方法高出10.3%准确率。同时引入决策对齐组相对策略优化（DA-GRPO）训练方法，使Orchestra-o1-8B达到开源多模态智能体的顶尖性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体编排框架局限于有限模态，难以适应包含文本、图像、音频、视频等多种输入的复杂多模态任务，尤其在异构模态协同时表现不佳，亟需一种可扩展、统一的编排机制以支持跨模态高效协作。

Method: 提出Orchestra-o1框架，采用统一编排机制实现模态感知的任务分解、在线子智能体专业化和并行子任务执行；结合决策对齐组相对策略优化（DA-GRPO）进行高效强化学习训练，提升智能体系统在多模态环境中的决策一致性与性能表现。

Result: Orchestra-o1在OmniGAIA基准上比第二佳方法提升10.3%准确率；Orchestra-o1-8B模型在所有公开可用的多模态智能体中达到最先进的性能水平。

Conclusion: Orchestra-o1成功构建了一个面向多模态任务的高效智能体协作体系，其统一编排机制与高效的训练策略为复杂现实世界任务提供了强有力的支持，标志着多模态智能体系统向规模化、通用化迈出了关键一步。

Abstract: The recent success of agent swarms has shifted the paradigm of large language model (LLM)-based agents from single-agent workflows to multi-agent systems, highlighting the importance of agent orchestration for task decomposition and collaboration. However, existing orchestration frameworks are limited to a narrow set of modalities and struggle to generalize to more complex settings where heterogeneous modalities coexist and interact. This limitation becomes particularly pronounced in omnimodal scenarios, where tasks require the unified understanding and coordination of diverse inputs such as text, image, audio, and video. In this work, we propose Orchestra-o1, an omnimodal agent orchestration framework designed to support efficient agent collaboration across multiple modalities. Orchestra-o1 introduces a unified orchestration mechanism that enables modality-aware task decomposition, online sub-agent specialization, and parallel sub-task execution. This scalable design allows agent systems to effectively tackle complex real-world tasks involving heterogeneous information sources, surpassing the second-best approach by 10.3% accuracy on the OmniGAIA benchmark. Furthermore, we introduce decision-aligned group relative policy optimization (DA-GRPO), an efficient agentic reinforcement learning approach for training Orchestra-o1-8B, which also achieves state-of-the-art performance against all existing open-source omnimodal agents.

### [209] [Hybrid Open-Ended Tri-Evolution Makes Better Deep Researcher](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13710)
*Hongming Piao,Chi Liu,Mengzhuo Chen,Yan Shu,Derek Li,Ying Wei,Bryan Dai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出HOTE框架，通过混合模式强化学习实现提议者、求解者和评判者三者的协同进化，以解决开放性研究任务中的深度研究与智能体演化难题。实验表明，8B模型在多个长文本研究基准上超越了更大的静态模型和现有训练方法，且三模块协同进化不可或缺。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI代理在开放性研究任务中面临两大挑战：深度研究受限于静态参数能力，而代理演化仅在可验证任务中有效，缺乏对开放性任务的支持。因此需要一种能够协同进化并适应开放环境的框架。

Method: 提出混合模式强化学习的HOTE框架，通过提议者、求解者和评判者三模块基于网络规模知识进行协同进化，实现自主演化的智能体系统。

Result: 在三个长格式深度研究基准上，经HOTE训练的8B模型表现优于最强的静态8-32B模型及现有先进训练方法，且训练时间更少；验证了三模块协同进化的必要性。

Conclusion: HOTE框架成功实现了开放性任务下智能体的协同演化，为迈向具备自主演化的通用人工智能提供了新路径。

Abstract: Deep research and agent evolution serve as de-facto tasks for AI agents in real-world applications toward artificial general intelligence. The former enables autonomous retrieval and integration of information in open-ended environments to tackle open-ended research tasks, yet it is constrained by the static parametric deep research capabilities of agent systems. The latter allows agents to autonomously interact with the environment to gain experiences that evolve model capabilities. However, its effectiveness has been widely validated only on verifiable tasks with standard answers, leaving a gap with open-ended research tasks. To bridge these two critical tasks, we propose the Hybrid Open-Ended Tri-Evolution (HOTE) framework, which leverages hybrid-mode reinforcement learning to facilitate the collaborative evolution of a proposer, solver and judge based on web-scale knowledge, moving toward autonomous evolving agents in open-ended tasks and environments. Extensive experiments on three long-form deep research benchmarks demonstrate that the 8B model trained via HOTE surpasses the strongest static open 8-32B models as well as those trained by state-of-the-art deep research training methods with less time overhead, and further verify that the evolution of all three modules in HOTE is indispensable.

</details>


### [210] [WorkBench Revisited: Workplace Agents Two Years On](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13715)
*Olly Styles*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 自2024年3月到2026年6月，WorkBench基准测试显示，顶级智能体从GPT-4进步至Claude Opus 4.8，任务完成率从43%提升至89%，无意有害行为从26%降至2.5%。性能与安全性同步提升，错误类型大幅减少，但基础失误仍偶发且可能造成不可逆损害。开放权重模型显著降低高绩效成本，而前沿模型成本保持稳定。研究更新了基准数据与代码，并分析了智能体进展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估智能体在真实工作场景中的能力与安全性演变，揭示性能与安全性的关系，推动高效、可靠智能体的发展。

Method: 通过对比2024年与2026年在WorkBench基准上的智能体表现，分析任务完成率与无意有害行为发生率的变化，评估不同模型（包括开源与专有）的性能与成本变化。

Result: Claude Opus 4.8在2026年实现89%的任务完成率，仅2.5%的无意有害行为；性能与安全性正相关；开放权重模型显著降低高绩效门槛，前沿模型成本稳定。

Conclusion: 智能体在任务完成率和安全性方面均取得显著进步，二者不再对立；尽管仍有微小风险，但整体趋势向好；开放模型降低了技术壁垒，推动更广泛的应用。

Abstract: The best agent on WorkBench in March 2024, GPT-4, completed 43% of tasks and took an unintended harmful action, such as emailing the wrong person, on 26% of them. We re-visit the benchmark in June 2026 and find that the best agent to date, Claude Opus 4.8, completes 89% and takes an unintended harmful action on 2.5%. Aside from this considerable progress in frontier agent performance, three things stand out. First, capability and safety go together on WorkBench rather than trade off, so the models that finish the most tasks also do the least unintended damage. Second, while several classes of error have been totally eliminated, frontier models still make some basic mistakes that occasionally result in irreversible harm, such as sending an email to the wrong person. Third, the rise of open-weight models has drastically lowered costs for a performance level that was previously only accessible to proprietary models, while frontier costs have stayed relatively stable. We release an updated version of the benchmark with data and code quality improvements, new model scores, and analysis of agent progress on WorkBench since 2024.

</details>


### [211] [Refusal Beyond a Single Direction: A Preliminary Comparison of Diff-in-Means and INLP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13720)
*Elisabetta Rocchetti,Alfio Ferrara*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究比较了基于DiM的干预方法与两种基于INLP的干预方法在控制聊天模型拒绝行为上的效果，发现INLP的反事实翻转方法在抑制拒绝方面与DiM方向删减相当，而零空间投影则较弱；限制INLP仅使用主导方向可在接近基线困惑度下保持大部分抑制效果，实现可调节的能力。几何分析显示，两种INLP方法作用于激活空间的不同区域：零空间投影将激活值压缩到有害与无害聚类之间，而反事实翻转将其移至相反聚类，暗示模型对概念缺失与对立概念的编码方式不同，这一发现值得进一步研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究INLP方法是否能与DiM方法在控制安全微调聊天模型的拒绝行为上表现相当，并评估其更丰富的参数化是否带来更具可调性的干预手段。

Method: 比较DiM（差值均值）方法与INLP（迭代零空间投影）中的两种干预策略——零空间投影和反事实翻转——在五种开源聊天模型上的效果，通过激活添加、方向删减、零空间投影和反事实翻转等操作进行实验，并分析其在拒绝抑制能力与模型困惑度之间的权衡。

Result: INLP反事实翻转在拒绝抑制方面表现与DiM方向删减相当，而零空间投影效果较弱；限制INLP仅使用主要方向时，仍能保持较强的抑制效果且困惑度接近基线，表明其具备可调节性；几何分析揭示两种干预在激活空间中作用于不同区域，提示模型对‘缺失’与‘对立’概念的表征存在本质差异。

Conclusion: INLP反事实翻转是一种有效的替代方案，可用于调控模型拒绝行为，且其几何特性揭示了模型内部对概念缺失与对立的编码机制差异，为未来研究提供了新方向。

Abstract: Arditi et al. (2024) has shown that refusal in safety fine-tuned chat models is mediated by a single linear direction in the residual stream, recoverable by a difference-in-means (DiM) of harmful and harmless activations. We compare DiM-based interventions (activation addition and directional ablation) with two interventions derived from Iterative Nullspace Projection (INLP) -- nullspace projection and counterfactual flipping -- on five open-weight chat models, asking whether INLP can match DiM at steering refusal and whether its richer parameterisation yields more tweakable interventions. INLP counterfactual flipping is competitive with DiM directional ablation on refusal suppression, while nullspace projection is consistently weaker. Restricting INLP to the leading directions of the extracted subspace preserves most of the suppression effect at near-baseline perplexity, giving a tunable capability. Geometrically, the two INLP interventions land in qualitatively different regions of activation space: nullspace projection collapses transformed activations \emph{between} the harmful and harmless clusters, while counterfactual flipping moves them into the opposite cluster, suggesting that the model encodes the absence of a concept differently from its opposite -- an intriguing distinction that warrants further investigation in future work.

</details>


### [212] [YeasierAgent: Agentic Social Sandbox as a Canvas for Intent-Driven Creation of Platform-Agnostic Symbiotic Agent-Native Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13722)
*Jory He*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统软件开发模式依赖设备耦合和固定图形布局，限制了应用的灵活性与社交性；现有智能代理多为孤立工具，缺乏情感陪伴与协同能力。本文旨在突破这些局限，构建更自然、可扩展且具有社会嵌入性的应用生态。

Method: 采用共生代理架构，引入叙事世界与场景感知交互机制，利用平台无关的交互单元（代理、场景、对话）进行系统设计，结合自动化生成、用户创建的世界以及空间多代理协作，构建统一的体验沙箱。

Result: 成功实现了跨平台、快速构建的代理原生应用，显著提升了应用的可扩展性与用户体验；验证了情感陪伴与工具执行在单一环境中协同的可能性，正式定义了‘共生代理原生应用’这一新类别。

Conclusion: YeaierAgent标志着从孤立工具型聊天机器人向融合社会性与功能性计算环境的重要转变，为未来人机协作提供了新的范式。

Abstract: This paper introduces YeasierAgent, an application-building paradigm based on symbiotic agents, narrative worlds, and scene-aware interaction. It challenges the conventional device-coupled model of software by redefining applications as collaborative spaces among users, agents, and worlds. We present a system architecture that achieves two primary contributions: (1) enabling the rapid, cross-platform construction of agent-native applications by utilizing platform-agnostic interactive units (agents, scenes, dialogue) rather than fixed graphical layouts; and (2) unifying the emotional companionship and practical tool execution attributes of intelligent agents within a single experiential sandbox. ### [214] [When Sample Selection Bias Precipitates Model Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.13732)
*Xinbao Qiao,Xianglong Du,Wei Liu,Jingqi Zhang,Peihua Mai,Meng Zhang,Yan Pang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 递归训练合成数据可缓解数据稀缺，但可能导致模型坍塌（model collapse），即分布尾部信息丢失、输出同质化。现有数据选择方法依赖参考分布，但在低资源环境下（如医疗或金融数据孤岛），本地参考分布不完整且有偏差，导致选择过程本身产生偏差，反而优先保留局部模式而剔除全局重要尾部样本，加速模型坍塌。理论证明此类孤岛式选择会加剧坍塌并引发幂律多样性衰减。提出一种基于Wasserstein距离的协作代理参考，可在不共享原始数据的前提下整合多个孤岛信息。实验表明，使用本地参考的选择在偏斜分布下失效，而协作代理参考能有效缓解多样性退化，提示在真实数据覆盖不足时需谨慎设计递归合成数据流程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决递归训练合成数据中因数据选择依赖局部参考分布而导致的模型坍塌问题，特别是在数据孤岛场景下真实数据覆盖不全时，传统选择策略可能适得其反。

Method: 构建基于Wasserstein距离的跨孤岛代理参考分布，通过聚合多个数据孤岛的统计特征生成无原始数据共享的参考分布；结合理论分析与实证验证，评估不同选择策略对多样性保持的影响。

Result: 本地参考下的数据选择在偏斜分布上显著降低多样性，加速模型坍塌；而协作代理参考能有效缓解多样性退化，提升合成数据的分布覆盖性。

Conclusion: 在数据孤岛和低资源条件下，依赖本地参考的数据选择会加剧模型坍塌；必须采用协作式代理参考机制以保障合成数据管道的多样性与鲁棒性，尤其在真实数据覆盖不全时需格外谨慎。

Abstract: The proliferation of recursive training on synthetic data can alleviate data scarcity but risks model collapse, where repeated training erodes distributional tails and homogenizes outputs. Data selection is widely viewed as a remedy, yet its reliability depends critically on the reference distribution used by the verifier. We show that in low-resource verification regimes, where each verifier observes only a small, fragmented, and biased slice of the target manifold, selection itself becomes biased. This situation naturally arises in low-resource data silos such as healthcare consortia or proprietary financial institutions, where raw data cannot be pooled and local references are inherently incomplete. As a result, selection preferentially retains samples aligned with the local manifold while pruning globally relevant tail modes, turning from a safeguard against collapse into a mechanism that precipitates it. We theoretically prove that such siloed selection accelerates collapse and induces power-law diversity decay. As an initial mitigation, we construct Wasserstein proxy references from multiple silos without sharing raw data. Empirical results confirm that local-reference selection fails on skewed distributions, whereas collaborative proxy references mitigate diversity degradation, suggesting that recursive synthetic-data pipelines require particular caution when real-data coverage is fragmented or scarce.
